发展性语言障碍

GPT-Academic Report

# Title:

Grammatical analysis of developmental language disorders: a study of the morphosyntax of children with specific language disorders, with hearing impairment and with Down’s syndrome

# Abstract:

Using a Dutch adaptation of the L A R S P procedure by Crystal, Fletcher and Garman (1976) this investigation aimed at two questions: ( I ) is it possible to discern patterns in the morphosyntax of three groups of language-disordered children: children with specific language disordcrs, children with hearing impairment and children with Down’s syndrome? and (2) can thcsc patterns be related to the clinical characteristics of the children? Analysis of samples of spontaneous speech produced an affirmative answer to the first question. The aqswer to the second question is that the different clinical characteristics of the children did not so much lead to differcnt kinds of languagc disorders as to differences in the degree of being language-disordered. The three groups of children showed more commonalities than differences in producing morphosyntax.

# Meta Translation

当然，以下是该论文的题目和摘要的中文翻译：

题目：
发展性语言障碍的语法分析：对特定语言障碍儿童、听觉障碍儿童和唐氏综合症儿童的形态句法研究

摘要：
本研究使用了Crystal、Fletcher和Garman（1976年）提出的LARSProcedure的一个荷兰版本，旨在探讨两个问题：
(1) 是否可以在三组语言障碍儿童（特定语言障碍儿童、听觉障碍儿童以及唐氏综合症儿童）中识别出形态句法上的模式？
(2) 是否可以将这些模式与儿童的临床特征联系起来？
通过对自发言语样本的分析，我们对第一个问题的回答是肯定的。而第二个问题的答案是：不同儿童的临床特征并没有导致不同的语言障碍类型，而是导致了语言障碍程度的不同。三个儿童群体在产生形态句法时表现出更多的共性而非差异。

# Introduction

When communicating with language-disordered children, the language production of, for instance, a hearing-impaired child may at first sound quite different from that of a child with Down’s syndrome. But over ten years ago, Bloom and Lahey (1978) pointed out the commonalities in language behaviour among children with different aetiologies. They added, however, that there have been contradictory reports in the literature concerning the question of whether a clinical syndrome, such as hearing impairment or mental retardation, can be associated with a particular language behaviour. Therefore more information is needed to be able to judge whether (or not) distinct language pathologies might be associated with different aetiologies.
Address correspondence to: Dr. F. Kuiken, Borgerstraat 3-B, 1053 PA Amsterdam, The Netherlands.

在与语言障碍儿童沟通时，例如听障儿童的语言产出最初可能会听起来与其他患有唐氏综合征的儿童有很大不同。然而，十多年来，Bloom和Lahey（1978）指出了不同病因的儿童在语言行为上存在的共同点。不过，他们也补充道，关于临床综合征（如听力受损或智力发育迟缓）是否与特定语言行为相关联的问题，在文献中存在相互矛盾的报告。因此，需要更多的信息才能判断是否存在不同的病因可能与特定的语言病理学相关联。

请将所有信件寄至：F. Kuiken博士，荷兰阿姆斯特丹市Borgerstraat街3号-B，邮政编码1053 PA。

# Gerurd Bol and Folkert Kuiken

We took up this question in the study to be reported and investigated whether it is possible to discern patterns in the morphosyntax of three groups of languagedisordered children: children with specific language disorders, hearing-impaired children and children with Down’s syndrome. By a pattern we mean a series of characteristics in the morphosyntax of a group of language-disordered children in which they differ from normal children. The second question we examined was: where such patterns can be discerned, can they be distinguished from one another in such a way as to show a correlation with the clinical characteristics of the children?
In order to answer the research questions, a model to assess the morphosyntactic level of language disordered children is required. Such a model should be based on normal langauge development. With reference to Dutch, the study of normal language development has been rather fragmentary. For that reason we started our study by developing a model for diagnosing and evaluating language disorders in Dutch children. This model was based on the LARSP profile chart developed by Crystal, Fletcher and Garman (1976).
In the next paragraphs we will present our research design, the subjects involved in the study and the method used. The Dutch profile chart will be discussed briefly. Then the results will be presented, followed by the conclusions of this study.

我们在这项研究中探讨了这一问题，并调查了是否有可能在三个语言障碍儿童群体的形态句法结构中辨别出模式：包括有特定语言障碍的儿童、听力受损儿童以及唐氏综合症儿童。这里的“模式”指的是在这些语言障碍儿童的语言形态句法中与其正常儿童有所差异的一系列特征。第二个探讨的问题是：如果能在这些模式中辨别出来，那么能否通过这些模式来显示与这些儿童的临床特征之间的关联？

为了回答这些研究问题，需要一个可以评估语言障碍儿童形态句法水平的模型。这个模型应当基于正常的语言发展。相对于荷兰语而言，有关正常语言发展的研究相对零散。因此，我们的研究从开发一个用于诊断和评估荷兰儿童语言障碍的模型开始。该模型是基于Crystal、Fletcher和Garman（1976年）开发的LARSP轮廓图表。

在接下来的部分中，我们将介绍我们的研究设计、参与的研究对象以及使用的方法。荷兰的轮廓图将会简要讨论。然后会展示结果，最后得出本研究的结论。

# Methods and subjects

In the construction of a profile chart reflecting the morphosyntactic development of Dutch children, our focus was on the age span between one and four years. This period was divided into six stages of six months. At each stage, spontaneous language samples were obtained from twelve children equally divided as to sex and social class (Fig. I).
The children were selected from playgroups and day-care centres in Amsterdam. The children were audiorecorded for one hour in everyday situations at their homes in the presence of at least one of the parents and two observers. After the transcription of the recordings 100 successive utterances from the eleventh minute of the recording onwards were used for the morphosyntactic analysis. Our notion of utterance was based on the 7’-unit as defined by Hunt (1970). All utterances were analyzed at clause, phrase and morphology level. The morphosyntactic framework we used was based on descriptive Dutch grammars (Gerts, Haeseryn, de Rood and van den Toorn 1984, Klooster, Verkuyl and Luif 1974, Pollmann and Sturm 1980, Van den Toorn 1979). In order to determine what morphosyntactic structures should be included in the profile chart at a certain stage, we applied two criteria. In the first place the structure should be used by at least 50% of the population at a particular stage. This criterion, adopted from Wells (l985), takes into account the requirement that the structure be used by the majority of the children. In the second place we applied a criterion of frequency: the median of the frequency with which a structure is used should have a value of at least 1.0. The application of these criteria has yielded the profile chart which will be discussed in the next section.
The speech of the three language-disordered groups was recorded at their schools, while the children were playing with their speech therapist. From each child 100 utterances were obtained for analysis according to the same morphosyntactic framework used for the normal children. According to the speech therapists, the language production level of the selected children did not go beyond that of normal four-year-olds. A further requirement was that their chronological age should be at least 3;6 years. This made it possible to compare the language disordered children with the normal children of stage VI from 3;6 to 4;O years. Nonparametric statistics were used for the comparison. The Kruskal-Wallis analysis of variance was applied to determine differences between the four groups (normal and language-disordered) and the Mann-Whitney U-test was used to determine differences between the normal children on the one hand and each language-disordered group on the other. The children with specific language disorders all lacked sufficient intellectual or physiological impairment to account for their difficulties in language acquisition. The children ranged from 4;8 to 8;2 years of age; with an average age of 5 ; l l years. All 18 children (14 boys and 4 girls) attended a school in Amsterdam for children with specific language disorders.
The hearing impaired children (1 1 boys and eight girls) suffered from sensorineural or mixed hearing loss. Their hearing impairment had been diagnosed before they were 1;6 years of age. Their hearing loss differed from 40 to 85 dB pure tone average on the better ear. The average hearing loss was 65.8 dB. They differed in age from 3;lO to 9; 1 years, with an average age of 5; 1 1 years. The children were of normal intelligence.
The mentally retarded children (seven boys and 1 1 girls) had all been diagnosed as suffering from trisomy 2 1 -Down’s syndrome. Their chronological age ranged from 8;4 to 18;ll years, with an average age of 14;4 years. Their intelligence level determined with a Dutch adaptation of the Merrill-Palmer Preschool Performance Tests, differed from 20 to 56, with an average IQ of 40.7. Their mental age was at least 3;6 years. All but one lived with their parents.

方法和研究对象

在构建反映荷兰儿童形态句法发展的图谱时，我们的研究重点放在1岁到4岁的年龄段。这一时期被划分为六个半年阶段。每个阶段，研究人员从12名儿童中获得了自发的语言样本，这12名儿童男女各半且社会经济背景相同（图1）。

这些儿童是从阿姆斯特丹的玩耍小组和日托中心中挑选出来的。儿童在一个小时以内的日常情况下，在其中一名家长及两名观察者的陪同下，在家中进行了声音录制。在录音转录后，从第11分钟开始选取100个连续发言句进行形态句法分析。我们关于发言句的概念是基于Hunt（1970年）的定义，即T’单位。所有发言句都在分句、短语和形态层面进行了分析。我们使用的形态句法框架基于描述性的荷兰语法书籍（Gerts, Haeseryn, de Rood和van den Toorn 1984；Klooster, Verkuyl和Luif 1974；Pollmann和Sturm 1980；Van den Toorn 1979）。为了确定某个特定阶段应纳入图谱的形态句法结构，我们应用了两个标准。首先，该结构应在特定阶段至少被50%的人群使用。这一标准来源于Wells（1985年），旨在确保结构为多数儿童所用。其次，我们还设定了频率标准：某结构被使用的频率中值应至少达到1.0。应用这两个标准得出了本节将要讨论的图谱。

这三个语言障碍组儿童的言语是在学校里录制的，此时他们正在与言语治疗师玩耍。每名儿童都提供了符合正常儿童同样形态句法框架的100句话用于分析。据言语治疗师介绍，这些受试儿童的语言产出水平未超过四岁普通儿童的水平。另外，他们还需要满足的另一个条件是其实际年龄至少为3岁6个月，以便于与3岁6个月至4岁期间的正常儿童第六阶段进行比较。采用非参数统计方法进行了比较分析，使用了Kruskal-Wallis方差分析来确定四个组（正常儿童和语言障碍组儿童）之间的差异，以及曼-惠特尼U检验来评估正常儿童与各语言障碍组之间的差异。

具有特定语言障碍的儿童在智力或生理方面没有不足以解释他们语言习得困难的症状。这些儿童的实际年龄范围为4岁8个月至8岁2个月，平均年龄为5岁11个月。所有18名儿童（其中包括14名男孩和4名女孩）都就读于阿姆斯特丹专门为具有特定语言障碍儿童设立的学校。

听力受损的儿童（11名男孩和8名女孩）存在感觉神经性或混合性听力损失。他们在1岁6个月之前已经被诊断出听力问题。他们的较好耳朵的纯音测定阈值听力损失范围为40到85dB不等，平均听力损失值为65.8dB。他们的实际年龄范围从3岁10个月到9岁1个月，平均年龄为5岁11个月。这些儿童智力正常。

智力迟钝的儿童（7名男孩和11名女孩）全部被诊断为患有21三体综合征（唐氏综合症）。他们的实际年龄范围从8岁4个月到18岁11个月，平均年龄为14岁4个月。根据梅里尔-帕尔默学龄前表现测试的荷兰适应版本评定，他们的智力水平范围为20至56，平均智商为40.7。他们的心理年龄至少为3岁6个月。除了一个孩子外，其他孩子都与父母同住。

# The profile chart Part-1

The upper part of the profile chart (Fig. 2) is reserved for general information on the child. The utterances which can not be analyzed morphosyntactically are noted in section A. Some quantitative measures of the child’s language production, like MLU and MLUL, are marked down in section B.
Stage I, which covers the period from l;O to 1;6 years, is the stage of the one element utterances. We distinguish three kinds of utterances here: the ones with a nominal character (Noun), indicating objects, the ones with a verbal character (Verb), indicating actions and events, and a category-Other-used to indicate properties and function words, et cetera.
In the second stage, from 1;6 to 2;O years, children have learned how to combine words, both at clause and phrase level. Children of this age in particular combine subjects, verbs and adverbial adjuncts to the clause structures SA, SV and AV. It is noteworthy that children at this stage already use utterances containing three or even four elements, although these utterances did not meet the criteria mentioned above to be included in the profile chart. At phrase level demonstrative and personal pronouns are used, besides combinations of a determiner with a noun. At word level the diminutive appears, as well as the second and third person singular forms of the verb in the present tense.

图谱分析（Part-1）

图2的上半部分用于记录有关儿童的一般信息。无法进行形态句法分析的话语在A部分记录。关于儿童语言产出的一些定量测量指标（如MLU和MLUL）在B部分记录下来。

第一阶段覆盖了从1岁0个月到1岁6个月的时间段，这一阶段是单元素话语的阶段。我们将这些话语分为三类：具有名词特征的（名词），用于表示物体；具有动词特征的（动词），表示动作和事件；另一类别为“其他”，用于表明属性和功能词等。

第二阶段是1岁6个月至2岁期间，在这一时期，儿童学会了如何组合词语，这既包括句子层面也包括短语层面。特别地，在这个年龄段，儿童学习将主语、动词和状语补语结合，形成SA（主语+形容词）、SV（主语+动词）和AV（副词+动词）等结构。值得注意的是，这个阶段的儿童已经会使用含有三个甚至四个元素的话语，尽管它们不符合上面提到的标准而未包含在图谱中。在短语层面上，除了限定词与名词的结合外，指示代词和个人代词也被使用。在单词层面上，出现了缩略形式（小品词）以及现在时态下的第三人称单数和第二人称单数动词形式。

# The profile chart Part-2

At Stage 111, from 2;O to 2;6 years, four clause structures consisting of two constituents appear: structures with an object (OV), e.g. gooien steen (‘throw stone’); structures with a complement (SC) which is in most cases the nominal part of the predicate, e.g. hond lief( ‘dog sweet’); structures consisting of two adverbial adjuncts (AA), like daar ook (‘there too’) and imperatives (Imper) of the type VX, in which V denotes the verb and X any other clause element, like kom hier (‘come here’). At this stage some three-element utterances (SVA, SAA, OAV, SVC and SVO) and twc fourelement utterances (SVAA and SVAO) become productive as well. At this stage these clause structures are mostly rather elementary, that is to say, they consist of single words. In the category of interrogatives (Inter), questions of the type VSX appear. At phrase level the use of prepositions can be noted. Constructions consisting of a preposition, a determiner and a noun, e.g. naar de tuin (‘to the garden’) become productive at the same time as those without a determiner, like naar bed (‘to bed’). The use of copulas is linked with the use of a complement at the clause level at this stage, as in hond is lief (‘dog is sweet’), resulting in an SVC structure at clause level. Auxiliaries can be found as well. Sometimes these are used in combination with past participles, which are registered at word level at this stage. Adjectives are used in combination with a noun. At word level the inflection of the adjective in Dutch (adjective-e) is scored. Other morphemes becoming productive are the plural form of nouns and the first person singular of the verb in the present tense.

在第III阶段，从2岁0个月到2岁6个月，出现四种由两个成分构成的句子结构：带宾语（OV）的结构，如“gooien steen”（扔石头）；带补语（SC）的结构，补语通常是谓语的部分名词，如“hond lief”（狗可爱）；由两个状语附加语（AA）组成的结构，像“daar ook”（在那里也）；以及命令句（Imp），类型为VX，其中V表示动词，X表示任何其他类型的句子成分，如“kom hier”（过来）。在这个阶段，一些三个成分的句子（SVA、SAA、OAV、SVC和SVO）以及两个四个成分的句子（SVAA和SVAO）也开始变得活跃起来。此阶段这些句子结构大多相对简单，也就是说，它们通常仅由单个单词组成。在疑问句（Inter）类别中，出现VSX型的问题。在短语层面，可以看到介词的使用。同时产出的构成包括一个介词、限定词和名词的组合，如“naar de tuin”（去花园），以及没有限定词的组合，如“naar bed”（去床边）。在这个阶段，系动词的使用与句子层次上的补语使用相关联，如“hond is lief”（狗是可爱的），从而形成Svc结构。还可以发现助动词，有时这些助动词会与过去分词结合使用，这些过去分词在此阶段在词法级别上被记录下来。形容词通常与名词一起使用。在词法层面，荷兰语中的形容词屈折变化（形容词-e）也被评分。其他正在变得活跃的词素包括名词的复数形式和现在时态的第一人称单数形式。

# The profile chart Part-3

At stage IV, from 2;6 to 3;O years, we see that the children produce the coordinating conjunction en (and). The two element utterances VC and OA and the three element utterance AAV meet the criteria set above. Given the use of SVAA at stage 111, one wonders why AAV meets the criteria only now. When we take a closer look at these structures, we discover that SVAA structures are of a more elementary character than AAV structures, which are more developed at phrase level At this stage we can also see utterances with four elements of the type SVAC, e.g. ik ben ook ziek (‘I am ill too’), and utterances which contain more than four elements, indicated by 4 + . Finally, at clause level, children are using wh-questions in utterances with two other clause elements, indicated by QXY. The interrogative pronouns which are used in these questions appear at phrase level in this stage. Possessive pronouns are used in combination with a noun. At this level we also see that the children produce post-modifications, e.g. de poes met witte pootjes (‘the cat with white feet’), in which met witte pootjes is analyzed as post-modification. Children start using phrase structures containing a preposition and a personal pronoun as well. The form of the pronoun in these constructions is the object form, which becomes productive later than the subject form at stage 11. Finally noun phrases consisting of a determiner, an adjective and a noun are used, as well as constructions consisting of two adverbs, like heel snel (‘very quickly’). At word level we see that children between 2;6 and 3;O years of age produce past tense forms.
At stage V at clause level children between 3;O and 3;6 years no longer coordinate utterances with And (Stage VI) only, but they also use other coordinating conjunctions, such as maar (‘but’), of (‘or’) and want (‘for’). Subordinating conjunctions appear as well, e.g. omdat (‘because’). We also see the use of question words, now with three other clause elements, indicated by QXYZ. At phrase level indefinite pronouns become productive, as well as structures in which the adjective is modified by an adverb, e.g. heel groot (‘very big’).
At stage VI, between 3;6 and 4;O years, children produce questions with inversion of verb and subject that contain four clause elements in total, indicated by VSXY. At phrase level we see that the category possessive pronoun plus noun from stage IV is now preceded by a preposition. Finally, at phrase level structures with er become productive. In Dutch there are two kinds of er to be noted here: one with a partitive meaning, as in ik heb er twee (‘I have got two of them’) and the repletive er which introduces an indefinite subject, as in er zit een pocs in de tuin (‘there is a cat in the garden’ ).
Structures which did not meet the criteria to be included in one of the stages are noted in the categories Other/other at the bottom of the profile chart.

在第四阶段（IV），从2岁6个月到3岁0个月，我们可以观察到儿童开始使用协调连词“en”（和）。双元素语句VC和OA，以及三元素语句AAV符合上述设定的标准。考虑到在第三阶段（III）中已经存在SVAA结构的使用，我们不禁疑惑为什么AAV直到此时才符合标准。当我们更仔细地分析这些结构时，发现SVAA结构比AAV结构更为基础，而后者在短语层面更为成熟。同时，在这个阶段我们还可以看到四元素类型 SVAC 的语句，比如“ik ben ook ziek”（我病了），以及包含四个以上元素的语句，这里用 4+ 标示。最后，在从句层面，儿童使用含有其他两个从句成分的特殊疑问句，用 QXY 表示。这些问题中的疑问代词在这个阶段出现在短语层面。同时，他们在名词前开始使用表所有格的代词。在这个层面上，我们还观察到儿童开始使用后置修饰语，例如“de poes met witte pootjes”（白脚的猫），这里的“met witte pootjes”被解释为后置修饰语。他们开始使用带有介词和人称代词的短语结构，这些结构中的代词形式是宾格形式，这种形式在第十一阶段之前的主格形式更早变得活跃。此外，确定词、形容词和名词组成的名词短语也被使用，还有由两个副词组成的句子，例如“heel snel”（非常快）。在词汇层面，年龄在2岁6个月至3岁0个月之间的儿童开始使用过去时态形式。
在第五阶段（V），在从句层面，3岁0个月至3岁6个月的儿童不再仅通过使用“En”（而且）来协调语句（第六阶段，VI），还使用其他并列连词，如“maar”（但是）、“of”（或者）、“want”（因为）。子句连词也开始出现，例如“omdat”（因为）。我们还看到疑问词与三个其他从句元素的组合使用，用QXYZ表示。在短语层面，不定代词开始变得普遍，以及形容词被副词修饰的结构，例如“heel groot”（非常大）。
在第六阶段（VI），3岁6个月至4岁0个月的儿童开始生产总共有四个从句元素的倒装动词与主语的疑问句，这用VSXY表示。在短语层面可以看到，来自第四阶段的所属代词加名词现在前面加上了一个介词。最后，在短语层面，包含“er”的结构变得常见。荷兰语中有两种需要在这里注意的“er”：一种具有分部含义，“ik heb er twee”（我有两个），另一种具有补足含义，引入一个不明确的主题，如“er zit een kat in de tuin”（花园里有一只猫）。
未满足进入任何阶段标准的结构记录在表格底部的“Other/其他”类别中。

# Results and discussion

In order to examine the possibility of patterns in the morphosyntax of the three groups of language-disordered children mentioned, we had to give a definition of what we would regard as a pattern. We defined a pattern as a set of statistically significant differences in the frequencies of the use of morphosyntactic structures between normal children and language-disordered ones. After applying the Kruskall-Wallis analysis it turned out that 28 of the 63 variables on the profile chart showed a significant difference (p < 005). Further analysis with the Mann-Whitney U-test were therefore performed in order to find out if any group differences exist (p < 0.05). The results of the Mann-Whitney U-tests on the normal children on the one hand and each language-disordered group on the other are represented in Table 1. This table shows in which morphosyntactic categories significant differences were found between two groups. In discussing the results we will not consider the variables from the upper part of the profile chart, with the exception of MLU and MLUL. In total 56 morphosyntactic variables were scored. The children with specific language disorders (SL) differ on 16 items from the normal children (NC). The hearing-impaired children (HI) differ on 22 items from the normal children. But most differences are found between the children with Down’s syndrome (DS) and the normal children: they differ on 28 items. In view of this large number of differences our first research question ‘Is it possible to discern patterns in the language production of three groups of languagedisordered children?’ can be answered affirmatively.
We need a method for characterizing patterns, in order to be able to recognize distinct profiles. We will do this by referring again to Table 1. In this table the sign > Table 1. Results of the Mann-Whitney U tests: variables in which the normal and languagedisordered children direr significantly ( p < 0 0 5 ) .

为了检验这三个语言障碍儿童组在形态句法方面的模式可能性，我们需要给“模式”下个定义。我们将“模式”定义为正常儿童与语言障碍儿童之间在形态句法结构使用频率上的统计显著性差异的集合。经过Kruskall-Wallis分析后，发现轮廓图中的63个变量中有28个显示出了显著差异（P<0.05）。因此，我们进一步利用Mann-Whitney U检验来确定是否存在任何群体差异（P<0.05）。表1展示了Mann-Whitney U检验的结果，分别针对正常儿童和每一群语言障碍儿童。此表显示了两个群体之间在哪些形态句法类别中存在显著差异。在讨论结果时，除了平均长度单位（MLU）和标准化平均长度单位（MLUL）来自轮廓图的上半部分外，其余变量将不予考虑。总共对56个形态句法变量进行了评分。具体的：

  • 具有特定语言障碍（SL）的儿童，在16个项目上与正常儿童（NC）有显著差异。
  • 听力受损的儿童（HI），在22个项目上与正常儿童有显著差异。
  • 最多差异出现在唐氏综合症（DS）儿童与正常儿童之间：在28个项目上有显著差异。

鉴于这种显著的数量差异，我们的第一个研究问题“是否能区分三个语言障碍儿童群体的语言生产中的模式”可以得到肯定的回答。

为了能够识别出不同的特征，我们需要一种方法来表征这些模式，并通过参考表1来实现这一点。在表1中，“>”符号代表了正常儿童与语言障碍儿童间存在显著差异的变量（P<0.05）。

特别语言障碍儿童的句法结构：

在这些儿童的句子层面，某些结构的使用频率比普通儿童更高：AV（主谓倒装）、OV（动宾倒装）和SC（简单句）。同时，其他一些结构的使用频率较低：SA（陈述句形式）、VSX、SVAO（复合成分句）、4+（四个以上组成部分的句子）和并列结构。
在短语层面的显著发现是，这些儿童在代词系统上似乎存在问题。含有个人代词或所有格代词的短语结构使用得比普通儿童少。

# NC-SL NC-HI Part-2

They also show fewer instances of the variables determiner + noun and the repletive and partitive ‘er’. With regard to morphology these children use few diminutives and agreement of first person singular.
As for the children with hearing impairment, their MLU and MLUL scores are lower than those of the normal children. At clause level a tendency similar to that of children with specific language disorders can be noticed: some utterances containing a subject are used less than in the case of normal children: VSX, SVAO, SVAC, 4 + , VSXY; likcwisc Coordinations are underused. The variablcs Noun, Verb and OV, on the contrary, are overused. At phrase lcvcl these children also seem to have problems with the use of pcrsonal and possessive pronouns. In addition to this, they showed fcwer instances of copulas and auxiliaries, which is not surprising, considering thc frequently reported findings on underuse of function words by these children (e.g. Hrannon 1968, Ramford andMentz 1979). The categories determiner + noun and repletive and partitive ‘er’ are also underused. At morphology level we find problems with verb agreement and with the use of the past tense.

他们还表现出较少使用限定词+名词和补语及部分“er”的情况。在形态学方面，这些儿童很少使用缩略形式和第一人称单数的同意形式。

对于听力受损的儿童，他们的MLU（平均长度单位）和MLUL（不含连词的平均长度单位）得分低于正常儿童。在子句层面可以注意到一种类似于特定语言障碍儿童的趋势：含有主语的一些句子的使用频率低于正常儿童；较少使用VSX（动-主-动）、SVAO（主-动-宾-其他元素）、SVAC（主-动-形容词-补语）及以上的结构、VSXY（更复杂的动-主-其他元素）结构，协调（Coordinations）也使用不足。相反，名词、动词以及OV（宾-动）结构却过度使用。在短语层面，这些儿童在使用人称代词和个人所有格代词时似乎也有困难。此外，他们表现出较少的系动词和助动词实例，这并不令人意外，考虑到先前已报道过的这些儿童功能词使用不足的情况（例如，Harmon 1968，Ramford和Mentz 1979）。限定词+名词和补语及部分“er”使用不足的问题同样存在。在形态学层面上，他们表现出与动词一致性和过去时态使用有关的问题。

以上即为NC-SL 和 NC-HI Part-2的翻译内容。如果有任何进一步的要求或需要具体某些部分的详细解释，请告知我。

# NC-SL NC-HI Part-3

In the group of children with Down’s syndrome the tendency to use many structurcs in which the subject is deleted and to use few subject predicate structures is even greater than in the other two groups. We notice an overuse of Noun, Verb, OV, VC and AAV and an underuse of VSX, SVAA, SVAO, SVAC, 4 + , Coordination and VSXY. Their M L U and M L U L scores are lower than those of the normal children. Besides problems with personal and possessive pronouns, which we also encountered at phrase level in the other two groups, children with Down’s syndrome have poor control over demonstrative and interrogative pronouns. Again, determiner + noun and replctive and partitive ‘er’ are underused. These children too use fewer auxiliary verbs. At the morphological level as well, these children differ more from the normal children than do the other two groups. The problems experienced here concern verb agreement, declension of nouns and adjectives and the use of the past tense.
If we compare these patterns (Table 2 ) we find in part 2.1 that there are no less than 1 1 structures in which the three groups differ from the normal children. Up to this point the patterns of the three language-impaired groups coincide with each other. But therc are also structures in which two of the three language-disordered groups diKer from the normal children, as in part 2.2.
In part 2.3 we have structures in which only one group of language-disordered children differs from the normal children. But at the point, where the patterns of the three groups seem to diverge, some differences can be related to general tendencies noticed in all three language-disordered groups. The first two tendencies regard the use of subject predicate structures. Utterances consisting of more than three constituents containing a subject, like SVAO or SVAC, are used less frequently by the language-disordered children, whereas utterances with no more than three constituents and, in general, not containing a subject, like OV or AAV, are used more often by the language-disordered than by the normal children. The third tendency concerns problems with the pronominal system. A fourth tendency may be problems with verb conjugation. So if we try to distinguish between these patterns, it seems that the differences between our patterns are mostly of a gradual nature. In all children we found conjugation problems, problems with the pronominal system and with subject predicate structures. But the degree to which different language-disordered groups manifest these tendencies varies from one group to another.

在唐氏综合症儿童组中，省略主语并使用较少的主谓结构的趋势甚至比其他两组更为明显。我们注意到他们过度使用名词、动词、OV（宾语-动词）、VC（动词-补语）和AAV（副动词-动词）结构，而很少使用VSX（动词-短语）、SVAA（主语-形容词-形容词）、SVAO（主语-形容词-宾语）、SVAC（主语-形容词-补语）以及四元及以上复合结构和连词结构VSXY。他们的MLU（平均长度单位）和MLUL（语言长度单位）得分低于正常儿童。除了一般其他两组也遇到的人称和所有格代词问题外，唐氏综合症儿童对指示代词和疑问代词的控制较差。同样，限定词加名词以及替换性和部分性“er”用法也较少。这些儿童使用辅助动词的数量也较少。在形态学层面，这些儿童与正常儿童之间的差异比另外两组更大。他们在这里所面临的问题包括动词一致性、名词和形容词变格以及过去时态的应用。

如果我们比较这些模式（表2），发现在第二部分1中，存在11种结构，其中三个语言障碍组与正常儿童有所不同。到目前为止，这三组语言障碍儿童在模式上是一致的。但在第二部分2中也有一些结构，其中两个语言障碍组与正常儿童不同。

在第二部分3中，有一些结构仅一组语言障碍儿童不同于正常儿童。然而，在这些模式看起来开始出现分歧的地方，一些差异可以与在所有三组语言障碍儿童中观察到的一般趋势联系起来。前两个趋势涉及主谓结构的使用。由超过三个成分组成且含主语的语句，如SVAO或SVAC，语言障碍儿童使用得较少；而由不超过三个成分组成的，且一般不含主语的语句，如OV或AAV，语言障碍儿童使用得比正常儿童更多。第三个趋势涉及代词系统的应用难题。第四个趋势可能是动词变位的问题。因此，如果我们尝试区分这些模式，似乎这些模式之间的差异主要是渐变性质的。在所有儿童中，我们发现了变位问题、代词系统问题以及主谓结构问题。但不同语言障碍组在展现这些倾向的程度上各有不同。

# Conclusions

The general language level of each group turned out to be far below that of the normal children from 3;6 to 4;O years of age. The morphosyntax of the languagedisordered groups differed considerably from that of the normal children. All

各组的一般语言水平明显低于3岁6个月到4岁正常儿童的水平。语言障碍组的形态句法与正常儿童的形态句法存在显著差异。所有语言障碍组的儿童在形态句法的使用上都显示出较大的差异。

请问您需要我继续翻译接下来的内容吗？或者您有其他的具体要求？

language-disordered children differed on 1 1 variables from the normal children. When the three patterns of the language-disordered groups are compared, four tendencies in the language production of each group can be observed:
(1) a less frequent use of categories with a subject predicate structure;
( 2 ) a more frequent use of categories without a subject predicate structure;
(3) a less frequent use of pronouns;
(4) less verb agreement.
We also discovered differences in the overall performance of the three groups. In general, the performance of the group with specific language disorders was better than that of the children with hearing impairment, whereas the hearing-impaired children as a whole performed better than the group with Down’s syndrome. The variables on which their patterns differed concerned the same structures in which all language-disordered children differed from the normal children. What differs from group to group is the degree to which the language is affected. ln other words: the different clinical characteristics of our children did not so much lead to different kinds of language disorders as to differences in degree of language disorder.
Our study confirms the statement by Bloom and Lahey (1978) that, at least as far as morphosyntax is concerned, language-disordered children with different aetiologies show more commonalities than differences. The differences that can be distinguished between different groups mainly concern the degree to which their morphosyntactic development is affected.

语言障碍儿童在11个变量上与正常儿童有所不同。当三组语言障碍儿童的语言模式进行比较时，可以观察到每组语言生产中的四个趋势：
（1）较少使用主谓结构的类别；
（2）更多使用没有主谓结构的类别；
（3）较少使用代词；
（4）动词一致性较差。

我们还发现三组儿童的整体表现存在差异。总体而言，特定语言障碍组的表现优于听力障碍儿童组，而听力障碍儿童的整体表现又优于唐氏综合征组。他们模式不同的变量涉及所有语言障碍儿童与正常儿童之间存在差异的相同结构。不同组别之间的差异在于语言受影响的程度有所不同。换句话说：我们的儿童不同的临床特征不仅导致了不同程度的语言障碍，而且主要影响了语言障碍的发展程度。

本研究证实了Bloom和Lahey（1978）的观点，至少从形态句法角度来看，不同病因的语言障碍儿童表现出更多的共同点而不是差异。不同组别之间可区分的差异主要集中在他们的形态句法发展受影响的程度上。

# Title:

Trajectories of pragmatic and nonliteral language development in children with autism spectrum disorders

# Abstract:

Individuals with autism spectrum disorders (ASDs) have difficulties with the development of social and communicative abilities. However, for domains of language development, some theories (such as the relevance theory; e.g., Happe ´, 1993) suggest that some areas of language (especially the domains of pragmatic language or nonliteral language) may be disproportionately impacted for those individuals with autism who do show considerable development in their vocabulary and/or syntax abilities. For typically developing (TD) children, skills in both nonliteral language and pragmatic language

# Meta Translation

当然，以下是题目和摘要的中文翻译：

标题：自闭症谱系障碍儿童语用和非字面语言发展的轨迹

摘要：自闭症谱系障碍（ASD）个体在社会和交流能力的发展上存在困难。然而，在语言发展领域中，一些理论（例如，关联理论；例如，Happe，1993）认为，对于那些在词汇和/或句法能力方面有显著发展的自闭症患者而言，某些领域的语言（尤其是语用语言或非字面语言）可能受到不成比例的影响。对于正常发育（TD）儿童而言，他们在非字面语言和语用语言方面的技能

希望这些翻译能满足您的需求。如果有任何更具体的要求或进一步的调整需求，请告诉我！

continue to improve throughout childhood (Rundblad & Annaz, 2010a;Ryder & Leinonen, 2003). Some research suggests that as a group, children with autism spectrum disorder (ASD) often have a difficult time understanding both pragmatic language (Lam & Yeung, 2012;Tager-Flusberg & Anderson, 1991) and nonliteral language (Rundblad & Annaz, 2010b). However, individuals with ASD show great variability in the rate of language acquisition across development (Tek, Mesite, Fein, & Naigles, 2014). Understanding the predictors of progress in pragmatic language and nonliteral language development for individuals with autism may be crucial for creating appropriate individualized targets for intervention (Klin et al., 2007).
Comprehension of pragmatic language and nonliteral language share a common feature in that they require children to not only understand the individual meaning of words embedded in a sentence structure, but also to understand and respond appropriately to the communicative intent of language embedded in social and linguistic contexts (McTear & Conti-Ramsden, 1992). The specific definition of pragmatic language versus nonliteral language (as well as the boundary between these domains) varies between research studies, as well as the tasks used to assess abilities in these domains. The current study examines predictors of the development of pragmatic language and nonliteral language abilities using two subscales from the Comprehensive Assessment of Spoken Language (CASL; Carrow-Woolfolk, 1999). Pragmatic language in this case refers to the understanding and use of the literal aspects of context during communication (e.g., understanding the socially appropriate use of language for relevant contexts, such as: greetings, expressions of gratitude, making direct requests and answering questions). Nonliteral language refers to use of language where there is a specific mismatch between the literal meaning of the individual words of the phrase and the expected interpretation (e.g., ‘’he was such a turtle’’ means that ‘’he was slow’’ and not ‘’he was a reptile with a shell’’). Types of nonliteral language include figurative language (e.g., metaphors, such as ‘’the girl was a butterfly’’), sarcasm (e.g., saying ‘’good job’’ when someone does poorly), and indirect requests (e.g., ‘’I want all eyes on the board’’). Importantly, various aspects of nonliteral language may vary in how close the intended meaning of the phrase is to the individual words.
The majority of research on both pragmatic language and nonliteral language abilities in children with ASD has used group-matching designs (often averaging across large age ranges). However, the overall heterogeneity in language abilities in children with ASD can be problematic for group matching designs (Tager-Flusberg, 2004). In particular, little is known about the development with age of these abilities in children with ASD. In addition, little is known about how vocabulary and/or syntax development relates to either pragmatic language or nonliteral language development for children with ASD, and whether or not these developmental relations differ between children with ASD and TD. Research has recently begun to use more developmentally sensitive approaches to examining language abilities for children with autism (e.g., Rundblad & Annaz, 2010b), but there are still remaining questions about the relative progress in development of pragmatic language and figurative language. The current study uses a cross-sectional developmental trajectory analysis (Thomas et al., 2009) to examine how pragmatic language and nonliteral language abilities develop in children with ASD and TD with regard to their age, syntax, and vocabulary abilities.

这些技能在儿童期继续改善（Rundblad & Annaz, 2010a; Ryder & Leinonen, 2003）。一些研究表明，总体而言，患有自闭症谱系障碍（ASD）的儿童在理解语用语言（Lam & Yeung, 2012; Tager-Flusberg & Anderson, 1991）和非字面语言（Rundblad & Annaz, 2010b）方面通常面临困难。然而，ASD的个体在语言习得的速度上表现出极大的变化性（Tek, Mesite, Fein, & Naigles, 2014）。理解ASD个体在语用语言和非字面语言发展方面的进展预测因素对于制定适当且个性化的干预目标至关重要（Klin等, 2007）。

语用语言理解和非字面语言的理解都共享一个特性，即要求儿童不仅理解句子结构中嵌入单词的个别含义，还要理解并恰当地回应语言中的交流意图，这些意图嵌入了社会和语言环境中（McTear & Conti-Ramsden, 1992）。语用语言与非字面语言的具体定义（以及这两个领域的边界）在不同的研究中有所不同，所使用评估这些领域能力的任务也各不相同。本研究通过使用《口语综合评估量表》（CASL；Carrow-Woolfolk, 1999）的两个子量表，来考察语用语言和非字面语言能力的发展预测因素。在这种情况下，语用语言是指在沟通过程中对上下文的字面方面进行理解和使用（例如，理解在合适背景下使用的社会上合适语言，如问候、表示感谢、直接提出请求和回答问题）。非字面语言是指表达个体词汇词组的字面意思与预期解释之间存在特定差异的语言使用方式（例如，”他像乌龟一样缓慢”意味着”他行动迟缓”而不是”他是一只有壳的爬行动物”）。非字面语言的类型包括修辞语言（例如，比喻，如”这个女孩像一只蝴蝶”）、讽刺（例如，当某人做得不好时说”干得好”）和间接请求（例如，”我希望所有人都盯着板子看”）。重要的是，非字面语言的各种元素在短语的预期意义与单词的字面意义之间的接近程度上可能有所不同。

大部分关于ASD儿童的语用语言和非字面语言能力的研究采用了群组匹配设计（通常是跨较大年龄范围进行平均）。然而，ASD儿童间语言能力的整体异质性可能会使群组匹配设计变得复杂（Tager-Flusberg, 2004）。特别需要指出的是，目前还很少有关于ASD儿童随着年龄增长这些能力的发展情况方面的研究。此外，关于ASD儿童的词汇和/或句法发展如何与语用语言或非字面语言发展相关联，以及这些发展关系是否因ASD儿童与通常发展的儿童（TD）而异，我们也知之甚少。最近的研究已经开始采用更符合发展敏感性的方法来考察ASD儿童的语言能力（例如，Rundblad & Annaz, 2010b），但对于语用语言和比喻语言发展的相对进展方面的疑问仍存在。本研究使用交叉纵向发展轨迹分析（Thomas等, 2009）来考察在年龄、语法和词汇能力方面，ASD儿童和通常发展的儿童（TD）的语用语言和非字面语言能力的发展情况。

# Typical and atypical development

Pragmatic language abilities develop across childhood and into adolescence for TD children (Nippold, 2000;Ryder & Leionen, 2014). For example, Ryder and Leinonen (2003) suggest that 5-year-old children are able to understand and answer more complex questions than 3-or 4-year-old children based on their increasingly more complex ability to use contextual information. Lokusa, Leinonen, & Ryder (2007) examined pragmatic language abilities in children, ages 3-9, and found that while three-year-old children were able to use some context for resolving potential ambiguity when answering questions, the use of context increased substantially among the older children. Research suggests that children with ASD have difficulties in their pragmatic language development, including difficulties with the use language in the context of social conversations (Loukusa & Moilanen, 2009;Reichow, Salamack, Paul, Volkmar, & Klin, 2008;Volden, Coolican, Garon, White, & Bryson, 2009;Young, Diehl, Morris, Hyman, & Bennetto, 2005). Lam and Yeung (2012) found that children and adolescents with ASD, ages 8-15 years, performed worse than individuals with TD when using an observational scale to measure the pragmatic language abilities, such as having more instances of ‘’out-of-synchrony communicative behavior’’ (Lam & Yeung, 2012). Children with ASD do show some developmental progress in pragmatic abilities. Specifically, Loukusa, Leinonen, Kuusikko, et al. (2007) found that children with ASD who were 10-12 years old performed better at pragmatic language measures than children with ASD who were younger (7-9 years), suggesting that pragmatic language abilities and the use of context increases with age and experience for individuals with ASD.
Nonliteral language comprehension also shows a protracted developmental period across childhood in typical development. Some TD children, ages 4-6 years, are able to demonstrate an emerging knowledge of metaphors, with older children and adolescents showing greater levels of metaphor comprehension (Le Sourn-Bissaoui, Caillies, Bernard, Deleau, & Brule, 2012;Rundblad & Annaz, 2010a;Vosinadou & Ortony, 1983;Winner, Rosenstiel, & Gardner, 1976). Additionally, comprehension of indirect requests (Bernicot, Laval, & Chaminaud, 2007;Ledbetter & Dent, 1988) and sarcasm (Glenwright & Pexman, 2010) also increase with age for TD children. Children with ASD may also have difficulties with understanding various aspects of nonliteral language compared to their same-age typically developing peers (Dennis, Lazenby, & Lockyer, 2001;MacKay & Shaw, 2004;Martin & McDonald, 2004;Rundblad & Annaz, 2010b). Research has found that children with ASD (diagnosed with Asgerger’s syndrome or high functioning autism) perform worse than TD children on measures of metaphor comprehension (Dennis et al., 2001;Nikolaenko, 2004). In addition, MacKay and Shaw (2004) found that children with Asgerger’s syndrome showed difficulties on a variety of nonliteral language measures (including irony, metonymy, and indirect requests) compared to TD children. While many studies find differences, at the group-level, in pragmatic and nonliteral language abilities between TD children and children with ASD, important questions still remain about the development of these language abilities both in individuals with TD and ASD.

典型与非典型发展

对于典型的发育（TD）儿童，语用语言能力的发展贯穿整个童年并持续到青少年时期（Nippold, 2000; Ryder & Leinonen, 2014）。例如，Ryder和Leinonen（2003年）提出，五岁儿童能够理解并回答比三岁或四岁儿童更复杂的问题，这得益于他们使用情境信息的能力越来越复杂。Lokusa、Leinonen和Ryder（2007年）研究了3至9岁儿童的语用语言能力，发现虽然三岁的儿童在回答问题时能利用一些情境信息来解决潜在的歧义，但更为年长的儿童对情境信息的使用大幅增加。研究表明，患有自闭症谱系障碍（ASD）的儿童在其语用语言发展中存在困难，包括在社会对话中有效使用语言的困难（Loukusa & Moilanen, 2009; Reichow, Salamack, Paul, Volkmar, & Klin, 2008; Volden, Coolican, Garon, White, & Bryson, 2009; Young, Diehl, Morris, Hyman, & Bennetto, 2005）。Lam和Yeung（2012年）发现，年龄在8到15岁之间的ASD儿童和青少年在使用观察量表测量语用语言能力时表现较差，比如表现出更多的“不同步沟通行为”（Lam & Yeung, 2012）。ASD儿童确实显示出他们在语用能力方面的一些发展进步。具体来说，Loukusa、Leinonen、Kuusikko等（2007年）发现，10至12岁的ASD儿童在语用语言测验中的表现优于7至9岁的ASD儿童，这表明ASD个体的语用语言能力和对情境的使用随着年龄和经验的增长而增加。

非字面语言的理解在典型的发育过程中也显示出了一个漫长的发展期。一些4至6岁的TD儿童能够展示出对他们隐喻知识的初步了解，而年长的儿童和青少年则表现出更高水平的隐喻理解（Le Sourn-Bissaoui, Caillies, Bernard, Deleau, & Brule, 2012; Rundblad & Annaz, 2010a; Vosinadou & Ortony, 1983; Winner, Rosenstiel, & Gardner, 1976）。此外，TD儿童对间接请求（Bernicot, Laval, & Chaminaud, 2007; Ledbetter & Dent, 1988）和讽刺（Glenwright & Pexman, 2010）的理解也随年龄增长而提高。与同龄的TD同伴相比，患有ASD的儿童可能也有不同的理解各种非字面语言方面的困难（Dennis, Lazenby, & Lockyer, 2001; MacKay & Shaw, 2004; Martin & McDonald, 2004; Rundblad & Annaz, 2010b）。研究发现，在隐喻理解方面，被诊断为阿斯伯格综合症或高功能自闭症的ASD儿童在成绩上低于TD儿童（Dennis 等人，2001；Nikolaenko, 2004）。此外，MacKay和Shaw（2004年）发现，患有阿斯伯格综合症的儿童在许多非字面语言方面都遇到了困难，包括反讽、换喻和间接请求，这些表现都低于TD儿童。尽管许多研究发现在典型发育儿童和ASD儿童之间存在群体级别的差异，但在TD和ASD个体的语言能力发展方面仍然存在重要问题。

# Factors supporting development Part-1

Factors supporting understanding of pragmatic language and nonliteral language for children have been examined in the literature, including the potential contributions of basic language abilities and theory of mind (TOM) for both language domains, though these relationships have been more commonly studied with regard to nonliteral language. For TD children, there is some evidence that language abilities develop together in parallel, with basic language abilities (such as vocabulary) correlating strongly with nonliteral language abilities (Johnson, 1991;Rundblad & Annaz, 2010a). Research suggests that understanding of nonliteral language is supported by the ability to use the linguistic and social context to abstract meaning, and that vocabulary and syntax abilities are likely to support this process (Gernsbacher & Pripas-Kapit, 2012;Rundblad & Annaz, 2010a;Vosniadou, 1987). With regard to pragmatic language, Volden et al. (2009) found that a composite of expressive and receptive basic language abilities predicted a large portion of the variance in pragmatic language ability for children with ASD. Eisenmajer and Prior (1991) found that pragmatic language abilities correlated with several basic language measures, supporting the relationship between basic language abilities and pragmatic language. There is, however, some controversy in the literature as to whether or not nonliteral language abilities are disproportionately impacted for children with ASD, beyond their potential differences in basic language abilities. For example, Rundblad and Annaz (2010b) found that receptive vocabulary abilities only predicted performance on metonyms, but not metaphors, in their sample of 10 children with ASD.
The relevance theory has driven research focused on the potential role of theory of mind for contributing to pragmatic language (Le Sourn-Bissaoui, Caillies, Gierski, & Motte, 2011;Loukusa & Moilanen, 2009) difficulties for children with ASD. Loukusa and Moilanen (2009) suggest that receptive vocabulary skills alone may be insufficient for understanding various aspects of pragmatic language for individuals with ASD, due to their likely difficulties with regard to the use of the social and linguistic context for understanding the meaning of these utterances. This line of research largely suggests that individuals with ASD struggle with these more advanced language abilities, even when they have good basic language abilities (e.g., receptive vocabulary), potentially due to weaknesses in utilizing the social and linguistic context for understanding the meaning of these utterances (Loukusa & Moilanen, 2009;Noens & van Berckelaer-Onnes, 2005).
Thus, limitations with theory of mind abilities have been implicated in difficulties with understanding nonliteral language, especially with regard to understanding metaphors (Happe ´, 1993)。

支持儿童理解实用语言和非字面语言的因素已在文献中被探讨，这些因素包括基本语言能力和心智理论（TOM）对于这两个语言领域可能的贡献，尽管这些关系在研究非字面语言方面更为常见。对于通常发展（TD）的儿童，有证据表明语言能力是并行发展的，基本语言能力（如词汇量）与非字面语言能力之间的相关性很强（Johnson, 1991; Rundblad & Annaz, 2010a）。研究表明，对非字面语言的理解受到利用语言和社会背景抽象意义的能力的支持，并且词汇量和句法能力很可能支持这一过程（Gernsbacher & Pripas-Kapit, 2012; Rundblad & Annaz, 2010a; Vosniadou, 1987）。就实用语言而言，Volden等（2009）发现，表达和接受基本语言能力的综合预测了自闭障碍（ASD）儿童实用语言能力方差的一个较大比例。Eisenmajer和Prior（1991）发现，实用语言能力与几种基本语言指标相关，这支持了基本语言能力和实用语言之间的关系。然而，在文献中存在一些争议，即除了他们的基本语言能力差异外，非字面语言能力是否更不成比例地受到影响。例如，Rundblad和Annaz（2010b）发现，在他们研究的10名ASD儿童样本中，接受性词汇能力仅预测了成语的表现，但并未预测隐喻。

关联理论推动了关于心智理论可能对ASD儿童实用语言（Le Sourn-Bissaoui, Caillies, Gierski, & Motte, 2011; Loukusa & Moilanen, 2009）困难的潜在贡献的研究。Loukusa和Moilanen（2009）认为，仅凭接受性词汇技能可能不足以理解ASD个体的各种实用语言方面，这可能是由于他们在使用社会和语言背景理解这些语句所蕴含的意义时存在的问题。这项研究主要表明，即使ASD个体具备良好的基础语言能力（例如，接受性词汇），他们仍在这些更高级的语言能力方面遇到困难，这可能是由于在利用社会和语言背景理解这些语句所蕴含意义方面的弱点（Loukusa & Moilanen, 2009; Noens & van Berckelaer-Onnes, 2005）。

因此，心智理论能力的局限性被认为是理解非字面语言困难的重要原因，特别是在理解隐喻方面（Happe ´, 1993）。

# Factors supporting development Part-2

While primarily examined with regard to performance on first-or second-order false belief measures (e.g., Happe ´, 1993), there have overall been mixed results with using false belief measures with older children, with some studies failing to find a unique contribution of false belief performance on nonliteral language abilities (e.g., Norbury, 2005;Rundblad & Annaz, 2010b). Other advanced measures of theory of mind, that are more developmentally sensitive across childhood, may instead better elucidate these relations. For example, performance on the children’s ‘’reading the mind in the eyes’’ task (RMTE; Baron-Cohen, Wheelwright, Spong, Scahill, & Lawson, 2001) is correlated with idiom comprehension abilities (e.g., understanding phrases such as ‘’raining cats and dogs’’) in children with autism (Whyte, Nelson, & Scherf, 2014), but it is unknown how this measure relates to measures of pragmatic language or nonliteral language abilities.
Other research suggests that receptive vocabulary may be an area of relative strength for individuals with ASD when compared to their syntax abilities (Eigsti, Bennetto, & Dadlani, 2007). It is possible that syntax abilities, specifically, are predictive of their relative pragmatic (Volden et al., 2009) and nonliteral language abilities (Gernsbacher & Pripas-Kapit, 2012;Norbury, 2004Norbury, , 2005;;Whyte, Nelson, & Khan, 2013) for individuals with ASD, rather than a diagnosis of ASD in particular. For nonliteral language, Norbury (2005) found that syntax comprehension is a better predictor of metaphor comprehension than receptive vocabulary in particular, for children with language impairments, regardless of whether or not they exhibited social impairments associated with ASD. Additionally, children with ASD (especially those with good syntax abilities) were able to benefit from the use of context in understanding unfamiliar idiomatic phrases (Norbury, 2004). This line of research overall suggests that some children with ASD may not show impairments in pragmatic language or nonliteral language if they show significant progress in the development of their basic language abilities (Gernsbacher & Pripas-Kapit, 2012;Norbury, 2004Norbury, , 2005;;Whyte et al., 2014). Thus, understanding the role of expressive vocabulary and syntax abilities in supporting the development of pragmatic language and nonliteral language may be important for choosing appropriate matching variables to prevent biased conclusions about the nature of language abilities for individuals with ASD。

尽管这些理论主要通过考察儿童在一级或二级错误信念测验中的表现（如Happe ´, 1993所提出的），对于年龄较大的儿童来说，使用错误信念测验的整体结果却是混合的，有些研究未能发现错误信念的表现对非字面语言能力有独特贡献（例如，Norbury, 2005; Rundblad & Annaz, 2010b）。其他更为发展敏感的高级心智理论测量方法可能更能阐明这些关系。比如，自闭症儿童在“读心眼”任务（RMTE；Baron-Cohen, Wheelwright, Spong, Scahill, & Lawson, 2001）中的表现与习语理解能力（即理解诸如“倾盆大雨”这样的短语）有关（Whyte, Nelson, & Scherf, 2014），但尚不清楚这一测验如何与衡量实用语言或非字面语言能力的测验相关。

其他研究表明，与他们的句法能力相比，自闭症个体的接受性词汇可能是相对较强的一项（Eigsti, Bennetto, & Dadlani, 2007）。有可能句法能力特别是能预测其相对实用（Volden 等人，2009）和非字面语言能力（Gernsbacher & Pripas-Kapit, 2012; Norbury, 2004, 2005; Whyte, Nelson, & Khan, 2013）的能力，并不一定是自闭症谱系障碍的具体诊断。就非字面语言而言，Norbury（2005年）发现，在语言障碍儿童中，特别是那些具有社交障碍症状的儿童，句法理解能力比接受性词汇是更好的隐喻理解的预测指标。此外，自闭症儿童（特别是句法能力较强的）能够从上下文中受益，从而帮助他们理解不熟悉的习语（Norbury, 2004）。这一系列研究整体上表明，一些自闭症儿童如果在基础语言能力的发展上取得显著进展，则可能不会显示出实用语言或非字面语言方面的障碍（Gernsbacher & Pripas-Kapit, 2012；Norbury, 2004, 2005；Whyte 等人，2014）。因此，了解表达性词汇和句法能力在支持实用语言和发展非字面语言方面的作用，可能对选择适当的匹配变量以防止对自闭症患者语言能力性质得出偏见结论至关重要。

# Factors supporting development Part-3

Further, any theoretical account of language development in children with TD as well as those with ASD needs to take into account how the varied language domains may develop together across childhood, and how this also may interact with other domains, such as theory of mind.

此外，任何关于典型发展（TD）儿童以及自闭症谱系障碍（ASD）儿童语言发展的理论解释都需要考虑到各种语言领域如何在童年时期共同发展，并且这种共同发展是如何与其他领域（如心智理论）相互作用的。

# Developmental trajectories

One approach to examining potential relations between language domains across development, arising from the neuroconstructivist theory, is the cross-sectional developmental trajectory analysis (Thomas et al., 2009). The developmental trajectory analysis described by Thomas et al. (2009) allows for examining differences in the rate of growth of language abilities across development, even for cross-sectional samples, using ANCOVA models to directly compare the potential differences in the intercepts and slopes of the trajectories. It is possible to look at age-related trajectories for a group of children with ASD compared to TD children to see if the children with ASD have a different rate of development with regard to chronological age. It is also possible to examine the rate of development in a behavior as a function of various possible predictors, such as vocabulary or syntax (Annaz, Karmiloff-Smith, & Thomas, 2008;Thomas et al., 2009). This analysis approach can detect group differences in the intercept of the trajectory (defined as differences at the youngest point of overlap in scores on the predictor variable between the groups), slowed rate of development (defined as differences in the slopes of the trend lines between groups), or both (Annaz et al., 2008;Thomas et al., 2009) for each potential predictor variable. This stands in contrast to traditional group matching approaches that are only sensitive to overall group differences.
For group matching approaches, the choice of matching variables needs to be theory-driven, as improperly matched groups runs a risk of leading to biased conclusions about the nature of symptoms in autism (Gernsbacher & Pripas-Kapit, 2012;Jarrold & Brock, 2004;Thomas et al., 2009). However, the trajectory approach does not require this same a priori group matching. Instead of controlling for differences in vocabulary and other potential matching variables between groups, this approach can tell us important information about how these variables may actually provide important contributions to the rate of development of pragmatic and nonliteral language abilities. While this approach does not reduce the need for longitudinal research, it is more developmentally sensitive than group matching designs, and can potentially inform future longitudinal research (Annaz et al., 2008;Thomas et al., 2009).
This cross-sectional developmental trajectory approach has been previously used in several studies to examine the development of vocabulary, nonliteral language, and face processing abilities of children with ASD (Annaz, Karmiloff-Smith, Johnson, & Thomas, 2009;Kover, McDuffie, Hagerman, & Abbeduto, 2013;Rundblad & Annaz, 2010b). For example, Rundblad and Annaz (2010b) used a developmental trajectory analysis to examine two different aspects of nonliteral language (metaphors and metonyms) in 11 children with ASD, ages 5-11 years. For the children with ASD, receptive vocabulary predicted performance on metonyms, but not metaphors (Rundblad & Annaz, 2010b). However, additional measures of language abilities (including syntax abilities and expressive vocabulary abilities) and larger sample sizes are needed to further investigate development of nonliteral language for children with ASD.

发展轨迹

从神经构造主义理论出发，考察发展过程中语言领域之间可能存在的关系的一种方法是横断发展轨迹分析（Thomas等，2009年）。Thomas等人（2009年）描述的发展轨迹分析允许通过使用协方差分析模型（ANCOVA）来比较横断样本中语言能力增长速度的差异，即使在横断研究中也是如此。通过这种方法，可以对比自闭症谱系障碍（ASD）儿童与典型发育（TD）儿童的发展轨迹，以确定ASD儿童是否因实际年龄而具有不同的发展速率。此外，该分析还可以检查行为发展的速率如何受多种可能的预测变量（如词汇量或句法能力）的影响（Annaz、Karmiloff-Smith和Thomas，2008年；Thomas等，2009年）。

这种分析方法可以检测出轨迹截距上的组间差异（定义为预测变量评分在最年轻重叠点之间的组间差异）、发展速率减慢（定义为趋势线斜率之间的组间差异），或者两者兼有（Annaz等，2008年；Thomas等，2009年），对于每个潜在的预测变量。这与仅对总体组间差异敏感的传统组匹配方法形成对比。

对于组匹配方法而言，选择匹配变量需要基于理论驱动，因为不当的组匹配可能导致对自闭症症状性质的偏见结论（Gernsbacher和Pripas-Kapit，2012年；Jarrold和Brock，2004年；Thomas等，2009年）。然而，轨迹方法不需要相同的先验组匹配。相反，这种方法无需控制词汇量和其他潜在匹配变量之间的差异，便可以提供有关这些变量如何实际上对语用语言和非字面语言能力的发展速率产生重要贡献的重要信息。尽管这种方法并不能减少对纵向研究的需求，但相比于组匹配设计，这种方法更能反映发展情况，并且可以为进一步的纵向研究提供潜在指导（Annaz等，2008年；Thomas等，2009年）。

以前一些研究已经使用了这种横断发展轨迹方法来探讨ASD儿童词汇、非字面语言和面部识别能力的发展（Annaz、Karmiloff-Smith、Johnson和Thomas，2009；Kover、McDuffie、Hagerman和Abbeduto，2013；Rundblad和Annaz，2010b）。例如，Rundblad和Annaz（2010b）使用发展轨迹分析检验了11名5至11岁患有ASD的儿童在非字面语言中的两个不同方面，即隐喻和转喻。对于ASD儿童来说，接收词汇预测了他们对转喻的反应表现，但却不能预测隐喻的表现（Rundblad和Annaz，2010b）。然而，需要更多的语言能力测量（包括句法能力和表达式词汇能力）以及更大的样本量来进一步调查ASD儿童非字面语言的发展。

# Current study

The current study uses the trajectory analysis methods of Thomas et al. (2009) to examine how age, vocabulary, syntax, and theory of mind predict performance on the pragmatic language and nonliteral language subtests of the Comprehensive Assessment of Spoken Language (CASL; Carrow-Woolfolk, 1999) for children with ASD and TD. The two subtests from the CASL (pragmatic language and nonliteral language) were chosen due to their potential use in measuring nonliteral and pragmatic language in clinical settings (e.g., Reichow et al., 2008). Additionally, these outcome measures are sensitive across a wide age range of development and are unlikely to show ceiling or floor effects for either individuals with TD or ASD.
For the current study, the age range of 5-12 years was chosen such that it would be likely that TD children aged 5-6 may perform poorly on these measures, with increasing mastery of pragmatic and nonliteral language with increasing age for the TD children. Thus, it is hypothesized that there may not be a difference in the youngest age of overlap between groups for the current sample (representing the intercepts of the trajectories). The primary outcome of interest, instead, is the comparison of the rate of development between groups for each trajectory. The current study hypothesizes that children with ASD will have slower rates of development of nonliteral and pragmatic language trajectories from the TD group when examining chronological age, but the two groups will not have significantly different nonliteral or pragmatic language trajectories when examining relations with syntax age-equivalence scores, vocabulary age-equivalence scores, or TOM scores. Additionally, it is predicted that TOM abilities will significantly relate to individual differences in pragmatic and nonliteral language abilities, above and beyond the contributions of basic language abilities.

本研究采用Thomas等人（2009年）的轨迹分析方法，考察年龄、词汇量、语法和心智理论如何预测自闭症谱系障碍（ASD）儿童和典型发展（TD）儿童在综合性口语评估（CASL；Carrow-Woolfolk，1999年）中的语用语言和非字面语言子测验的表现。之所以选择CASL的这两个子测验（语用语言和非字面语言），是因为它们在临床上可能被用来测量非字面语言和语用语言（例如，Reichow等人，2008年）。此外，这些测量结果对于广泛的发育阶段都敏感，并且不太可能出现天花板效应或地板效应，无论是对TD儿童还是ASD儿童。

在本研究中，选择了5至12岁的年龄段，以期在此年龄段内，5至6岁的TD儿童在这两项测量中可能表现较差，而随着TD儿童年龄的增长，他们的语用语言和非字面语言能力将逐渐提高。因此，假设在当前样本中，两个群体在最年轻的重叠年龄上可能没有显著差异（即，它们各自轨迹的截距）。而主要关注的结果是比较两组之间每条轨迹的发展速度差异。目前的研究假设，当考虑实际年龄时，ASD儿童在非字面语言和语用语言轨迹的发展速度会慢于TD儿童，但当观察与语法年龄等分数、词汇年龄等分数或TOM得分的关系时，两组在非字面语言和语用语言轨迹方面不会显示出显著性差异。此外，还预期TOM能力在控制基本语言能力的影响后，仍然会显著影响个体之间的语用和非字面语言能力差异。

# Children with ASD

A total of 26 children (21 m, 5 f), ages 5-12 (M = 9.07, SD = 1.87) years, who were previously diagnosed with an autism spectrum disorder (ASD), participated in the study (see Table 1). Highly verbal children were included if they had a previous diagnosis by a clinician under the DSM-IV criteria (American Psychiatric Association, 1994) of autism or high-functioning autism (n = 8), Asperger’s syndrome (n = 13), or pervasive developmental disorder (PDD-NOS; n = 5), based on parent report. The current study collapses across these diagnostic labels, as suggested by the newest DSM-5 criteria (e.g., Mahjouri & Lord, 2012); especially given the recent concerns of potential variability in how these diagnostic labels were applied by clinicians and researchers (e.g., Lord et al., 2012). Participants were included if they were able to speak in sentences, were receiving treatment services or educational supports related to ASD, and had a raw score above 60 on the parent report Social Responsiveness Scale (SRS) that indicated the presence of high current levels of autistic social impairments (Constantino, 2002). Scores on the SRS measure of autism symptom severity ranged from 60 to 155 (M = 108.61) for the children with ASD. One additional child with ASD (not included in the above totals) was excluded due to having a score below 60 on the SRS.
A total of 21 of the 26 children with ASD were either currently or previously enrolled in speech therapy services. Participants were native English speakers from middle-class neighborhoods in the United States, and had normal or corrected-to-normal hearing and vision. Parent report indicated that 22 children were non-Hispanic and Caucasian, 2 children were Hispanic and Caucasian, 1 child was American Indian, and 1 child was biracial. Participants were recruited through fliers distributed through an autism participant recruitment database, special education classrooms at schools, and autism social skills intervention programs.

共有26名儿童（21名男童，5名女童）参与了本研究，年龄在5至12岁之间（平均年龄为9.07岁，标准差为1.87岁），这些儿童之前被诊断为自闭症谱系障碍（ASD）（参见表1）。如果经过临床医师根据《美国精神疾病诊断与统计手册》第四版（DSM-IV；美国精神医学协会，1994年）的标准（自闭症或高功能自闭症n=8，阿斯伯格综合症n=13，广泛性发育障碍未另行说明PDD-NOSn=5）诊断为具有高度语言能力的儿童也被纳入研究（基于家长报告）。当前研究根据最新的DSM-5标准（例如，Mahjouri & Lord, 2012）合并了这些诊断标签；特别是考虑到最近关于临床医生和研究人员在应用这些诊断标签时可能存在变异性的担忧（例如，Lord等, 2012）。参与者入选的标准是能够用句子进行交流、正在接受与ASD相关的治疗服务或教育支持，并且在父母报告的社会反应量表（SRS）中原始分数高于60分，表明存在高水平的自闭症社交障碍（Constantino, 2002）。自闭症症状严重程度量表（SRS测量）的得分范围为60到155分（平均值为108.61分）。有一名额外的ASD儿童由于SRS得分低于60分而被排除在外。

26名ASD儿童中有21名目前或此前曾参加过言语治疗服务。参与者来自美国中产阶级社区，母语为英语，听力和视力正常或矫正后正常。家长报告显示，22名儿童是非西班牙裔白人，2名为西班牙裔和白人，1名为美洲印第安人，1名为混血。参与者通过分发给自闭症受试者招募数据库、学校特殊教育教室和自闭症社交技能干预项目的传单进行招募。

# TD children

A total of 69 typically developing children (39 m, 30 f), ages 5-12 years (M = 8.4 years, SD = 24.14), participated in the study (see Table 1). Children were excluded from the TD group if they had a diagnosis of a language impairments, a diagnosis of any other developmental disorder (such as ADHD or autism), were currently receiving speech therapy services, or had a score on the SRS above 50 (allowing for a 10 point gap in the SRS scores between groups). Participants were native English speakers from middle-class neighborhoods, with normal or corrected-to-normal hearing and vision. Parent report indicated that 57 children were non-Hispanic and Caucasian, 5 children were Hispanic and Caucasian, 1 child was American Indian, 5 children were biracial, and 1 child was African-American. Participants were recruited using fliers and phone calls to families from a participant recruitment database containing information from birth records in a geographic area within approximately an hour drive of the university.
The TD children were recruited to span from the youngest mental age (represented by age-equivalence scores on vocabulary and syntax) to the oldest chronological age of the children with ASD (see Table 1). When using a trajectory analysis, restricting the normal variability of the TD children by removal of any individuals with high performance on any predictor variable may bias the results of the trajectories (Thomas et al., 2009), and it is recommended that specific group matching on the predictor variables not be done for this analysis. Thus, while the children with ASD had significantly lower syntax scores than TD children, t(93) = 2.29, p < .05, this mean difference for syntax is unlikely to impact any of the current study results. The children with ASD also had higher SRS scores than the TD children, t(93) = 23.02, p < .05. For the TD children, chronological age was predictive of 74.5% of the variance in vocabulary age-equivalence scores, from the verbal IQ subtest of the Kaufman Brief Intelligence Test, 2nd edition (KBIT2; Kaufman & Kaufman, 2004), and 66.2% of the variance in syntax age-equivalence scores from the CASL syntax construction subtest. In addition, standardized nonverbal IQ scores (from the KBIT-2 nonverbal IQ subtest) for the TD children were in the average range (M = 107.68; SD = 15.71).

共计69名通常发展儿童（39名男性，30名女性），年龄在5至12岁之间（平均年龄为8.4岁，标准差为24.14），参与了本研究（详见表1）。如果儿童被诊断出有语言障碍、其他发育障碍（如ADHD或自闭症）、当前正在接受言语治疗服务，或在社会交往量表(SRS)上的得分超过50分（允许组间SRS得分相差10分），则被排除在通常发展群体之外。参与者均为来自中产阶级社区的母语是英语的儿童，并且听力和视力正常或已矫正至正常水平。父母报告指出，57名儿童是非西班牙裔白人，5名儿童是西班牙裔白人，1名儿童是美国印第安人，5名儿童是混血儿，1名儿童是非裔美国人。参与者是通过散发传单和电话联系参与招募数据库中的家庭来招募的，该数据库包含了距大学一小时车程内的地理区域内出生证明的信息。

通常发展儿童被招募来覆盖从最小的心智年龄（由词汇和句法的年龄等值分数表示）到自闭症谱系障碍儿童中最大的实际年龄范围（参见表1）。当使用轨迹分析时，去除所有预测变量上表现高的参与者以限制通常发展儿童的正常变异性可能会使轨迹的结果偏向化（Thomas等，2009年），并且建议在这一分析中不要对预测变量进行特定的群体匹配。因此，尽管自闭症谱系障碍儿童的句法得分显著低于通常发展儿童，t(93) = 2.29, p < .05，这种差异不大可能影响当前研究结果。自闭症谱系障碍儿童的社会交往量表(SRS)的得分也高于通常发展儿童，t(93) = 23.02, p < .05。对于通常发展儿童而言，实际年龄可以解释语言年龄等值分数变异性的74.5%，基于考夫曼简短智力测验第二版（KBIT2；Kaufman & Kaufman，2004）的口语IQ子测试，以及句法建构子测试中句法年龄等值分数变异性的66.2%。此外，通常发展儿童的标准非言语IQ分数（来自KBIT-2非言语IQ子测试）处于平均水平（平均值=107.68；标准差=15.71）。

# Pragmatic language

The Pragmatic Judgment subtest of the CASL was completed (Carrow-Woolfolk, 1999). Items on this measure involved judging the appropriate use of language in a social context (e.g., explaining that it is n’t appropriate to talk about dissecting worms when eating lunch at school, or to talk loudly in a movie theater), and verbally producing language appropriate for the context (e.g., ordering food in a restaurant, making requests, saying please or thank you, asking for directions, and greeting people appropriately). An example item includes: ‘’Suppose the telephone rings. You pick it up. What do you say?’’ (Carrow-Woolfolk, 1999). Responses did not need to be grammatically correct as long as they were pragmatically appropriate for the situation. Raw scores could range from 1 to 63.

《语用判断》子测试是使用《儿童语用语言量表》（CASL；Carrow-Woolfolk, 1999）完成的。该量表中的项目涉及判断在社交情境中语言使用的适当性（例如，在学校吃午饭时解释不应该谈论解剖蚯蚓的话题，或在电影院大声说话），以及口头生成符合情境的语言（例如，在餐厅点餐、提出请求、说“请”或“谢谢”、问路和恰当地问候他人）。一个示例题目是：“假设电话响了，你接起了电话。你会说什么？”（Carrow-Woolfolk, 1999）。只要回答在情境上得当，不一定需要语法正确。原始得分范围可以从1分到63分。

# Nonliteral language

The Nonliteral Language subtest of the CASL was completed (Carrow-Woolfolk, 1999). This subtest contains various types of nonliteral language expressions, where the intent of the spoken phrases differs from a literal interpretation, categorized as figurative, indirect requests, and sarcasm (Carrow-Woolfolk, 1999). Each non-literal phrase is presented in the context of a short sentence supporting the figurative meaning. For example, items could include metaphors, such as: ‘’Janet was waiting for Sara to finish changing into her swimsuit. Janet said, ‘You are such a turtle.’ What did Janet mean?’’ An example of indirect requests included: ‘’The teacher told the class that he wanted all eyes on the board. What did he mean?’’ The two children scoring zero points on this measure (one with ASD and one with TD) are excluded from the analysis due to recommendations of the test protocols (Carrow-Woolfolk, 1999). Total nonliteral raw scores could range from 1 to 50.

非字面语言子测试由CASL完成（Carrow-Woolfolk, 1999）。该子测试包含多种类型的非字面语言表达，这些表达的意图与字面理解不同，被分类为比喻、间接请求和讽刺（Carrow-Woolfolk, 1999）。每个非字面短语都以一个支持比喻意义的简短句子为背景呈现。例如，项目中可能包括比喻表达：“珍妮特在等萨拉换好泳衣。珍妮特说：‘你真是个乌龟。’珍妮特是什么意思？”间接请求的例子有：“老师告诉全班同学，他希望所有的人都把目光集中在黑板上。他的意思是？”

根据测试协议的建议（Carrow-Woolfolk, 1999），在这项测试中获得零分的两名儿童（一名患有自闭症谱系障碍，一名属于普通发展组）被排除在分析之外。非字面语言原始分数范围从1到50。

# Syntax

The Syntax Construction subtest of the CASL was completed (Carrow-Woolfolk, 1999). The experimenter presented pictures and asked the child to verbally complete sentences. The targeted syntactic structures (e.g., verb tense, plurals, and prepositional phrases) in the sentences grew increasingly complex throughout the test. Syntax raw scores (out of a possible 60 points) were converted into age-equivalence scores (in months).

语法结构部分的测试使用了CASL的语法构造子测验（Carrow-Woolfolk，1999）。实验者展示了图片，并要求儿童口头完成句子。在整个测试过程中，句子中目标化的语法结构（例如动词时态、复数形式和介词短语）逐渐变得更为复杂。语法原始分数（最高60分）被转换成等效年龄分数（以月为单位）。

# Vocabulary

Receptive and expressive vocabulary abilities were assessed using the Verbal IQ subtests from the Kaufman Brief Intelligence Test, 2nd edition (KBIT2; Kaufman & Kaufman, 2004). This vocabulary measure was a composite of two sub-tests, verbal knowledge (measuring receptive vocabulary) and riddles (measuring verbal comprehension and expressive vocabulary). The riddles subtest asked children to provide one word answers to questions such as: ‘’what hops, eats carrots, and has long ears?’’ (e.g., rabbit or bunny). Total raw vocabulary scores (out of 108 points) were converted into ageequivalence scores (in months).

接收性和表达性词汇能力通过凯夫曼简明智力测验第二版（Kaufman Brief Intelligence Test, 2nd edition, KBIT2；Kaufman & Kaufman, 2004）的言语智商子测试来评估。该词汇测量工具包括两个子测试：言语知识（衡量接受性词汇）和猜谜游戏（衡量言语理解能力和表达性词汇）。猜谜子测试要求儿童用一个词回答问题，例如：“什么会跳跃、吃胡萝卜并且有长耳朵？”（例如，兔子或兔崽子）。总原始词汇分数（满分108分）转换为年龄当量分数（以月为单位）。

# Theory of mind

The children’s version of the ‘’Reading the Mind in the Eyes’’ (RMTE) task was used to measure theory of mind abilities ( Baron-Cohen et al., 2001). During this task, children viewed pictures of the eye regions of faces. The children were asked to choose one of four labels which best matched the expression or mental state of the person in the pictures (i.e., shy, worried, thinking about something, not believing). The labels were read out loud to the children. Scores could range from 0 to 28.

使用儿童版本的“眼神读心”（RMTE）任务来测量理论思维能力（Baron-Cohen等，2001）。在该任务中，儿童观看脸部眼睛区域的照片。要求儿童从四个标签中选择一个最符合照片中人物的表情或心理状态（例如，害羞、担忧、在想着某事、不相信）。标签由研究者大声读给儿童听。得分范围从0到28分。

# Additional background measures

The matrices subtest of the KBIT-2 was used to measure nonverbal IQ (Kaufman & Kaufman, 2004). One parent for each child completed the Social Responsiveness Scale (SRS), which is a questionnaire used to assess current social skills and repetitive behaviors, with higher scores indicating more severe social impairments associated with ASD symptomology (Constantino, 2002). Nonverbal IQ and SRS scores were not significantly correlated with either pragmatic language or nonliteral language scores (all p > .05).

使用KBIT-2的矩阵子测试来测量非言语智商（Kaufman & Kaufman, 2004）。每位儿童的一位家长完成了《社会应答量表》(SRS)，这是一个用于评估当前社交技能和重复行为的问卷，得分越高表示自闭症症状相关的社交障碍越严重（Constantino, 2002）。非言语智商和SRS得分与实用语言或非字面语言得分之间没有显著相关性（所有p值> .05）。

# Procedure

Prior to their child’s participation in the study, a parent or legal guardian provided informed consent and then completed a brief demographic questionnaire and the SRS for their child. In addition, all children provided verbal assent prior to participating. The experimental procedures complied with the standards of the university’s review board. Participant families were compensated for their time. The study was completed over two hours (completed over 1 or 2 sessions). Testing took place either in offices in the research lab, or in a quiet room in the child’s home (for families who were unable to travel to the lab). Testing procedures were kept as similar as possible across testing locations, and children completed the tasks in the same order. For all tasks in the current study, the test items were read aloud to the children, and children were asked to respond verbally (or by pointing when appropriate). Breaks were provided between tasks as necessary to ensure attention.

在儿童参与研究之前，其父母或法定监护人提供了知情同意，并完成了关于其子女的简要人口统计问卷和SRS（社交沟通评估量表）。此外，所有儿童在参与前均口头表示同意。实验程序符合大学审查委员会的标准。参与者家庭因其时间而得到了补偿。该研究在两小时内完成（分1次或2次完成）。测试地点要么在研究实验室内的办公室进行，要么在儿童家中安静的房间进行（对于无法前往实验室的家庭而言）。尽量保持各测试地点的测试程序一致，儿童以相同的顺序完成各项任务。在本研究的所有任务中，测试项目都由研究人员读给儿童听，并要求他们口头回答（或根据需要以指指点点的方式回答）。必要时，在各个任务之间提供休息以确保儿童的注意力集中。

# Developmental trajectory analysis

The cross-sectional developmental trajectory analysis approach followed the methods of Thomas et al. (2009). Separate regressions were conducted for each group (ASD and TD) to see if each of the outcome variables (pragmatic language and nonliteral language) increases with each of the predictor variables (chronological age, syntax age-equivalence scores, vocabulary age-equivalence scores, or TOM scores). These regressions allow for establishing whether or not the outcome measures show a significant relation with the predictors for each of the two groups (e.g., if pragmatic language increases with age). In addition, Cook’s Distance values were calculated for each regression, with all values less than the recommended cut-off of one, suggesting that there were no significant outliers in the current dataset for either the ASD or TD groups.
Once establishing that there are reliable linear trajectories for each group, the trajectories of the two groups are compared using ANCOVA models, with pragmatic CASL scores and nonliteral CASL scores as separate outcome variables. Thomas et al. (2009) suggests that each predictor variable needs to be re-scaled to compare the groups starting from the youngest age at which the two groups overlap to be able to interpret differences between groups at the intercept. To prevent extrapolating outside the age/score ranges measured, the predictor variables were scaled by subtracting each individual’s score (from both groups) from the youngest age at which the two groups overlapped, so that zero represented the first point of overlap between the two trajectories (Thomas et al., 2009). This scaling is done so that the value of zero for the intercept represents the start of the age range that has been measured, and thus potential differences measured in the intercept of the trajectory (e.g., the ‘’youngest age of overlap’’ or ‘’earliest point of overlap’’) refer to measurements at this zero point for each predictor variable. For chronological age and RMTE scores, this was scaled as months from the youngest age of the ASD group. For the vocabulary and syntax predictor variables, where the TD group performed slightly higher than the ASD group, this was instead scaled to months from youngest TD age-equivalence score.
To compare cross-sectional developmental trajectories for chronological age, an ANCOVA is conducted with the predictor variables of: diagnosis as a fixed factor (representing potential differences in the intercept -at the youngest age of overlap between groups), as well as age (months from the youngest age of overlap) as a covariate. This model also includes the analysis of the interaction between scaled age scores and diagnosis (representing the slope of the trajectory, and specifically measuring potential differences in the rate of development with age; Thomas et al., 2009). Thus, unlike group matching studies (comparing one mean value averaging across age), the results from this trajectory analysis provide two pieces of information about potential differences between the trajectories for individuals with ASD and TD with regard to age. First, is there a significant difference in the youngest age of overlap between the groups (representing the intercept of this trajectory)? Second, is there a difference in the rate of development between the groups (indicated by a significant interaction between diagnosis and the scaled age variable)? The results from both of these potential differences are included in the below results, though this second result (the rate of development) is of primary interest in the current study. The same models are then repeated separately for the vocabulary, syntax, and RMTE predictors, in place of age in the models.

发展轨迹分析

采用交叉截面发展轨迹分析方法，遵循了Thomas等人（2009）的方法。首先对每个组别（自闭症谱系障碍组和典型发育组）分别进行回归分析，以探究因变量（交际语言和非字面语言）是否随着任何一个预测变量（实际年龄、句法年龄等效分数、词汇年龄等效分数或心智理论得分）的增加而变化。这些回归分析可以确定因变量在两组中与各个预测变量之间是否存在显著关系（例如，如果交际语言随着年龄的增加而增加）。此外，还为每个回归计算了Cook’s Distance值，所有值均低于推荐的临界值1，表明当前数据集中无论是自闭症谱系障碍组还是典型发育组都不存在显著异常值。

确认每组都有可靠的线性轨迹后，使用ANCOVA模型比较这两组的轨迹，将交际CASL评分和非字面CASL评分作为独立的因变量。Thomas等人（2009）建议每个预测变量需要重新缩放，以便从两组最早重叠开始的最年轻年龄段开始比较，从而能够解释两个组别间在截距处的差异。为了避免超越所测量的年龄/得分范围，通过从每人的得分（两组中的得分）减去两组最早重叠的实际年龄，来缩放预测变量，使得零点代表两条轨迹最早重叠的时刻（Thomas等人，2009年）。这使零点值代表测量年龄范围的起点，因此，轨迹截距处所测量到的潜在差异（例如，“最早的重叠年龄”或“首次重叠点”）指的是每个预测变量在此零点处的测量结果。对于实际年龄和RMTE得分，这是按照自闭症谱系障碍组中最年轻的年龄缩放的月份数。对于词汇和句法预测变量，考虑到典型发育组的表现略高于自闭症谱系障碍组，该值调整为从典型发育组的最年轻年龄等效分数（按月计）。

为了比较不同实际年龄的发展轨迹，通过将诊断（作为固定因子，代表两组重叠时最年轻年龄的潜在截距差异）以及年龄（从两组重叠的最年轻年龄按月计算）作为协变量来进行ANCOVA分析。该模型还包括对缩放年龄分数与诊断之间交互作用的分析（代表轨迹的斜率，具体测量随年龄增长的发展速度差异；Thomas等人，2009）。因此，不同于群体匹配研究（对比平均值并在年龄上取平均），这种轨迹分析的结果提供了有关自闭症个体与典型发育个体关于年龄的潜在轨迹差异的两项信息。首先，两组之间的早期重叠年龄是否存在显著差异（代表这一轨迹的截距？）；其次，两组间的发展速度是否存在差异（由诊断与缩放年龄变量之间的显著交互来指示？）。尽管两个潜在差异的结果都包含在下面的结果中，但目前研究的主要兴趣在于第二个结果，即发展速度的变化。接下来，为了代替年龄，在模型中重复相同的过程进行词汇、句法和RMTE预测变量的分析。

# Pragmatic language trajectories

Pragmatic language scores from the CASL increased with chronological age, both for TD children, R 2 = .66, F(1,66) = 126.20, p < .001, and children with ASD, R 2 = .32, F(1,23) = 10.72, p < .01. Comparing the groups, the TD children and children with ASD did not significantly differ at the youngest age of overlap between groups (representing no differences in the intercept of the trajectories), p > .05. Children with ASD exhibited a slower rate of development for pragmatic language with chronological age compared to the TD children; interaction of age x group (representing differences in the slope of the trajectories), F(1,89) = 3.90, p < .05, h 2 p ¼ :04. See Fig. 1. Pragmatic language increased with syntax age-equivalence scores, both for TD children, R 2 = .68, F(1,66) = 139.57, p < .001, and children with ASD, R 2 = .70, F(1,23) = 53.21, p < .001. Comparing the groups, the TD children and children with ASD did not significantly differ at the earliest point of overlap in syntax scores between groups, p > .05, and further there was not a significant interaction between syntax abilities and diagnosis, p > .05, suggesting that the groups did not differ in their pragmatic trajectories with regard to syntax. See Fig. 1.
(A) (B) (C) (D)
Pragmatic language raw scores increased with vocabulary age-equivalence scores, both for TD children, R 2 = .72, F(1,64) = 163.32, p < .001, and children with ASD R 2 = .61, F(1,23) = 36.41, p < .001. Comparing the groups, the TD children and children with ASD did not significantly differ at the lowest point of overlap in vocabulary scores between groups, p > .05, and there was not a significant interaction between vocabulary and diagnosis, p > .05, suggesting that the groups did not differ in their pragmatic trajectories with regard to vocabulary abilities. See Fig. 1.
Pragmatic language raw scores increased with TOM scores, both for TD children, R 2 = .32, F(1,66) = 31.43, p < .001, and children with ASD R 2 = .37, F(1,23) = 13.52, p < .001. Comparing the groups, the TD children and children with ASD did not significantly differ at the lowest point of overlap in TOM scores between groups, p > .05, and there was not a significant interaction between TOM and diagnosis, p > .05, suggesting that the groups did not differ in their pragmatic trajectories with regard to TOM abilities. See Fig. 1.

实用语言轨迹

CASL的实用语言评分随实际年龄的增长而增加，对于典型发展（TD）儿童而言，R² = .66，F(1,66) = 126.20，p < .001；对于自闭症谱系障碍（ASD）儿童而言，R² = .32，F(1,23) = 10.72，p < .01。比较两组，在两组重叠的最小年龄下，TD儿童和ASD儿童没有显著差异（表示轨迹截距没有差异），p > .05。与TD儿童相比，ASD儿童的实用语言发展随实际年龄增长的速度较慢；年龄×组交互作用（表示轨迹斜率的差异），F(1,89) = 3.90，p < .05，h²p = .04。见图1。实用语言评分随着句法年龄段分数的增加而上升，对于TD儿童，R² = .68，F(1,66) = 139.57，p < .001；对于ASD儿童，R² = .70，F(1,23) = 53.21，p < .001。比较两组，在句法评分重叠的最初点上，TD儿童和ASD儿童没有显著差异，p > .05，并且句法能力和诊断之间没有显著交互效应，p > .05，表明在句法能力方面，两组在实用性语言轨迹上没有差异。见图1。

(A) (B) (C) (D)

实用语言原始评分随词汇年龄段分数的增加而增加，对于TD儿童，R² = .72，F(1,64) = 163.32，p < .001；同样地对ASD儿童，R² = .61，F(1,23) = 36.41，p < .001。在词汇能力重叠的最低点，TD儿童与ASD儿童没有显著差异，p > .05，且词汇能力和诊断之间也没有显著交互效应，p > .05，表明在词汇能力方面，两组在实质性语言轨迹上没有差异。见图1。

实用语言原始评分随心智理论（ToM）得分提高而增加，对于TD儿童，R² = .32，F(1,66) = 31.43，p < .001；同样对ASD儿童，R² = .37，F(1,23) = 13.52，p < .001。在心智理论得分的最低点，TD儿童与ASD儿童没有显著差异，p > .05，并且心智理论和诊断之间没有显著交互效应，p > .05，表明在心智理论能力方面，两组在实用性语言轨迹上没有差异。见图1。

# Nonliteral language trajectories

Nonliteral language raw scores from the CASL increased with chronological age, both for TD children, R 2 = .70, F(1,66) = 151.46, p < .001, and children with ASD, R 2 = .21, F(1,23) = 6.17, p < .05. Comparing the groups, the TD children and children with ASD did not significantly differ at the youngest age of overlap between groups, p > .05. Children with ASD exhibited a slower rate of development for nonliteral language with chronological age compared to the TD children; interaction of age x group, F(1,89) = 14.06, p < .001, h 2 p ¼ :14. See Fig. 2. Nonliteral language raw scores increased with syntax age-equivalence scores for TD children, R 2 = .69, F(1,66) = 146.41, p < .001, and children with ASD, R 2 = .57, F(1,23) = 29.82, p < .001. Comparing the groups, the TD children and children with ASD did not significantly differ at the lowest point of overlap in syntax scores between groups, p > .05. Children with ASD exhibited a slower rate of development than TD children for nonliteral language with regard to syntax age-equivalence scores, F(1,89) = 3.94, p < .05, h 2 p ¼ :04. See Fig. 2. Nonliteral language raw scores increased with vocabulary age equivalence scores, both for TD children, R 2 = .68, F(1,64) = 133.43, p < .001, and children with ASD, R 2 = .66, F(1,23) = 44.18, p < .001. Comparing the groups, the TD children and children with ASD did not significantly differ at the lowest point of overlap in vocabulary scores between groups, p > .05, and there was not a significant interaction between vocabulary abilities and diagnosis, p > .05, suggesting that the groups did not differ in their nonliteral language trajectories with regard to vocabulary abilities. See Fig. 2. Nonliteral language raw scores increased with TOM scores, both for TD children, R 2 = .44, F(1,66) = 51.70, p < .001, and children with ASD, R 2 = .31, F(1,23) = 10.33, p < .01. Comparing the groups, the TD children and children with ASD did not significantly differ at the lowest point of overlap in TOM scores between groups, p > .05, and there was not a significant interaction between TOM abilities and diagnosis, p > .05, suggesting that the groups did not differ in their nonliteral language trajectories with regard to TOM abilities. See Fig. 2.
(A) (C) (D)

非字面语言的原始分数从CASL随实际年龄增加，无论是对于典型发展（TD）儿童，R² = .70，F(1,66) = 151.46，p < .001，还是对于患有自闭症谱系障碍（ASD）的儿童，R² = .21，F(1,23) = 6.17，p < .05。比较两个群体，在两个群体重叠的最年轻年龄段，TD儿童和ASD儿童之间没有显著差异，p > .05。与TD儿童相比，ASD儿童在非字面语言方面的成长速度较慢；年龄与群体的交互作用，F(1,89) = 14.06，p < .001，偏η² = .14。详见图2。

非字面语言的原始分数随TD儿童的句法年龄等分数增加，R² = .69，F(1,66) = 146.41，p < .001，以及患有ASD的儿童，R² = .57，F(1,23) = 29.82，p < .001。比较两个群体，在句法分数重叠的最低点，TD儿童和ASD儿童之间没有显著差异，p > .05。在句法年龄等分数方面，ASD儿童在非字面语言发展上的增速低于TD儿童，F(1,89) = 3.94，p < .05，偏η² = .04。详见图2。

非字面语言的原始分数随TD儿童的词汇年龄等分数增加，R² = .68，F(1,64) = 133.43，p < .001，以及患有ASD的儿童，R² = .66，F(1,23) = 44.18，p < .001。比较两个群体，在词汇分数重叠的最低点，TD儿童和ASD儿童之间没有显著差异，p > .05，并且词汇能力和诊断之间的交互作用不显著，p > .05，这表明在词汇能力方面，两个群体在非字面语言的发展路径上没有显著差异。详见图2。

非字面语言的原始分数随TD儿童的“心智理论”（TOM）分数增加，R² = .44，F(1,66) = 51.70，p < .001，以及患有ASD的儿童，R² = .31，F(1,23) = 10.33，p < .01。比较两个群体，在TOM分数重叠的最低点，TD儿童和ASD儿童之间没有显著差异，p > .05，并且TOM能力和诊断之间的交互作用不显著，p > .05，这表明在TOM能力方面，两个群体在非字面语言的发展路径上没有显著差异。详见图2。
