# Partial correlations

To further examine the relationship between TOM abilities and each of the two outcome variables, partial correlations (controlling for both vocabulary and syntax age-equivalence scores) were conducted. When controlling for basic language abilities, TOM abilities significantly correlate with pragmatic language scores for TD children, r(61) = .25, p < .05, but not for children with ASD, p > .05. TOM abilities significantly correlate with nonliteral language abilities for TD children, r(61) = .42, p < .01, and for children with ASD, r(20) = .37, p < .05.

为了进一步探讨心智理论（TOM）能力与两个结果变量之间的关系，在控制词汇量和语法年龄等值分数的情况下，进行了部分相关分析。当控制基本语言能力时，TOM 能力与典型发展（TD）儿童的实用语言得分显著相关，r(61) = .25, p < .05，但与 ASD 儿童的相关不显著，p > .05。TOM 能力与 TD 儿童的非字面语言能力显著相关，r(61) = .42, p < .01，并且与 ASD 儿童的非字面语言能力也显著相关，r(20) = .37, p < .05。

# Discussion

The current study used a cross-sectional trajectory approach, following the methods of Thomas et al. (2009), to examine the development of pragmatic language and nonliteral language (metaphor, sarcasm, indirect requests) for children with ASD and TD children. For both TD children and children with ASD, ages 5-12 years, chronological age, basic language abilities (syntax and vocabulary), and TOM abilities, were significantly predictive of raw scores on both the pragmatic language and nonliteral language subtests of the CASL. Older children with ASD had higher numbers of correct responses on the pragmatic language and nonliteral language subtests of the CASL than younger children with ASD. In addition, children with ASD who had higher vocabulary or syntax age-equivalence scores performed better on nonliteral language and pragmatic language measures than children with ASD who had lower vocabulary or syntax scores.
For the trajectory analysis, as predicted, no analysis showed significant differences for the youngest age of overlap between groups (representing the intercept of the trajectory), or for the lowest overlap in either vocabulary or syntax scores. This was largely due to the low scores of the TD group at the youngest ages (e.g., 5 years) on the particular measures used in this study, and this age range (5-12 years) was chosen to be able to specifically focus on the rate of development for these outcome variables. The current results suggest that while the children with ASD showed a slower rate of development of both pragmatic language and nonliteral language compared to TD children with regard to age, the rate of development for the groups did not significantly differ when accounting for vocabulary abilities or TOM abilities. Similarly, the rate of development did not significantly differ for pragmatic language abilities when accounting for syntax abilities. However, for the nonliteral language measure, when accounting for syntax abilities, children with ASD did show a significantly slower rate of development than TD children.

本研究采用截面轨迹方法，遵循Thomas等（2009年）的研究方法，考察了自闭症谱系障碍（ASD）儿童和普通发展（TD）儿童在实用语言和非字面语言（如隐喻、讽刺、间接请求）方面的发展情况。对于TD儿童和ASD儿童（年龄在5至12岁之间），实证年龄、基础语言能力（语法和词汇）以及心智理论（TOM）能力，都是预测CASL的实用语言和非字面语言子测试原始分数的重要因素。与较年轻的ASD儿童相比，ASD儿童中年龄较大的孩子在CASL的实用语言和非字面语言子测试上的正确答案数量更高。此外，ASD儿童中词汇量或语法匹配分数较高的孩子，在非字面语言和实用语言的评分上表现得比词汇量或语法匹配分数较低的孩子更好。

对于轨迹分析，正如预期的那样，没有分析显示组间重叠最小年龄（代表轨迹的截距）或最低词汇或语法得分中有显著差异。这主要是因为，研究中使用的特定测试在最年轻年龄组（例如，5岁）时，TD组的得分普遍较低。选择这个年龄范围（5-12岁），是为了能够特别关注这些结果变量的发展速度。目前的结果表明，虽然与TD儿童相比，ASD儿童在实用语言和非字面语言方面的发展速度更慢，但当考虑到词汇能力或TOM能力时，不同群体之间的这种发展速度差异并不显著。同样地，当考虑到语法能力时，实用语言能力的发展速度差异也不显著。然而，当考虑到语法能力时，ASD儿童在非字面语言方面的平均发展速度显著慢于TD儿童。

# Pragmatic language development

The current study found that syntax abilities (as measured by the syntax construction subtest of the CASL) and vocabulary abilities (receptive vocabulary and riddles subtest of the KBIT-2) were both strong predictors of pragmatic language (as measured by the pragmatic language subtest of the CASL) in children with ASD and TD children. The results of the current study are consistent with prior research studies suggesting that basic language abilities can predict current performance on pragmatic language abilities in children with ASD (Volden et al., 2009). For example, Volden et al. (2009) found that a combination of expressive and receptive basic language abilities significantly predicted pragmatic language abilities in children, ages 6-13 years, with ASD. The results for age suggested that there was not a significant difference at the youngest age of overlap between the two groups, but that the slopes of the trajectories (measuring rate of development with age) were significantly different. The current study adds to the literature with the finding that pragmatic language abilities show a slower rate of development with age for children with ASD, compared to TD children, but the rate of development did not differ between groups with regard to either vocabulary or syntax abilities. This suggests that individuals with ASD show similar trajectories for pragmatic abilities when accounting for their basic language abilities, supporting theories of pragmatic language development that emphasize the important foundation of basic language abilities for individuals with ASD. Additionally, pragmatic language abilities were higher for both children with ASD and TD when they had higher TOM abilities (with no significant difference between groups in the intercept and slope of the trajectories). However, when controlling for basic language abilities, TOM was only related to pragmatic language for the TD group and not the children with ASD. This TOM task measures the understanding of complex mental states (based on labeling the expressions of the eye regions of faces). The results provide some positive evidence for the conclusion that theory of mind abilities potentially contribute to the development of pragmatic language abilities, particularly for TD children.

本研究发现，语言的句法能力（通过CASL的句法构造子测试衡量）和词汇能力（KBIT-2的接受性词汇和谜语子测试）都是自闭症儿童（ASD儿童）和普通发展儿童（TD儿童）在实用语言能力（通过CASL的实用语言子测试衡量）方面的重要预测因素。当前研究的结果与之前的多项研究表明基本语言能力可以预测自闭症儿童在实用语言能力方面的当前表现的研究结果一致（Volden等人，2009）。例如，Volden等人（2009）发现，6至13岁自闭症儿童的表达性和接受性基本语言能力的结合显著地预示了他们的实用语言能力。

年龄因素的结果表明，在两个组别最年轻交集年龄段没有显著差异，但是在随年龄增长的发展速度上（即发展轨迹的斜率）有显著差异。本研究进一步指出，与普通发展儿童相比，自闭症儿童在年龄增长时实用语言能力的发展速度较慢，但就词汇或句法能力而言，两组儿童在发展速度上并无显著差异。这表明当考虑到自闭症个体的基本语言能力时，他们在实用语言能力方面的轨迹是相似的，这也支持了强调基本语言能力对于自闭症个体实用语言发展重要性的理论。

此外，无论是自闭症儿童还是普通发展儿童，其理论理解能力（TOM）越高，其实用语言能力也越高（并且两组间的截距和斜率无显著差异）。然而，当控制了基本语言能力后，TOM仅与普通发展儿童的实用语言能力相关，而非自闭症儿童。这项TOM任务测量的是对复杂心理状态的理解（基于对面部眼睛区域表情的标注）。这些结果为结论提供了部分正面证据，即理论理解能力可能对实用语言能力的发展有所贡献，尤其是在普通发展儿童中。

# Nonliteral language development

Nonliteral language abilities showed significant increases with age and both measures of basic language abilities for children with ASD and TD children. When examining the trajectory for chronological age, there was no difference between the groups at the youngest age of overlap, but children with ASD showed a slower rate of development with increasing age. A benefit of the trajectory analysis in the current study was that separately including vocabulary or syntax as predictors allowed for revealing how these two aspects of basic language show mostly similar, but also certain different relations, with aspects of nonliteral language development. For the syntax predictor, children with ASD showed a slightly but significantly slower rate of development compared to the TD group for nonliteral language. In contrast, the rate of development for nonliteral language abilities was not significantly different between children with ASD and TD in relation to their vocabulary abilities.
The results of the current study are not consistent, however, with one previous study of nonliteral language using a similar cross-sectional developmental trajectory analysis. Rundblad and Annaz (2010b) found that the children with ASD did not show a significant relation between either predictor variable (age or receptive vocabulary) and metaphor performance, with many of the children with ASD scoring zero out of 10 possible points on metaphor comprehension. Additionally, the children with ASD did not show increases in metonym comprehension with chronological age, though metonym scores did increase with vocabulary. Especially given that Rundblad and Annaz (2010b) found different patterns in their trajectory analysis between their two measures of nonliteral language, it is likely that different measures of nonliteral language may show different trajectory results. For the current study, the use of developmentally sensitive measures (e.g., inclusion of a mix of easy and hard items in the CASL measure) and a larger sample of individuals with ASD provided evidence that children with ASD are able to learn nonliteral language, that knowledge of nonliteral language increases with age, and that their nonliteral language development is largely in line with their combined receptive and expressive vocabulary developmental levels. The vocabulary measure used in the current study included verbal comprehension abilities (e.g., answering questions, such as ‘’what hops, eats carrots, and has long ears?’’) in addition to receptive vocabulary abilities, which differs from the more traditional receptive vocabulary measure used in previous studies (e.g., Rundblad & Annaz, 2010b). Thus, the choice of language variables is likely to impact the results.
The present results suggest that when particular children with ASD have managed to achieve significant receptive and expressive vocabulary skills, these skills will dynamically play into greater successes in acquiring new levels of nonliteral language, in a fashion similar to the dynamic supports in TD provided by advancing vocabulary abilities. However, children with ASD did show slower rates of development in their nonliteral language abilities when considering scores on syntax (although syntax was still a significant predictor of nonliteral language scores), which does not directly support the hypothesis of Gernsbacher and Pripas-Kapit (2012). Instead, a combination of basic language skills and TOM abilities may play a role in the development of nonliteral language comprehension. Scores on the RMTE task also showed significant relations to nonliteral language in both the trajectory analysis and the partial correlation analysis. TOM abilities predicted nonliteral language performance for both TD children and children with ASD (with no group difference in the intercept or slopes of the trajectory analysis). The correlation between TOM abilities and nonliteral language remained significant even after controlling for basic language abilities. The current study supports the hypothesis that nonliteral language skills are related to both basic language and TOM abilities.

非字面语言能力的发展章节

非字面语言能力在自闭症谱系障碍（ASD）儿童和典型发展（TD）儿童的基本语言能力上都表现出显著的年龄增长。当考察按照实际年龄的轨迹时，在年龄最早的重叠阶段，两组之间没有差异，但随着年龄的增长，ASD儿童的发展速度较慢。本研究中轨迹分析的一个优点是，将词汇或句法分别作为预测变量，这使得我们能够揭示这两个基本语言方面与非字面语言发展的大多数相似关系，但也显示出某些不同的关系。对于句法预测变量，ASD儿童与TD儿童相比，在非字面语言发展上显示出稍微但显著更慢的发展速度。相反，从词汇能力的角度来看，ASD儿童与TD儿童的非字面语言能力发展速度没有显著差异。

然而，本研究的结果并不支持一项使用类似横断式发展阶段分析的先前关于非字面语言的研究。Rundblad 和 Annaz (2010b) 发现，ASD 儿童在两个预测变量（年龄或接受性词汇）与隐喻表现之间没有显著的关系，许多 ASD 儿童在隐喻理解上的得分是 10 分中的零分。此外，ASD 儿童在年龄增长的情况下，并没有表现出对提喻理解的增加，尽管提喻评分随着词汇量的增长而增加。特别是鉴于 Rundblad 和 Annaz (2010b) 在他们的轨迹分析中发现了两种非字面语言测量之间的不同模式，可能不同的非字面语言测量会呈现出不同的轨迹结果。本研究使用了具有发展阶段敏感性的测量（例如，在CASL测量中包含了一定数量的简单和困难项目），并采用更大的ASD患者样本提供证据表明，ASD儿童能够学习非字面语言，知道这种语言随着年龄的增长而增加，并且他们的非字面语言发展主要与他们结合的接受性和表达性词汇发展水平一致。本研究中使用的词汇测量除了包括接受性词汇能力外，还涵盖了言语理解能力（例如，回答问题，“什么东西跳，吃胡萝卜，有长耳朵？”），这不同于以往研究中使用的传统接受性词汇测量（例如，Rundblad & Annaz, 2010b）。因此，所选择的语言变量很可能会对结果产生影响。

当前的结果表明，当特定的ASD儿童掌握了显著的接受性和表达性词汇技能时，这些技能将以类似于动态支持TD儿童词汇逐渐进步的方式，促进他们在掌握非字面语言新层次上的更大成功。然而，考虑到句法规则得分后，ASD儿童的非字面语言能力发展速度确实更慢（尽管句法仍然是非字面语言成绩的重要预测因子），这并不能直接支持Gernsbacher和Pripas-Kapit（2012）的假设。相反，基本语言技能和心智理论（TOM）能力的组合可能在非字面语言理解的发展中起到作用。RMTE任务得分也在轨迹分析和部分相关分析中显著地反映了非字面语言的关系。TOM能力预测了TD儿童和ASD儿童的非字面语言表现（轨迹分析的截距或斜率没有组间差异）。即使控制了基本语言能力后，TOM能力和非字面语言之间的相关性仍然是显著的。本研究支持了非字面语言技能与基本语言和TOM能力相关的假设。

# Limitations and future directions

The sample in the current study was comprised of high functioning and verbal individuals with ASD (diagnosed with autism, Asgerger’s syndrome, or PDD-NOS). Therefore, it is possible that the results may not generalize to lower functioning individuals with ASD. Additionally, current scores on diagnostic observational measures, such as the Autism Diagnostic Observation Scale (ADOS; Lord, Rutter, DiLavore, & Risi, 1999) were not available for the participants with ASD in the current study. Future research should include, when feasible, ADOS testing scores for participants. It is important to note that nonliteral language skills have been shown to not correlate strongly with measures of autistic social symptoms (Norbury, 2004(Norbury, , 2005;;Rundblad & Annaz, 2010a, 2010b), and both children with a diagnosis of autism or a diagnosis of Asperger’s syndrome showed difficulties with metaphor comprehension in previous research. Thus, differences in diagnostic inclusion criteria would be unlikely to impact the results of the present research.
It may, however, be possible to see different results when measuring receptive skills through procedures that do not require complex language production. Future research should use additional measures of syntax, nonliteral, and pragmatic aspects of language to see if the present results replicate across different measures of language development. Group matching designs, in particular, should be sensitive to how variability in the choices of matching variables may lead to different conclusions about the nature of language abilities for children with ASD (e.g., Norbury, 2005;Whyte et al., 2014).
Future research should include longitudinal designs to examine how various aspects of nonliteral and pragmatic language develop over time within individual children. While the cross-sectional trajectories are a helpful tool for examining trends across groups of people, it is likely that sub-groups of individuals with ASD will show different patterns of language development over time. The cross-sectional trajectories, however, can help with informing longitudinal study designs by suggesting measures that are likely to show development across target age ranges. The current study suggests that the CASL may be developmentally sensitive measures for examining pragmatic and nonliteral language abilities for children with ASD, and that the KBIT-2 composite of expressive and receptive vocabulary abilities may be an important predictor of success on figurative and pragmatic language abilities.

限制与未来研究方向

当前研究的样本包括了高功能及语言能力良好的自闭症谱系障碍（ASD）个体（被诊断为自闭症、阿斯伯格综合征或广泛性发育障碍未特定型[PDD-NOS]）。因此，结果可能不适用于功能较低的ASD个体。此外，目前研究中ASD参与者的诊断观察评分（如《自闭症诊断观察量表》[ADOS；Lord、Rutter、DiLavore和Risi，1999年]）不可用。未来的研究应尽可能包括参与者的ADOS测试成绩。值得注意的是，非字面语言技能并未与自闭症社交症状的测量值显示出强烈的关联（Norbury, 2004, 2005; Rundblad & Annaz, 2010a, 2010b），并且之前的研究显示，患有自闭症诊断或阿斯伯格综合征诊断的儿童在理解隐喻方面存在困难。因此，诊断纳入标准的不同不太可能影响当前研究的结果。

然而，当使用不需要复杂语言生成的程序来测量接收技能时，可能会得到不同的结果。未来的研究应使用语言发展的句法、非字面及语用方面的额外测量指标，以验证当前结果是否会跨不同语言发展指标重复出现。特别是匹配设计应该对选择匹配变量的变化敏感，这可能会导致关于ASD儿童语言能力本质的不同结论（例如，Norbury, 2005; Whyte 等人, 2014）。

未来的研究应包括纵向设计，以考察在单个儿童中非字面和语用语言的不同方面随时间的发展情况。虽然交叉轨迹是一个有用的工具，可以观察不同人群的趋势，但很可能是ASD的亚组会随着时间表现出不同的语言发展模式。然而，交叉轨迹可以帮助告知纵向研究的设计，通过建议在目标年龄段内可能显示出发展的衡量标准。当前研究表明，CASL可能是用于检查ASD儿童语用和非字面语言能力的发展敏感指标，而KBIT-2对表达性和接收性词汇能力的综合评估可能是成功掌握比喻和语用语言技能的重要预测因素。

# Conclusions

The current study examined cross-sectional developmental trajectories for both pragmatic language (understanding contextually appropriate language) and nonliteral language subtests of the CASL (comprised of figurative language, sarcasm, and indirect requests). The children with ASD (ages 5-12 years) showed a slower rate of development for both pragmatic language and nonliteral language with chronological age. However, both chronological age and basic language age-equivalence scores significantly predicted performance on nonliteral and pragmatic language for the children with ASD, as well as for children with TD. The present results provide a strong challenge to prior suggestions (e.g., Loukusa & Moilanen, 2009) that pragmatic and/or nonliteral language skills represent particularly difficult domains for children with ASD, above and beyond basic language difficulties. Instead, the pragmatic trajectories for children with ASD and TD children did not significantly differ when accounting for either vocabulary or syntax abilities. In like fashion, for nonliteral language abilities, developmental trajectories for the TD and ASD did not significantly differ when accounting for vocabulary abilities, though the children with ASD did show slower rates of development for nonliteral language when accounting for syntax abilities.
Although the children with ASD may reach vocabulary and syntax benchmarks more slowly than the typically developing children, for any given level of vocabulary or syntax the children with ASD appear to have dynamically applied their basic language skills with similar effectiveness as TD children to the mastery of new levels of pragmatic language and to nonliteral language. These results give new emphasis to the previously tentative conclusion that when children with ASD are able to improve their basic language skills then it is highly likely that the children will also make improvements in pragmatic language and in use of other nonliteral language expressions. Additionally, a combination of basic language abilities, as well as advanced TOM abilities, may aid in the understanding of both pragmatic language and nonliteral language. Thus, when a child is in the progress of newly sorting out multiple relations between a pragmatic linguistic expression and different contexts (or between literal versus nonliteral meanings), these new mappings will be more richly supported as both the basic language abilities and TOM abilities of the child improve. Understanding predictors of individual differences both in the present study and in future longitudinal research can aid the selection of individualized intervention targets in multiple domains of language, including pragmatic language and nonliteral language abilities (Nelson, 2001;Nelson, Welsh, Camarata, Heimann, & Tjus, 2001;Whyte, Nelson, & Khan, 2013). Further, the results of the current study should provide encouragement to future innovations in language therapies and interventions that would aim to jointly facilitate complex syntax growth for individuals with ASD and growth in aspects of pragmatic or nonliteral language.

  1. According to past research, typically developing children as young as _____ are able to demonstrate some basic knowledge of nonliteral language. a. 2 to 3 years b. 4 to 6 years c. 7 to 8 years d. 9 to 11 years 2. Differences between group matching designs and the cross-sectional developmental trajectory analysis include: a. Longitudinal data b. The need for a priori group matching c. Cross-sectional data d. Information about group differences in the rate of development e. Both B and D 3. The results for the pragmatic language outcome measure suggests that compared to typically developing children, children with autism spectrum disorders (ASD) show: a. Delays in the onset of pragmatic language with regards to chronological age b. Delays in the rate of pragmatic language with regards to chronological age c. Delays in the rate of pragmatic language with regards to syntax abilities d. Delays in the rate of pragmatic language with regards to vocabulary abilities 4. True or false: The current study found that children with ASD who had higher vocabulary abilities performed better on nonliteral language than children with ASD who had lower vocabulary abilities.
  2. For typically developing children, figurative and pragmatic language abilities are significantly predicted by: a. Age b. Vocabulary abilities c. Syntax abilities d. Theory of mind e. All of the above

结论

本研究考察了学龄前至学龄儿童（5-12岁）在语用语言和非字面语言子测试方面的发展轨迹。语用语言指的是理解语境上恰当的语言；非字面语言则包括隐喻性语言、讽刺性语言及间接请求。患有自闭症谱系障碍（ASD）的儿童在年龄增长的同时表现出在语用语言和非字面语言方面发展速度较慢的现象。然而，无论是以年龄还是基础语言的年龄当量分数来衡量，这些因素对于患有ASD的儿童以及正常发展的（TD）儿童而言，在预测他们在语用语言及非字面语言上的表现时都具有显著预测力。这一结果强烈挑战了先前的观点（例如：Loukusa和Moilanen于2009年提出的观点），即对于患有ASD的儿童而言，语用语言和/或非字面语言技能代表了特别困难的语言领域，这种困难不仅仅限于基本语言能力方面的难题。相反，当考虑到词汇或语法能力时，患有ASD的儿童与正常发展的儿童在语用语言方面的发展轨迹没有显著差异。同样地，在考虑到词汇能力的情况下，正常发展儿童与ASD儿童在非字面语言能力方面的发展轨迹也没有显著差异。尽管ASD儿童可能比正常的儿童更慢达到词汇和语法的标准，但在给定水平的词汇或语法条件下，ASD儿童似乎已经有效地、相似有效地运用其基本语言技能去掌握新的、更复杂的语用语言和隐喻性语言表达。这些结果为先前关于ASD儿童可以通过改进基本语言技能而提高他们在语用语言和隐喻性语言等非字面语言表达能力的谨慎推论提供了强有力的支持。此外，基本语言能力和高级心智理论（TOM）能力结合可能会有助于理解和应用语用语言和非字面语言。因此，当儿童在将语用语言表达与不同情境（或字面意义与非字面意义之间的区分）联系起来时，在这两种能力不断提高的前提下，这种新的关联会得到更丰富的支持。进一步理解个别差异的预测因素，在当前研究及未来的纵向研究中都将有助于多个语言领域的个体化干预目标的选择，包括语用语言和非字面语言能力。因此，本研究的结果应该为未来开发旨在促进ASD个体复杂句法的成长并提升其在语用或隐喻性语言方面的成长的疗法与干预措施提供鼓励。

小测验答案：

  1. a. 2至3岁
  2. e. 选项B（事先群体匹配的需求）、和 D（关于发展速度群体差异的信息）
  3. b. 按照生理年龄计算时，ASD儿童在语用语言上发展的速度较慢。
  4. 真。本研究表明，拥有较高词汇能力的ASD儿童相比拥有较低词汇能力的ASD儿童，在非字面语言方面表现更好。
  5. e. 以上全部（年龄、词汇能力、句法能力及心智理论）。

原文[0/18]：

Department of Linguistics Department of Psychology University of Essex University of Essex Addresses for Correspondence: Harald Clahsen Christine Temple Department of Linguistics Department of Psychology University of Essex University of Essex Colchester, C04 3SQ, UK Colchester, C04 3SQ, UK Tel: +44/1206/87-2228 Tel: +44/1206/87-3589 email: harald@essex.ac.uk tempc@essex.ac.uk *To appear in: Yonata Levy & Jeannette Schaeffer (Eds.), Towards a definition of SpecificLanguage Impairment in children. Kluwer.

February 2001 2

1 Introduction Williams syndrome [WS] is a genetic disorder associated with learning difficulties, with an incidence of 1 in 25,000 (Greenberg, 1990). It is caused by a microdeletion on the long arm of chromosome 7 at 7q11.23, which affects one allele of the elastin gene and other contiguous genes (Ewart et al., 1993; Tassabehji et al., 1996; Frangiskakis et al., 1996). Within cognitive skills, there is a spatial disorder, for example in drawing and relative strength in language. The development of language is also uneven but there is dispute about the actual performance on language tasks and the best theoreticalinterpretation of this performance.

In two previous studies investigating morpho-syntactic skills in subjects with WS, Clahsen and Almazan (1998, 2001) found that the subjects with WS do not show any syntactic impairment, and that they perform excellently on regular past tense and regular plural inflection. On the other hand, their scores on irregular past tense and irregular plural forms were found to be lower than those of unimpaired mental age controls. Moreover, the subjects with WS were seen to use regular rules of inflection excessively, even in circumstances in which unimpaired children (and adults) would not use them. Clahsen and Almazan proposed an account of this unusual pattern of morpho-syntactic skills, in terms of a modular view of the language faculty in which the knowledge of language is assumed to consist of two separate components, a lexicon of stored entries and a computational system of combinatorial operations to form larger linguistic expressions (e.g. Chomsky 1995, Pinker 1999). They argued that in WS, these two core modules of language are dissociated such that the computational (rule-based) system for language is selectively spared, while lexicalrepresentations and/or their access procedures are impaired.

Recently, however, this account of WS has been challenged, and an alternative non-modular connectionist model has been proposed to explain the performance of subjects with WS (Thomas & Karmiloff-Smith 1999, Thomas et al. 1999). According to this neuro-constructivist approach, the linguistic performance of a subject with WS is argued to reflect shifted constraints in the representation and development of language, whereby there is more weight on phonological information and less on semantic information. More specifically, subjects with WS are claimed to have ‘overly rich phonological representations’ which prevent them from learning the past tense

3

properly and from generalizing inflectional patterns to novel items. The present study criticises the proposals of Thomas and Karmiloff-Smith (1999) and Thomas et al. (1999). It then provides evidence from three sources on the linguistic skills of subjects with WS that bears on this controversy. Results will be presented on the use of comparative adjectives in WS, receptive and productive vocabularies and their reading and writing skills. It is argued that the new findings provide further support for the hypothesis of a selective lexical deficit in WS, which does not require a connectionist interpretation, and has task specificity, which is problematic forsuch accounts.

  • 将发表于：Yonata Levy & Jeannette Schaeffer (编)，《儿童特定语言障碍的定义》。Kluwer。

2001年2月

引言

威廉姆斯综合征 [WS] 是一种与学习困难相关的遗传性疾病，其发生率为二十五万分之一（Greenberg, 1990）。该病由7号染色体长臂上的7q11.23微缺失引起，影响了一个弹力蛋白基因等位基因及其他相邻基因（Ewart et al., 1993; Tassabehji et al., 1996; Frangiskakis et al., 1996）。在认知技能方面，威廉姆斯综合征患者具有空间处理障碍，例如在绘图方面，而在语言方面则表现相对较强。尽管语言发展也不均衡，但对其在语言任务中的实际表现及其最佳理论解释仍存在争议。

在之前的两项研究中，Clahsen 和 Almazan (1998, 2001) 发现，WS 患者没有表现出任何句法障碍，并且他们在规则过去时和规则复数词形变化上表现优异。然而，他们在不规则过去时和不规则复数形式上的得分低于正常智力年龄对照组。此外，WS 患者在那些正常儿童（及成人）不会使用规则的情况下，过度使用了规则变化。Clahsen 和 Almazan 提出了一种解释这种非常规的形态句法能力模式的理论，即从模块化的语言功能观点出发，假设语言知识由两个独立的部分组成：存储词汇表和用于形成更复杂的语言表达式的组合运算系统（如 Chomsky, 1995; Pinker, 1999）。他们认为，在 WS 患者中，这两个核心的语言模块是分离的，使得基于规则的语言计算系统选择性地保留完好，而词汇表示及其访问程序则受损。

然而，近来对这一关于 WS 的解释提出了挑战，并提出了一种替代性的非模块化联结主义模型来解释 WS 患者的语言表现（Thomas & Karmiloff-Smith 1999, Thomas et al. 1999）。根据这种神经构建主义方法，WS 患者的语言表现反映了语言表征和发展过程中约束条件的转移，其中语音信息权重较大，语义信息权重较小。具体而言，据称 WS 患者具有“过于丰富的语音表征”，这妨碍了他们正确学习过去时态并将其推广到新项目。本研究批评了 Thomas 和 Karmiloff-Smith (1999) 以及 Thomas 等人 (1999) 的提议，并提供了来自三个来源的证据，针对 WS 患者的语言能力对此争议进行了探讨。将展示结果包括 WS 患者对比较级形容词的使用、接受性和产生性词汇量以及他们的阅读和写作技能。本文认为，这些新的发现进一步支持了 WS 中选择性词汇缺陷的假设，该假设不需要联结主义的解释，并且具有任务特异性，这对这类解释构成了挑战。

原文[1/18]：

2 Impaired phonological representations in WS? Thomas and Karmiloff-Smith (Thomas and Karmiloff-Smith 1999, Thomas et al. 1999) argue that subjects with WS differ from unimpaired children and adults in their phonological representation system. The idea is that the language of subjects with WS develops under a different set of constraints from normal child language development and that subjects with WS place ‘more weight on phonological information and less weight on semantic information’ (Thomas et al. 1999: 40). This idea has been implemented in a connectionist network for past-tense formation in which the phonological input representations are overspecified in a way such that the network is unable to detect similarities between different phonological representations. In other words, phonological representations in subjects with WS are said to be ‘overly-detailed’ and more specific than those of unimpaired children. Thomas et al. (1999) argue that this difference explains why WS children perform worse on irregular past-tense formation than unimpaired controls; this is presumably because the stem and past-tense forms of irregular verbs tend to be phonologically more different from each other than those of regular verbs (compare teach – taught vs. walk – walked). Overly detailed phonological representations are also said to explain why the WS group produced significantly fewer irregularizations, i.e. overapplications of irregular past-tense forms, than typically developing children (p.30); in Thomas & Karmiloff-Smith’s account this is because the overspecified phonological representations of existing past-tense forms in WS prevent associative generalizations to new items. They stress that ‘the apparent deficit in irregular past tense formation

4

is …a consequence of delayed language development (p.45) and that their linguistic behaviourresults from an initial phonological deficit” (p.44).

In broad terms, the empirical findings on past-tense formation in WS from Thomas et al. (1999) are similar to those reported in Clahsen and Almazan (1998). In both studies, the subjects with WS were seen to perform worse on irregulars than unimpaired children and to rarely produce overapplications of irregular inflection. The discussion here will focus on their hypotheses ofdelayed language development and a phonological deficit in WS.

Consider first the hypothesized delay of language development in WS. In some important respects, the subjects with WS studied by Thomas et al. (1999) perform worse when they get older. This is evident from their Fig.4, which shows that both in terms of chronological and verbal mental age, the older subjects with WS produce more –ed overregularizations to nonce words that rhyme with existing irregular verbs than the younger ones. The opposite pattern is found from the unimpaired controls: the older they get, the less often they add –ed to rhyming irregulars. This difference is hard to reconcile with the view that the linguistic profile of subjects with WS simply represents adelay of normal language development.

Another challenge for the delay hypothesis comes from the results of a recent study of plural formation and compounding (Clahsen & Almazan 2001). Results from three experiments showed that the subjects with WS excessively overapplied the regular plural –s, even in circumstances in which typically developing children hardly ever use –s plurals, namely as non-head elements inside compounds. In contrast to unimpaired controls, the subjects with WS maintained regular -s plurals inside compounds, producing ungrammatical derived compounds such as *rats-eater as well as many ungrammatical root compounds with regular -s plurals as non-head elements, *foots cake, *gooses fax, etc. In an additional comprehension experiment, the children with WS were found frequently to misinterpret compounds like red rats eater as the eater being red rather than the victims. This indicated that in contrast to unimpaired children, the presence of a regular plural did not have any effect on the interpretation of the compound by children with WS. The results from these three experiments show that in subjects with WS regular plurals can occur freely inside compounds. This is different from adult English as well as from early child language. Gordon

  1. 威廉姆斯综合症（Williams Syndrome, WS）中的受损音韵表征？托马斯和卡尔米洛夫-史密斯（Thomas and Karmiloff-Smith 1999，Thomas et al. 1999）认为，患有威廉姆斯综合症的受试者与其无受损儿童和成人在音韵表征系统上存在差异。他们的观点是，WS患者的语言发展在不同的一组约束下进行，而不是像正常儿童的语言发展那样，并且WS患者“更重视音韵信息而较少依赖语义信息”（Thomas et al. 1999: 40）。这一想法在一个连接主义网络中得到了实现，该网络用于过去时态的形成，其中音韵输入表征被过度指定，从而使网络无法检测到不同音韵表征之间的相似性。换言之，WS患者中的音韵表征据说比未受损儿童的更加“过度详细”和具体。托马斯等人（1999）认为，这种差异解释了为什么WS儿童在不规则过去时态的形成方面表现得比无受损对照组差；这可能是由于不规则动词的词干和过去时态形式在音韵上比规则动词的差异更大（比较teach – taught与walk – walked）。过于详细的音韵表征还被认为解释了为什么WS组产生的不规则化现象（即不规则过去时态形式的过度应用）显著少于典型发育的儿童（p.30）；根据托马斯和卡尔米洛夫-史密斯的观点，这是因为现有的过去时态形式在WS中的过度指定音韵表征阻止了对新项的联想泛化。他们强调，“不规则过去时态形成的明显缺陷……是语言发展延迟的结果（p.45），并且他们的语言行为是由最初的音韵缺陷引起的”（p.44）。

广义上说，托马斯等人（1999）关于WS中过去时态形成的研究结果与克拉森和阿尔马赞（Clahsen and Almazan 1998）报告的结果类似。在这两项研究中，WS受试者在不规则形式上的表现比无受损儿童差，并且很少产生不规则屈折的过度应用。此处将重点讨论他们关于WS中语言发展延迟和音韵缺陷的假设。

首先考虑WS中存在的语言发展延迟假设。在一些重要方面，托马斯等人（1999）研究的WS受试者随着年龄增长表现更差。这一点从图4中可以看出，无论是按实际年龄还是言语心理年龄计算，年纪较大的WS受试者对那些听起来像是现有不规则动词的新造词添加-ed形式的频率高于年轻的WS受试者。相反地，无受损对照组的情况则是：年龄越大，对听起来像不规则动词的新造词添加-ed形式的频率越低。这种差异难以与WS受试者的语言特征仅仅是正常语言发展延迟的观点相一致。

对该延迟假说的另一个挑战来自于最近一项关于复数形成和复合词的研究（Clahsen & Almazan 2001）。三项实验的结果表明，WS受试者过度使用规则复数-s，即使在典型发育的儿童几乎不会使用-s复数的情况下也是如此，即在复合词中作为非主词成分。与无受损对照组相比，WS受试者在复合词中仍然保留规则-s复数，产生了诸如rats-eater这样的不合语法的派生复合词以及许多包含规则-s复数作为非主词成分的不合语法的基本复合词，例如foots cake, *gooses fax等。在额外的理解实验中，发现WS儿童经常误解red rats eater这样的复合词，将其解释为eater是红色的而不是其对象是红色的。这表明，在WS儿童中，规则复数的存在对复合词的解释没有任何影响。这三项实验的结果显示，在WS受试者中，规则复数能够在复合词中自由出现。这与成人英语和早期儿童语言有所不同。 Gordon

原文[2/18]：

(1985) and Alegre & Gordon (1995) found that even the youngest children in their samples, i.e. the 3-year olds, were sensitive to the difference between regular and irregular plurals inside compounds. Clahsen et al. (1992, 1996) replicated Gordon’s results for German child language. All age groups of unimpaired children in the Clahsen et al. studies produced irregular plurals inside compounds and avoided regular plurals. Hence the pattern of plurals inside compounds observed in WS does not correspond to any developmental stage found in unimpaired children. These results cast doubt on Thomas & Karmiloff-Smith’s (1999) delay hypothesis. Consider next the hypothesized phonological deficit in WS, which is proposed to explain why for existing verbs WS children perform worse on irregulars than on regulars and why on nonce verbs they generalize less than unimpaired controls. A difficulty for this account concerns observed differences between overapplication of regular and irregular patterns in the WS data. Thomas et al. (1999) did not directly compare these kinds of overapplications but they observed that the WS group produced significantly fewer irregularizations than typically developing children. Clahsen & Almazan (1998) compared overapplications of regular and irregular past-tense forms directly. They found that subjects with WS heavily overapplied the regular past tense -ed, whereas irregularizations were extremely rare. The -ed affix was (incorrectly) supplied by the subjects with WS to 38% of the existing irregular verbs tested (as opposed to 13% for the unimpaired controls), and to 65% of the nonce verbs that rhymed only with existing irregular verbs (compared to 19% for the unimpaired children), while irregularizations occurred in less than 10%. Similar results were obtained for noun plurals (Clahsen & Almazan 2001). The subjects with WS heavily overapplied the regular plural affix, with rates twice as high as those of unimpaired control children, while irregular patterns were not overapplied. This is also confirmed by the results of a recent study with German-speaking subjects with WS (Krause & Penke 2000). It was found that the subjects with WS overregularized the regular -t participle, even to high-frequency irregular verbs, an error that did not occur in the control data. They also found that, in contrast to the unimpaired controls, overapplications of irregular plural patterns were almost non-existent in the WS data. These findings replicate those on English indicating that inflectional rules may be

6

excessively used in subjects with WS. From Thomas & Karmiloff-Smith’s phonological deficit account, one would expect that subjects with WS would be impaired in generalizing all kinds of inflectional patterns, because their phonological representations are overly detailed. The finding, however, that subjects with WS seem to be more willing to overextend regular inflectional patterns than irregular ones is leftunexplained.

It is also difficult to see how the phonological deficit hypothesis might account for the incorrect compound formations with regular plurals as non-head elements (e.g. *rats-eater) made by subjects with WS. These kinds of error do not result from any difficulty with irregular inflection or an impairment in generalizing to nonce words. The two competing forms (e.g. rat and rats) are both existing word forms, and even if subjects with WS had ‘overly detailed phonological representations’, this would not explain why children with WS frequently use the plural form inside compounds, whereas typically developing children almost always use the singular form. From a morphological perspective, however, the behaviour of the subjects with WS in compounding fits in with their frequent overapplications of the regular past tense –ed and the regular plural –s. What is common to these processes is that an otherwise productive morphological operation (e.g. -ed affixation, -s affixation, lexical compounding) is constrained or has exceptions in adult language, and it is these exceptions and constraints that cause difficulty forthe subjects with WS.

Another point of concern with the phonological deficit account is related to Thomas & Karmiloff Smith’s (1999) discussion of ‘shifted constraints’, the idea that the overspecification of phonological representations in WS implies that their semantic representations are impoverished. The logic here is not clear. Several researchers have argued that lexical-semantic aspects of language are impaired in WS (e.g. Bellugi et al. 1994), but how this should follow from a phonological deficit is not obvious. Even in connectionist non-modular accounts of language (e.g. Elman et al. 1996), sound and meaning are encoded and represented separately, i.e. phonology andsemantics are logically independent.

A final problem with the theory of phonological deficit in which subjects with WS place “more

当然，以下是你提供的文本的中文翻译：

(1985) 年和 Alegre & Gordon (1995) 的研究发现，即使他们的样本中最年幼的孩子，即3岁的孩子，也能够区分复合词中的规则复数和不规则复数。Clahsen 等人 (1992, 1996) 在德语儿童语言中复制了 Gordon 的结果。Clahsen 等人的研究中所有年龄段的无碍儿童都在复合词中产出了不规则复数，并避免使用规则复数。因此，在 Williams 综合征 (WS) 中观察到的复合词中的复数模式并不对应于任何在无碍儿童发展中发现的阶段。这些结果对 Thomas 和 Karmiloff-Smith (1999) 提出的延迟假说提出了质疑。

接下来考虑 WS 中假设的语音缺陷，这可以解释为什么在已有的动词上 WS 儿童在不规则形式上的表现比规则形式差，以及为什么在非实词动词上他们的一般化能力比无碍对照组差。这一解释的一个难点在于 WS 数据中规则和不规则模式过度应用的差异。Thomas 等人 (1999) 没有直接比较这两种类型的过度应用，但他们观察到 WS 组产生的不规则化形式显著少于典型发展的儿童。Clahsen 和 Almazan (1998) 直接比较了规则和不规则过去分词形式的过度应用。他们发现，WS 受试者广泛过度使用规则的 -ed 过去分词，而不规则化则极为罕见。-ed 词缀被 WS 受试者（错误地）附加到测试中的 38% 已知不规则动词上（相比之下，对照组为 13%），以及 65% 仅与现有不规则动词押韵的非实词动词上（相比之下，对照组为 19%），而不规则化的发生率不足 10%。类似的结果也在名词复数上得到了验证 (Clahsen 和 Almazan 2001)。WS 受试者广泛过度使用规则复数后缀，其频率是无碍对照组的两倍，而不规则模式则没有被过度应用。这一点也在一项针对说德语的 WS 患者的近期研究 (Krause 和 Penke 2000) 中得到了证实。研究发现，WS 受试者会过度规范化规则的 -t 分词，即使是在高频不规则动词上也是如此，而这种错误在对照数据中并没有出现。此外，与无碍对照组相比，WS 数据中的不规则复数模式几乎不存在过度应用。这些发现与英语的研究结果一致，表明 WS 患者可能过多地使用屈折规则。

根据 Thomas 和 Karmiloff-Smith 的语音缺陷理论，人们会预期 WS 患者会在各种屈折模式的一般化过程中存在缺陷，因为他们的语音表征过于详细。然而，WS 悟性似乎更愿意过度扩展规则屈折模式而不是不规则屈折模式的结果却没有得到解释。

另外，很难理解语音缺陷假设如何解释 WS 患者产生的带有规则复数作为非主元素的错误复合词（例如 *rats-eater）。这类错误并不是由于不规则屈折或在非实词词汇上的一般化受损所引起的。两种竞争的形式（例如 rat 和 rats）都是现有的词形，即使 WS 患者具有“过于详细的语音表征”，这也无法解释为什么 WS 儿童在复合词中频繁使用复数形式，而典型发展的儿童几乎总是使用单数形式。从形态学的角度来看，WS 受试者在复合词中的行为与他们频繁过度使用规则过去分词 -ed 和规则复数 -s 是一致的。这些过程共有的特征是，原本多产的形态操作（例如 -ed 附着、-s 附着、词汇复合）在成人语言中有例外或限制，正是这些例外和限制给 WS 受试者带来了困难。

另一个关于语音缺陷假说的问题涉及 Thomas 和 Karmiloff-Smith (1999) 关于“转移限制”的讨论，即 WS 中语音表征的过度规格导致其语义表征贫乏的想法。这里的逻辑并不明确。一些研究者认为 WS 在语言的词汇-语义方面存在缺陷（例如 Bellugi 等人 1994），但如何从语音缺陷推导出这种结果并不显而易见。甚至在联结主义的非模块化语言理论中（例如 Elman 等人 1996），声音和意义也是分开编码和表示的，即语音和语义在逻辑上是独立的。

关于 WS 患者“更多依赖”语音缺陷理论的最后一个问题是…

7

weight on phonological information and less weight on semantic information” is the difficulty for this formulation in accounting for differences in ability in WS, between skills on different forms of lexico-semantic tasks. Several studies have reported superior performance on receptive vocabulary using the Peabody Picture Vocabulary Test [PPVT] or British Picture Vocabulary Scale [BPVS]. Subjects with WS performed significantly better than normal mental age matched controls (Bellugi et al. 1990) and above the level of the subjects’ mental ages, derived from other measures (Tyler et al. 1997, Temple et al. 2001). Superior performance has also been reported on tasks of oral fluency, in which words have to be selected from the lexicon to conform to specified phonological (e.g. beginning with the letter ‘f’) or semantic (names of animals) constraints (Volterra et al. 1996, Bellugi et al. 1994), though not every study reports this quantitative advantage (Rossen et al. 1996). These areas of potential lexico-semantic advantage contrast with studies in which lexico semantic impairment is suggested, such as impoverished ability in defining words (Bellugi et al. 1990) and naming (Bromberg et al. 1994). If such results were reliable their task-specific effects would pose problems for generalised theories such as Thomas and Karmiloff-Smith’s. Even if one accepted that overspecified phonological representations could lead to impoverished semantic representations (though see above), the theory does not account for their task-specific manifestations. The theory could account for impaired naming, where a word has to be retrieved in response to a picture. However, it could not simultaneously account for enhanced receptive vocabulary where a picture is selected from a spoken word and enhanced semantic fluency where a word is retrieved in response to a semantic cue. Whilst task-specific effects are often problematic for generalised theories, they are less problematic for modular theories. Results from analyses of contrasting lexical skills in WS and their theoretical implications (Temple et al. 2001) arediscussed further in section 4.

Initial investigations of early reading skills in WS have produced similar contrasts. The pattern of reading described is characterised by semantic errors and complete inability to read nonwords and parallels that of deep dyslexia (Marshall & Newcombe 1966, Coltheart et al. 1980). Phonological processes in the reading in WS have developed to the extent that some individual letters can be sounded correctly. However, this fails to block semantic errors, which indicates modularity

8

between phonological and semantic processes in reading rather than any “shifted constraint” of one influencing the other. The severe impairment of phonological skills in reading despite some competent oral phonological abilities also argues for modularity within phonological processesthemselves (Temple 2001).

Overall, the results discussed above indicate that the proposal of delay in normal language development in WS resulting from overly detailed phonological representations is unable to account for the pattern of linguistic performance observed in WS. In the following sections, the results from studies of comparative adjectives, lexical skills and literacy will be discussed in moredetail.

“在语音信息上赋予更大的权重而在语义信息上赋予较小的权重”这一表述在解释威廉斯综合征（Williams Syndrome, WS）患者不同能力和不同形式的词汇-语义任务之间的差异时存在困难。多项研究报道了在使用皮博迪图片词汇测试 [Peabody Picture Vocabulary Test, PPVT] 或英国图片词汇量表 [British Picture Vocabulary Scale, BPVS] 测量的接受性词汇方面，WS 患者的出色表现。与正常匹配的精神年龄对照组相比，WS 悅者的表现在统计上显著更好（Bellugi 等，1990），并且超出根据其他测量得出的精神年龄水平（Tyler 等，1997；Temple 等，2001）。也有研究报告，在口头流畅度任务中表现出色，这些任务要求从词汇中选择符合特定语音（例如以字母 ‘f’ 开头）或语义（动物名称）限制的词语（Volterra 等，1996；Bellugi 等，1994），尽管不是每项研究都报告了这种定量优势（Rossen 等，1996）。这些潜在的词汇-语义优势领域与一些研究形成了对比，这些研究提示了词汇-语义损伤，如定义词汇能力的贫乏（Bellugi 等，1990）和命名能力的下降（Bromberg 等，1994）。如果这些结果可靠的话，它们的任务特异性效应会为一般化理论（如 Thomas 和 Karmiloff-Smith 的理论）带来问题。即使我们接受了过度指定的语音表示可能导致贫乏的语义表示（但见上文），该理论也无法解释其任务特异性的表现。该理论可以解释命名缺陷，即需要从图片中检索词汇的情况。然而，它不能同时解释接受性词汇的增强（从听到的词汇中选择图片）以及语义流畅度的增强（从语义线索中检索词汇）。尽管一般化理论常常难以处理任务特异性效应，但对于模块化理论来说，这些问题较少。WS 对照词汇技能的研究及其理论含义（Temple 等，2001）将在第 4 部分进一步讨论。

对 WS 早期阅读技能的初步研究表明了类似的对比。描述的阅读模式以语义错误和完全无法阅读非词为特点，并且与深度失读症（Marshall & Newcombe, 1966; Coltheart 等，1980）类似。在 WS 中，阅读中的语音过程已经发展到某个程度，个别字母能够被正确发音。然而，这并不能防止语义错误的发生，这表明在阅读过程中语音过程和语义过程之间存在模块化而非一种影响另一种的“约束转移”。尽管具有一定的口语语音能力，但阅读中的语音技能却严重受损，这也支持了语音过程本身内的模块化（Temple, 2001）。

总的来说，上述讨论的结果表明，由于过于详细的语音表示导致的正常语言发展的迟缓这一假设无法解释 WS 患者的语言表现模式。在接下来的部分中，将更详细地讨论比较形容词、词汇技能和读写能力方面的研究结果。

3 Comparative adjectives in WS To further examine the morpho-syntactic skills of subjects with WS, we have examined how they form comparative adjectives. Gradable adjectives in English can form comparatives by –er suffixation (big bigger) and/or by a periphrastic form with more (unusual more unusual). In addition, a small number of highly frequent adjectives have suppletive comparative forms (good – better, bad – worse). For most adjectives, the suffixed and the periphrastic comparative are in complementary distribution, while for some adjectives, both options exist (see Barber 1964, Aronoff 1976, Frank 1972). The use of –er suffixation is to a certain extent constrained by syllable structure, in addition to other factors: monosyllabic adjectives typically form –er comparatives, likewise disyllabic adjectives ending in –y (e.g. happy), while the comparative of most other adjectives with more than one syllable is formed periphrastically (e.g. more modern). This distribution, however, is not without exceptions. Aronoff (1976) cites *apter versus stupider as exceptions. Note also that monosyllabic adjectives can readily be used with more, when a speaker wants to emphasize the idea of comparison, for example by adding a than-clause (John is more mad than Bob) and in the so-called correlative construction (The more old he is, the more wise he becomes). Moreover, borrowed gradable adjectives, even monosyllabic ones, resist –er suffixation (chic *chicer, macho *machoer). Even though most disyllabic adjectives take periphrastic comparatives, there are many that require the suffixed comparative, e.g. adjectives ending in–ple, -ble, -tle and -dle (simpler, nobler, subtler, idler). Finally, disyllabic adjectives ending in -ly,

9

-ow, -some, and –er (e.g. lovely, narrow, handsome, clever) as well as those with initial or final syllable stress (e.g. pleasant, profound) have both comparative options available, according to Frank(1972).

The linguistic analysis of periphrastic and suppletive comparative forms is fairly straightforward and uncontroversial. Suppletive comparatives such as worse, better and further are probably lexically listed, and the periphrastic construction involves the insertion/merger of more for adjectives that do not have a morphologically formed comparative. Graziano-King (1999) presents an analysis of the more+Adj construction in terms of Chomsky (1995) in which the periphrastic construction is formed in the syntax, as a last resort to check an abstract degree feature when a bare adjective form is unable to do so; in other words, more insertion is blocked by the presence of a suppletive or suffixed comparative form. By contrast, the linguistic representation of –er comparatives is controversial. Several linguists have posited an –er suffixation rule that is said to be morphophonogically conditioned such that it only applies to monosyllabic adjectives and disyllabic ones with certain endings (see e.g. Aronoff 1976, DiSciullo & Williams 1987). The difficulty, however, has been to capture all the exceptions that resist –er suffixation. Consider, for example, *apter versus stupider mentioned above, or handsomer versus *irksomer. Moreover, Graziano-King (1999) observed that all of the exceptions to –er suffixation are low-frequency adjectives. On these grounds, she suggested that there is no –er suffixation rule for English comparatives and that the existing –er comparatives are lexically listed. Support for these claims comes from an acceptability judgement task performed with 70 adult native speakers, 36 four-year-olds and 36 seven-year-olds in which an –er comparative preference was found for high-frequency mono-syllabic adjectives, but not for low-frequency ones. Unimpaired children have been reported to produce both –er and more comparatives early on. Graziano-King (1999) analysed corpora from the CHILDES database (MacWhinney 1995) of two children (age range: 0;7 – 8;0) and found 220 instances of -er comparatives and 22 more forms. There were also 13 cases of double markings, such as more lighter, more specialer, more cleaner. Similar results were obtained from elicited production experiments. Children of all age groups studied

3 威廉姆斯综合症（WS）中的比较级形容词
为了进一步研究患有威廉姆斯综合症的受试者的形态句法能力，我们考察了他们如何形成比较级形容词。在英语中，可分级形容词可以通过加-er后缀（如 big → bigger）和/或通过使用more 的迂回形式（如 unusual → more unusual）来构成比较级。此外，少数高频形容词具有替代性的比较级形式（如 good → better, bad → worse）。对于大多数形容词来说，带后缀的比较级和迂回形式的比较级是互补分布的，而有些形容词两种形式都可以使用（参见 Barber 1964, Aronoff 1976, Frank 1972）。-er 后缀的使用在一定程度上受到音节结构以及其他因素的限制：单音节形容词通常使用-er 比较级，类双音节以-y 结尾的形容词也是如此（例如 happy），而大多数其他多音节的形容词则采用迂回形式的比较级（例如 more modern）。然而，这种分布并非没有例外。Aronoff (1976) 举例 *apter 和 stupider 为例外。还应注意的是，当说话者想要强调比较的概念时，单音节形容词可以很容易地用 more 来表达，例如加上 than 从句（John is more mad than Bob），以及所谓的关联结构（The more old he is, the more wise he becomes）。此外，借来的可分级形容词，即使是单音节的，也避免使用-er 后缀（如 chic → *chicer, macho → *machoer）。尽管大多数双音节形容词采用迂回形式的比较级，但仍有许多需要使用带后缀的比较级，例如以-ple、-ble、-tle 和 -dle 结尾的形容词（simpler, nobler, subtler, idler）。最后，根据 Frank (1972)，以 -ly, -ow, -some, 和 -er 结尾的双音节形容词（如 lovely, narrow, handsome, clever），以及那些带有初始或末尾音节重音的形容词（如 pleasant, profound），都有两种比较级选项可供选择。

periphrastic 和替代性比较级形式的语言学分析相对简单且无争议。替代性比较级如 worse, better 和 further 可能是词汇列表中的条目，而迂回形式则涉及插入/合并 more 用于那些没有形态学形成的比较级形式的形容词。Graziano-King (1999) 根据 Chomsky (1995) 的理论对 more+Adj 构造进行了分析，认为该迂回构造是在句法中形成的，作为一种最后手段，用来检查抽象程度特征，当一个单独的形容词形式无法做到这一点时；换句话说，当存在替代性或带后缀的形式时，more 插入会被阻止。相比之下，-er 比较级的语言表示是有争议的。几位语言学家假设了一个被语义音位条件限制的 -er 后缀规则，该规则仅适用于单音节形容词和某些结尾的双音节形容词（参见 Aronoff 1976, DiSciullo & Williams 1987）。然而，难点在于捕捉所有抵制 -er 后缀的现象。例如前面提到的 *apter 和 stupider，或者 handsomer 和 *irksomer。此外，Graziano-King (1999) 观察到，所有的 -er 后缀例外都是低频形容词。基于这些原因，她建议英语比较级并没有 -er 后缀规则，现存的 -er 比较级是词汇表中的项目。支持这一观点的证据来自于一项对70名成人母语者、36名四岁儿童和36名七岁儿童进行的可接受性判断任务，结果发现高频率单音节形容词倾向于使用 -er 比较级，但低频的单音节形容词则不然。据报道，正常的儿童在早期就可以产生 -er 和 more 比较级。Graziano-King (1999) 分析了 CHILDES 数据库（MacWhinney 1995）中两名儿童（年龄范围：0;7 – 8;0）的语料，发现了220例 -er 比较级和22例 more 形式。还有13例双重标记的情况，如 more lighter, more specialer, more cleaner。类似的结论也是从引发生成实验中获得的。所有年龄段的儿童在这项研究中都表现出相似的结果。

In the following, we will report the results of an elicited production experiment that was administered to 4 subjects with WS and to two control groups of 15 unimpaired children each withchronological ages similar to the mental ages of the WS children1.

Participants The 4 subjects with WS are the same as those examined in previous studies from our group (see Clahsen & Almazan 1988, 2001, Temple et al. 2001). The subjects’ chronological ages are as follows: Jane 11;2, Florence 12;7, Emily 13;1, Martin 15;4. Their mental ages were derived from scores on the Wechsler Intelligence Scale for Children IIIUK (Wechsler 1992). By this method, Emily and Jane had mental ages of 5;4 and 5;7, whilst Florence and Martin had mental ages of 7;5 and 7;7 respectively. A detailed profile of these subjects and the results of other standardized tests including the British Picture Vocabulary Scale [BPVS] (Dunn et al. 1982) and the Test of Reception of Grammar (TROG, Bishop 1983) can be found in our previous studies of WS. BPVSscores are also discussed in section 4.

The two control groups consist of monolingual English-speaking children who live in native homes and were randomly selected by date of birth from a state school in Suffolk, England. The first control group consists of 15 children with a mean chronological age of 5;3 years (range: 4;10 to 5;8), and the second one of 15 children with a mean chronological age of 7;4 years (range: 6;10 to 7;9). Subjects who had any known neurological abnormality, learning difficulties or a history ofspecial needs were excluded.

The materials and procedures were adopted from Dalalakis (1994); similar kinds of elicitation tasks for comparatives have been used by Layton & Stick (1979) and Gathercole (1985). Twenty pairs of pictures were used in which two items were depicted that differed in terms of a gradable attribute, e.g. size. The pictures were accompanied by two sentences, which were read aloud to the children. For example: This circle is big. This is even _____? The children were prompted to complete the sentence with a comparative form. Five kinds of target adjectives were used as shown in (1):

(1) ER adjectives MORE adject. EITHER IRREGULARS NONCE big dangerous round good weff funny expensive straight bad kell sad modern tasty bimmy young unusual bitter toshal little open According to Dalalakis (1994), the adjectives in the first column require –er comparative forms in adult English, those in the second column have periphrastic comparatives, while those in the third column may take either form. The adjectives good and bad have irregular (suppletive) comparatives. The first three nonce adjectives were expected to elicit –er comparatives, weff and kell because they are monosyllabic and bimmy because of the –y ending, while toshal should be more likely to yield aperiphrastic comparative.

The stimulus materials were presented to each child individually. One of the unimpaired control children failed to complete the experiment, and her responses were not included in the analysis. All other unimpaired and WS children did not show any difficulty understanding the task. The children’sresponses were written down and tape-recorded for verification.

生成了更多带有“-er”形式的比较级，尽管他们在正确标记需要“-er”形式的形容词方面更为成功。例如，Gathercole（1985: 96）发现，她的样本中年龄最小的孩子，即2岁5个月到3岁的孩子，也能产生带后缀和迂回形式的比较级，其正确率分别为28%和15%。

以下我们将报告一个诱发性产出实验的结果，该实验对4名威廉姆斯综合症（Williams Syndrome, WS）患者以及两个对照组进行，每个对照组由15名发育正常儿童组成，这些儿童的实际年龄与WS儿童的心理年龄相似。

参与者：这4名WS患者是我们研究小组之前研究中调查的同一对象（参见Clahsen & Almazan 1988, 2001; Temple et al. 2001）。这些患者的年龄如下：Jane 11岁2个月，Florence 12岁7个月，Emily 13岁1个月，Martin 15岁4个月。他们的心理年龄是通过韦克斯勒儿童智力量表第三版英国版（Wechsler, 1992）得分推导出来的。通过这种方法，Emily 和 Jane 的心理年龄分别为5岁4个月和5岁7个月，而Florence 和 Martin的心理年龄分别为7岁5个月和7岁7个月。关于这些受试者的详细资料以及包括《英国图画词汇量表》[BPVS] (Dunn et al. 1982)和《语法接受测试》(TROG, Bishop 1983)等标准化测试结果可以在我们之前关于WS的研究中找到。BPVS得分也在第4节中有讨论。

两组对照组包括生活在国内家庭中的单语英语儿童，他们是从英格兰萨福克郡的一所公立学校按出生日期随机挑选的。第一对照组由15名实际年龄平均为5岁3个月（范围：4岁10个月至5岁8个月）的儿童组成，第二对照组由15名实际年龄平均为7岁4个月（范围：6岁10个月至7岁9个月）的儿童组成。已知有神经异常、学习困难或特殊需求史的受试者被排除在外。

材料和程序采用了Dalalakis (1994)的方法；Layton & Stick (1979)和Gathercole (1985)也使用了类似的诱发比较级的形式任务。一共使用了20对图片，每张图片描绘了在某个等级属性上有所不同的两个项目，例如大小。图片附有两句提示语，读给孩子们听。例如：“这个圆圈很大。这个甚至更____？”然后引导孩子们用比较级形式完成句子。使用了五种目标形容词，如（1）所示：

(1) ER 形容词 MORE 形容词 EITHER IRREGULARS NONCE
big dangerous round good weff funny expensive straight bad kell sad modern tasty bimmy young unusual bitter toshal little open

根据Dalalakis (1994)，第一列的形容词在成人英语中需要“-er”形式作为比较级，第二列具有迂回形式的比较级，而第三列可以采用任何形式。形容词good和bad具有不规则（补充的）比较级。前三种虚构形容词期望引发“-er”形式的比较级，wef和kell因为是单音节词，bimmy因为以“-y”结尾；而toshal则更可能产生迂回形式的比较级。

刺激材料逐一向每个孩子展示。其中一个未受损的对照组儿童未能完成实验，她的回答没有包含在分析中。其他所有未受损儿童和WS儿童都没有表现出理解任务的困难。孩子们的回答被记录下来并录音以供验证。

//INSERT TAB. 1 HERE// Consider first the data from the unimpaired children. Tab.1 shows that the 5-year olds and the 7-year-olds produced –er comparatives as well as periphrastic forms with more, even though in both groups of children the suffixed forms were used more frequently than the periphrastic construction. Moreover, Tab.1 shows that the comparatives of ER adjectives are most often correctly formed by both groups of children, while for MORE adjectives they are less successful. There were also 3 cases of double markings, 2 from the 7-year-olds, 1 from the 5-year-olds, in which the children produced both more and a suffixed form, e.g. more bigger. These results from the control children replicate those of the previous studies of unimpaired children’s comparativeformations mentioned above.

The data from the WS children differ in several ways from those of the control children. The WS children (taken as a group) produced significantly more –er errors than the unimpaired children, t= 3.38, p < 0.01. That the WS children overapplied –er suffixation more often than the control children is clear, for example, from the MORE adjectives in Tab.1, for which the children with WS produced 89% and 90% -er overapplications, twice as many as the unimpaired children. In the other adjective types, there is also a clearer preference for -er in the WS data than in those of the normals. Tab.1 shows that the WS children achieve similar correctness scores to the normals for adjectives for which -er forms are grammatical, but they perform worse on adjectives that require other comparative forms. Adjectives that require irregular comparatives are all incorrect in the WS data, and only one of the MORE adjectives is correctly formed by the WS children. Instead, the WS children produce -er comparatives for all kinds of adjectives. The periphrastic construction, on

13

the other hand, is underused by the WS children, relative to unimpaired controls. The WS children do not produce any comparatives with more for ER adjectives, for nonce forms or for adjectives that allow both –er and more. There are also no cases of double markings (more bigger) in the WS data. Another difference between the WS children and the unimpaired controls concerns the use of stem forms, i.e. cases in which the adjective was simply repeated without any comparative marking. There are quite a few such responses in the data from the control children, particularly in the 5-year-olds, 49% for MORE adjectives and 30% in the EITHER group, indicating that they were unwilling to apply –er or more comparative formation in these cases. The WS children, however, produced just 7 stem forms that did not have a comparative marking. Instead, they mostoften applied –er suffixation.

Summarizing, the data from the WS children show that they have just one way of forming comparatives, and this is –er affixation, which they apply freely to any adjective. This holds for both groups of WS children studied here. In contrast to that, the unimpaired children produce not only –er comparatives, but also periphrastic comparative constructions, suppletive comparatives, and double markings (more bigger). The data also show that the use of –er is more constrained inthe unimpaired children than in the subjects with WS.

含有目标词干的回应在表1中针对所研究的五种形容词进行了展示。这些百分比展示了这些回应的细分情况。儿童如果产生了（无法理解的）误读，或将目标形容词替换为其他词汇，这样的回应未被纳入分析；这类回应占5岁正常对照组总回应的20%，7岁正常对照组总回应的8%，而威廉斯综合症（WS）数据中的此类回应仅占总回应的1%。

//在此处插入表1//

首先考虑来自无语言障碍儿童的数据。表1显示，5岁和7岁的儿童既产生了-er形式的比较级，也产生了带有“more”的迂回形式，尽管两组儿童使用的缀合形式比迂回构造更频繁。此外，表1还显示，两个年龄段的儿童在ER形容词的比较级形成上最为正确，而在MORE形容词上的成功度较低。还有3个双重标记的情况，其中7岁儿童有2例，5岁儿童有1例，他们同时使用了“more”和一个缀合形式，例如“more bigger”。这些来自对照组儿童的结果重复了上述提到的关于无障碍儿童比较级形成的先前研究。

威廉斯综合症（WS）儿童的数据与对照组儿童的数据在几个方面有所不同。作为一个群体，WS儿童产生的-er错误显著多于无障碍儿童，t=3.38, p<0.01。显然，WS儿童过量应用-er缀合的情况比对照组儿童更为常见。例如，在表1的 MORE 形容词中，WS 儿童对于这些形容词分别产生了 89% 和 90% 的 -er 错误应用，这一比例是无障碍儿童的两倍。在其他类型的形容词中，WS数据也表现出了比正常儿童更倾向于使用-er的形式。表1显示，对于那些-er形式符合语法规则的形容词，WS儿童达到了与正常儿童相似的正确率，但在需要其他比较形式的形容词上表现较差。对于需要不规则比较级的形容词，在WS数据中全部都是错误的，而且只有一个是通过“more”形式正确形成的。相反地，对于所有类型的形容词，WS儿童都倾向于产生-er形式的比较级。另一方面，相较于无障碍对照组，WS儿童较少使用“more”这种迂回构造。WS儿童没有为 ER 形容词、非真实形式或允许同时使用 –er 和 more 的形容词生成任何带有 more 的比较级。WS 数据中也没有发现双重标记（如 more bigger）的情况。另外一项不同之处在于词干形式的使用，即简单重复形容词而不加比较标记的情况。在对照组儿童的数据中，特别是5岁儿童的数据中，这类响应较为常见，MORE 形容词为49%，EITHER 组别为30%，表明他们不愿意在这种情况下使用 -er 或 more 比较形式。相比之下，WS 儿童仅有7次未带比较标记的词干形式响应。他们最常进行的是-er附加。

总之，WS儿童的数据表明，他们形成比较级只有一种方式，即-er后缀，并且他们自由地将其应用于任何形容词。这一规律适用于本研究中两个年龄组的WS儿童。与此相反，无障碍儿童不仅产生-er形式的比较级，还会产生带有“more”的迂回形式的比较级，以及补充性比较级和双重标记（more bigger）。数据还显示，在无障碍儿童中，-er的使用受到更多限制，而在WS患者中则更加自由。

继续翻译：

另一方面，相对于无障碍对照组而言，WS儿童使用的迂回结构“more”相对较少。WS儿童没有为ER形容词、非真实形式或允许使用-er和more的形容词生成任何带有more的比较级。在WS数据中也不存在双重标记的情形（例如more bigger）。另一个WS儿童与无障碍对照组之间的区别是对词干形式的使用，即形容词简单重复而没有添加任何比较标记的情况。在对照组儿童，尤其是5岁儿童的数据中，有很多这类反应，MORE形容词占49%，EITHER组别占30%，这表明他们在这些情况下不愿意使用-er或more来形成比较级。然而，WS儿童只有7次未带比较标记的词干形式的响应，取而代之的是，他们最常使用-er后缀。

简而言之，来自WS儿童的数据表明，他们仅有一种形成比较级的方式，那就是-er后缀，并且他们将这种方式自由地应用于各种形容词。这适用于这里研究的两个WS儿童年龄组。与此相比，无障碍儿童不仅形成了-er形式的比较级，还能形成带有“more”的迂回结构、替代性比较级以及双重标记（如more bigger）。数据还表明，无障碍儿童对-er的使用比WS受试者更为受限。

原文[7/18]：

Discussion The WS data from the present experiment show that these children excessively overapply –er comparative adjective formation, and that the lexical exceptions and constraints on –er comparatives in English do not influence their comparative formations. These observations indicate that they have developed an –er suffixation rule which can freely generalize to any adjective. This interpretation of the comparatives data fits in with what we found on these children’s performance in the past tense and their use of noun plurals (Clahsen & Almazan 1998, 2001). Their performance was explained in terms of a selective lexical deficit: WS children have difficulty retrieving or accessing irregular past-tense and plural forms, which are lexically stored as subnodes of complex lexical entries. The lexeme drive, for example, comprises a base form (drive) and two subentries (driven, drove). The children with WS can access the base form when

14

required, but their performance on the lexical exceptions (i.e. the subentries) seems to be impaired. Combinatorial operations, on the other hand, for example rules of affixation, seem to be unaffected in the WS children, hence their high correctness scores on regular past-tense and plural formation and their frequent –ed and –s plural overregularization errors. The comparatives data confirm the dissociation found for past tense and plural formation in WS. Comparative formation with –er is lexically constrained in English. It has even been suggested that –er comparatives are lexically stored in adult native speakers (Graziano-King 1999). If this is correct, adjectives that allow –er comparatives would have subentries for these forms; the adjective hot, for example, would have subentries for hotter and (probably also for) hottest. The WS data suggest that these children generate comparatives by a general –er affixation rule which can apply to any adjective. Thus, the WS children rely on their computational (rule-based) system to form comparatives, and they either fail to store or activate comparative forms in the lexicon. Thus, similarly to their past tense and plural performance, the comparatives data indicate that the WS children make use of combinatorialoperations to compensate for a lexical deficit.

Consider, as an alternative to this interpretation of the data, the findings on comparatives in the light of Thomas & Karmiloff-Smith’s account of WS. Recall that according to their hypothesis of ‘overly rich phonological representations’ in WS, these children should be impaired in generalizing inflectional patterns, particularly to nonce words. This is because the overspecification of existing items impedes generalizations. Thus, the phonological deficit account predicts reduced levels of overgeneralization in WS. It is clear from the data in Tab.1 that this prediction is not confirmed by the present data. We found high -er overapplication rates, both for existing and nonce adjective forms, higher than those of unimpaired control children. A second related claim of Thomas & Karmiloff-Smith’s account is that the morpho-syntactic skills of WS children represent a delay of normal development. This predicts that the linguistic performance of WS children should be similar to that of younger unimpaired children. The comparatives data do not confirm the delay hypothesis. It was found that the children with WS relied almost exclusively on –er comparative affixation and heavily overapplied it without any obvious restriction.

15

Unimpaired children of all age groups tested in the comparative elicitation task (as well as in other tasks) behaved differently. Recall, for example, the findings from Gathercole (1985) which are based on a similar kind of elicitation task to that used here. She observed that even the youngest children in her sample, i.e. the 2;5 to 3-year-olds, produced not only –er comparatives but also periphrastic (more) comparatives, and that not only –er was used in overapplication errors, but that more was also overapplied to ER adjectives. Thus, it seems as if the WS comparative behaviour doesnot simply represent delayed language development.

翻译[7/18]：

讨论

本次实验的威廉姆斯综合症（WS）数据显示，这些儿童过度使用了-er比较级形容词的构形，并且英语中对-er比较级的词汇例外和限制并没有影响他们的比较级构形。这些观察结果表明，他们已经形成了一种可以自由泛化到任何形容词的-er后缀规则。这种对比较级数据的解释符合我们以前在这些儿童过去时态表现及名词复数使用方面的发现 (Clahsen & Almazan 1998, 2001)。他们的表现被解释为选择性词汇缺陷：WS儿童在检索或获取不规则过去时态和复数形式方面有困难，而这些形式是以复杂词汇条目的子节点形式存储在词库中的。例如，动词“drive”包含一个基本形式（drive）和两个子条目（driven, drove）。有WS的儿童在需要时可以访问基本形式，但他们在词汇例外（即子条目）上的表现似乎受到损害。另一方面，组合操作，例如后缀规则，在WS儿童中似乎没有受到影响，因此他们在规则过去时态和复数形式的正确率较高，并且经常出现过度规则化的错误，如-ed和-s复数。

比较级数据进一步确认了在威廉姆斯综合症中发现的过去时态和复数形成之间的分离现象。英语中的-er比较级是受词汇约束的。甚至有人认为，成年母语者中的-er比较级也是以词汇形式存储的 (Graziano-King 1999)。如果这是正确的，那么允许-er比较级的形容词会有这些形式的子条目；例如，形容词“hot”会有“hotter”和（可能还有）“hottest”的子条目。WS的数据表明，这些儿童通过一种通用的-er后缀规则来生成比较级，这一规则可应用于任何形容词。因此，WS儿童依赖其计算（基于规则）系统来形成比较级，并且他们要么未能在词库中存储比较级形式，要么无法激活这些形式。因此，类似于他们在过去时态和复数上的表现，比较级数据表明WS儿童利用组合操作来弥补词汇缺陷。

考虑另一种对数据的解释，即将比较级发现与Thomas & Karmiloff-Smith对威廉姆斯综合症的解释结合起来。回忆一下，根据他们关于WS“过于丰富的音韵表示”的假设，这些儿童应该在推广屈折模式方面受到损害，特别是对于非单词。这是因为现有项目的过度指定阻碍了概括。因此，音韵缺陷解释预测WS中的过度概括水平会降低。显然，从表1中的数据来看，这一预测并未得到当前数据的支持。我们发现，无论是对于现有的还是非单词的形容词形式，-er的过度应用率都非常高，高于正常对照组儿童。Thomas & Karmiloff-Smith解释的第二个相关主张是，WS儿童的形态句法技能代表了正常发展的延迟。这预测WS儿童的语言表现应类似于年幼的正常儿童。然而，比较级数据并未确认这种延迟假说。我们发现，WS儿童几乎完全依赖-er比较级后缀，并且高度过度使用它，没有任何明显的限制。

所有年龄组的正常儿童在比较级诱导任务（以及其他任务）中的表现都有所不同。例如，回想Gathercole (1985) 的发现，她使用的诱导任务与这里类似。她观察到，即使是她样本中最年轻的儿童（即2岁半至3岁的儿童），不仅产生了-er比较级，还产生了迂回的（more）比较级，并且在过度应用错误中不仅使用了-er，还将more过度应用于ER形容词。因此，似乎WS的比较级行为并不简单地代表语言发展的延迟。

原文[8/18]：

4 Lexical skills in WS As reported above, several previous studies found contrasts in subjects with WS in their performance between enhanced receptive vocabulary and oral fluency on the one hand (Bellugi et al. 1990, Tyler et al. 1997, Volterra et al. 1996) and impaired naming and word definition on the other (Bellugi et al. 1990, Bromberg et al. 1994). Issues have also been raised about atypical language use in WS. It has been described as having many of the qualities of cocktail party speech (Bradley & Udwin 1989, Udwin et al. 1987) with frequent use of social phrases and idioms. Individual word use has also been reported as unusual. Bellugi et al. (1992) provide the example “I’ll have to evacuate the glass” meaning “empty the glass”. Unusual selections within oral fluency responses for the children with WS are also reported with increased numbers of low frequency responses (e.g. terandon, unicorn, in animal fluency) and significantly more items of low frequency among later items in lists, even where overall performance levels numerically aresimilar (Rossen et al. 1996).

These issues of possible lexical talent and impairment and atypical use of vocabulary have been explored recently, in a study of the four children with WS described above (Temple et al. 2001). Consider, first, the results of various psychometric measures to assess the children’s lexico semantic skill in relation to their mental age. Receptive vocabulary age was determined from scores on the BPVS (Dunn et al. 1982) and naming age was determined from the naming subtest of the British Ability Scales (Elliot et al. 1983). Age equivalent scores for knowledge of semantic concepts were determined from the similarities subtest of the WISC-IIIUK (Wechsler et al. 1992).

16

This requires the child to judge how two words are the same, an easy item being wheel and ball and a difficult item being liberty and justice. The child is told that there is a similarity and that the items are the same in some way and they must identify the similarity. The scores on these psychometric measures are summarised in Tab. 2. This indicates that all the children with WS have receptive vocabulary scores above the level of their mental ages. They also all have semantic concept ages above the level of their mental age. Yet, all the children have naming ages below the receptive vocabulary levels and they are therefore all anomic in relation to these measures oflexico-semantic representation.

//INSERT TAB. 2 HERE// Receptive vocabulary was further examined by using multiple examples of items from the same semantic field. Children heard a spoken word and had to select a picture, which matched that word. This format was the same as for the BPVS. However, in the BPVS the requirement is to select a picture, which matches the word, from an array containing three distracters, some of which resemble the target but are not semantically linked. In contrast, here the child had to select the target from an array containing 23 semantic distracters, all of which were from the same semantic field. The items employed were names for animals (including birds and sea creatures), indoor objects, foods and clothes, with stimuli selected from Snodgrass and Vanderwart (1980). When the children had to select in this way from multiple distracters in the same semantic field, their receptive vocabulary levels were significantly weaker than those of mental age controls. For example Martin is correct on 75% of items compared to a mental age control score of 94% (sd=2.92) [z=6.50, p<0.001]. Thus, when detailed semantic specification is required, the system which has developed for the child with WS is less effective than normal. It is possible that the system improves with age but it is also possible that the elevated levels of receptive vocabulary reported in adults with WS (e.g. Bellugi et al. 1990, Tyler et al. 1997) are only superficially correct, as they are also based on results from the BPVS or the similar PPVT (Dunn & Dunn 1981). Testing of older cases of WS with the multiple semantic distracters employed by Temple etal. (2001) would resolve this issue.

翻译[8/18]：

  1. 威廉姆斯综合征（WS）中的词汇技能

如上所述，几项先前的研究发现WS患者的表现在一方面表现为增强的接受性词汇和口语流利度（Bellugi等人1990年，Tyler等人1997年，Volterra等人1996年），而在另一方面则存在命名和词义定义的缺陷（Bellugi等人1990年，Bromberg等人1994年）。关于WS中的非典型语言使用也提出了问题。这种语言使用被描述为具有许多鸡尾酒会谈话的特点（Bradley & Udwin 1989, Udwin等人1987），经常使用社交短语和成语。个别词语的使用也被报道为不寻常。Bellugi等人（1992）提供了一个例子：“我必须清空玻璃杯”意思是“倒空玻璃杯”。在WS儿童的口语流利反应中也报告了一些不寻常的选择，低频反应数量增加（例如，在动物流畅性测试中提到terandon和独角兽），即使总体表现水平在数值上相似，在列表的较后部分显著包含更多低频项目（Rossen等人1996）。

上述可能的词汇天赋和障碍以及词汇的非典型使用问题在最近的一项研究中得到了探讨，该研究涉及上述四位WS儿童（Temple等人2001）。首先考虑用于评估这些儿童相对于其心理年龄的词汇-语义技能的各种心理测量指标的结果。通过BPVS（Dunn等人1982）得分确定接受性词汇年龄，通过英国能力量表中的命名子测试（Elliot等人1983）得分确定命名年龄。从WISC-IIIUK（Wechsler等人1992）的相似性子测试确定语义概念知识的年龄当量得分。

这要求儿童判断两个词是如何相同的，一个简单的题目是轮子和球，一个难一些的题目是自由和平等。孩子被告知这两个词有相似之处，并且在某种程度上是一样的，他们必须识别这个相似之处。这些心理测量指标的结果总结见表2。这表明所有WS儿童的接受性词汇分数都高于其心理年龄。他们的语义概念年龄也都高于心理年龄。然而，所有儿童的命名年龄低于接受性词汇水平，因此，根据这些词汇-语义表征的测量指标，他们都处于失名状态。

//在此插入表2//

进一步通过使用同一语义域中的多个例项来检查接受性词汇。儿童听到一个口语词并选择与其匹配的图片。这一格式与BPVS相同。然而，在BPVS中，要求从一组包含三个干扰项的图阵中选择匹配目标单词的图片，其中一些干扰项类似于目标但没有语义关联。相比之下，在这里，儿童必须从一组包含23个语义干扰项的图阵中选出目标，所有这些干扰项都来自同一语义域。所使用的物品名称包括动物（包括鸟类和海洋生物）、室内物品、食物和衣物，刺激物选自Snodgrass和Vanderwart（1980）。当孩子不得不从同一语义域中的多个干扰项中选择时，他们的接受性词汇水平明显弱于控制组的心理年龄。例如，Martin对75%的项目正确，而心理年龄对照组的得分为94%（标准差=2.92）[z=6.50，p<0.001]。因此，当需要详细的语义规范时，对于WS儿童发展的系统来说，其效果不如正常情况。有可能随着年龄的增长系统会有所改善，但也有可能成人WS患者报告的高接受性词汇水平（例如Bellugi等人1990年，Tyler等人1997年）仅仅是表面上正确的，因为这些结果也是基于BPVS或类似的PPVT（Dunn & Dunn 1981）得出的。通过对年长的WS病例进行Temple等人（2001）使用的多重语义干扰测试，可以解决这个问题。

原文[9/18]：

The pervasive naming impairment reported in the psychometric measures above was found in the more detailed analysis to be most marked in the children with older mental ages. Overt error analysis was possible in comparison to control performance but also in comparison to recently published error data on the children’s naming of the Snodgrass and Vanderwart stimuli (1980) by Cycowicz (1997). This analysis indicated that for every child with WS, error responses included a significantly larger proportion of responses that were atypical, than those made by mental age controls. Examples of atypical responses made by the children with WS are caterpillar ! “antelope” (Emily), lobster ! “ostrich” (Martin), broom ! “saucepan”, spanner ! “corkscrew”. Despite these naming difficulties, Temple et al. (2001) found that oral fluency scores were significantly above mental age level for three of the four children with WS. Yet responses also had atypical characteristics with all the children showing a significantly elevated proportion ofresponses of low frequency.

Finally, reaction times were measured to naming pictures, colours and some other sets of stimuli. This study was conducted only with Florence and Martin, who were found to have the most marked anomia in the detailed analysis. The stimuli were selected to be as easy as possible in terms of being of high frequency, high familiarity and with early age-of-acquisition. Accuracy was high, above 89% in all categories for both controls and the children with WS. The mean response times for naming pictures and colours accurately are given in Tab.3. These results indicated that both Martin and Florence’s reaction times were significantly faster than mental age controls at naming pictures. Martin is also significantly faster at naming colours. Data from 10 year old controls are also given in Tab. 3. Martin is also significantly faster than these children who are three years above his mental age level. Florence is 1.5 sds above the speed for these children. //INSERT TAB. 3 HERE// These results summarise as follows. There is a pattern of high skill in receptive vocabulary when the distracters are neither too numerous nor too similar in semantic specification; high skill in identifying similarities between pairs of words when told that there is such a similarity and it should be identified, with no time constraint; and high skill in finding words according to a single

18

general semantic or phonological cue in oral fluency when selections have to be as fast and numerous as possible. Also when naming is accurate it is significantly faster than normal. In contrast, there is weak skill in receptive vocabulary when fine grain semantic knowledge is required. There are naming difficulties and naming errors are atypical and more loosely related in meaning to targets than for controls. Responses in oral fluency also include higher proportions ofnumbers of atypical low frequency responses.

Discussion Temple et al. (2001) proposed that lexical access in WS is constrained differently from normal, with looser criteria for target identification but a more rapid arrival at selected targets. This leads to fast-sloppy access and in some cases only partial activation of the full semantic specification for lexical targets. They propose that this enhanced speed contributes to the language advantage seen on some tasks but with incomplete activation increasing the error rate and affecting the pattern of errors on others. The rapid incomplete activation may be sufficient to generate good performance in receptive vocabulary when broad semantic knowledge is required but is insufficiently detailed for good performance in the face of multiple semantically similar competing distracters in the more detailed task. The fast but inadequate activation leads to naming errors and high rates of atypical errors. It enables high rates of selection in oral fluency when the word can be any one in a broad semantic field, without the requirement for fine grain semantic specification. It also enables good performance on the similarities sub-test when the children are told that there is a relationship between pairs of items and they must keep looking for it with no time constraints, which mayreduce the “sloppy activation”.

Temple et al (2001) propose a modular explanation for these effects in WS, integrating them with a modular model of lexical access. The good receptive vocabulary scores on the BPVS and good similarities performance would argue for good development of the semantic system itself. Poor picture naming would then occur at a word selection/search stage intermediate between the semantic system and the speech output lexicon. However, the poor performance on the receptive vocabulary task where there are multiple semantic distracters suggests that specification of entries

翻译[9/18]：

在上述心理测量中报告的普遍命名障碍，在更详细的分析中发现，在心智年龄较大的儿童中最为明显。通过对错误进行显性分析，不仅将其与对照组的表现进行比较，还与Cycowicz（1997年）最近发布的关于Williams综合症儿童对Snodgrass和Vanderwart（1980年）刺激物命名的错误数据进行了比较。该分析表明，对于每一个Williams综合症（WS）儿童，其错误反应中包含的比例显著高于心智年龄对照组的非典型反应。例如，Emily将毛毛虫命名为“羚羊”；Martin将龙虾命名为“鸵鸟”；其他例子还包括将扫帚命名为“锅”，将扳手套命名为“开瓶器”。尽管存在这些命名困难，Temple等人（2001年）发现四名患有WS的儿童中有三名的口语流畅度得分显著高于他们的心智年龄水平。然而，他们的反应也具有非典型特征，所有儿童表现出低频回答比例显著升高。

最后，对图片、颜色以及其他一些刺激物的命名反应时间进行了测量。这项研究仅对Florence和Martin进行了实施，他们在详细分析中显示出最明显的无名症状。选择的刺激物尽可能简单，频率高、熟悉度高且习得年龄早。准确性很高，对照组和WSC组儿童的所有类别中的准确率均超过89%。表3列出了Florence和Martin准确命名图片和颜色的平均反应时间。结果表明，Florence和Martin在图片命名反应时间上显著快于心智年龄对照组。此外，Martin在颜色命名反应时间上也显著更快。表3还提供了10岁对照组的数据。数据显示，Martin的反应速度也显著快于比他心智年龄高三年的孩子，而Florence的速度则比这些孩子快1.5个标准差。//插入表3在这里//

这些结果总结如下：当干扰项既不是太多也不是在语义上过于相似时，受试者在接收词汇方面有很高的技能；当被告知两词之间存在某种相似性需要识别且没有时间限制时，识别词汇相似性的技能也很高；在口头流畅性方面，当需要快速和大量选择时，根据单一的一般语义或语音线索找到单词的技能也很高。此外，准确命名时，反应时间显著快于正常水平。相比之下，当需要精细的语义知识时，接收词汇方面的技能较弱。命名过程中遇到困难，且命名错误是非典型的，并且与目标的意义关联比对照组更为松散。口头流畅性的回答中也包含更高比例的非典型低频回答。

讨论
Temple等人（2001年）提出，Williams综合症中的词汇访问受到不同于正常的不同约束，以更宽松的目标识别标准但更快达到选定目标的方式进行。这导致了快速但粗糙的目标访问，并在某些情况下仅有部分激活词汇目标的完整语义规格。他们建议这种增强的速度有助于某些任务上的语言优势，但不完整的激活会增加错误率并影响其他任务中的错误模式。快速但不完全的激活可能足以在需要广泛语义知识的接受词汇任务上产生良好的表现，但对于更细致的任务中多个语义相似的竞争干扰项，则不足以提供良好的表现。这种快速但不足的激活导致命名错误和高比例的非常规错误。它还能在广泛的语义领域内进行高频率的选择，而不需要精细的语义规格，从而在口头流利度上表现出高效率。在告诉儿童成对项目之间存在关系并要求持续寻找这种关系且没有时间限制的情况下，它也能带来良好的类似性子测试表现，这可能会减少“粗糙激活”。

Temple等人（2001年）提出了一个模块化的解释来说明WS中的这些效应，将其与词汇访问的模块化模型结合起来。BPVS的良好接受词汇得分和良好的类比性能表明语义系统的良好发展。不良的图片命名可能发生在介于语义系统和言语输出词汇之间的词选择/搜索阶段。然而，在多个语义干扰项的接受词汇任务上表现不佳表明条目规格的发育也可能存在问题。
