The impairment affects the representation in the semantic system or their activation via fast-sloppy access. This account also fits in with the proposed interpretation of the results on inflectional morphology in children with WS. If to access the irregular past form a blocking operation inhibiting the regularly inflected form is required (Pinker 1999), the children with WS may have a lexical system where access is too fast with insufficient editing of responses. The regular past form may then be processed effectively but also elicited where an irregular past form would be more appropriate. A similar mechanism could operate upon the comparatives data presented above. Some of the results concerning lexical skills are not incompatible with a connectionist network within which there is less weight than normal on semantic representations. Such an explanation could account for naming difficulties and possibly for atypical errors and selections in oral fluency. Increased weight on phonological representations might even be able to account for elevated initial letter performance on oral fluency. However, it is not clear why reduced weight on semantic representations would also lead to elevated performance on semantic fluency, nor why performance with verbal concepts (similarities) is so good, nor why naming when accurate would be faster than normal. Modular theories have greater flexibility in providing explanations for sucha range of effects.

5 Reading in WS If lexical retrieval is characterised by fast sloppy selection and semantic specification may be impoverished or atypical, one would predict difficulties in reading development with high rates of paralexias. Delayed reading development in WS, in terms of reading age has been reported in group studies of children and adults (Howlin et al., Davies & Udwin 1998, Udwin, Yule & Martin 1987). There have not yet been any detailed psycholinguistic analyses of reading, nor have there been any group studies of early reading development. Temple (2001) provides a case description of early reading development in one of the cases of WS discussed above which includes an erroranalysis of paralexic responses.

20

On a standard test, the Schonell, Emily has a reading age of 5 years 1 month. In total, across word lists, 361 words were presented for reading aloud, of which 25 were read correctly and 320 induced paralexic errors. The words read aloud correctly were high in frequency and the nouns and adjectives read aloud correctly were highly imageable. Of the overt paralexic errors 51(16%) were semantic paralexias (e.g. queen ! “people”, blue ! “red”, chimney ! “house”, five ! “seven”, garden ! “beach”); 19(6%) were visuo-semantic (e.g. ball! “lead”, stupid ! “silly”, bird ! “bee”, mother ! “mum”, sock ! “mask”) and 17 (5%) were visual+semantic (e.g. shampoo ! “light” [via lamp], floor ! “stupid” [via fool], glass ! “everyone” [via class],shampoo ! “light” [via lamp], cloud ! “naughty” [via loud]).

翻译[10/18]：

在语义系统内部，表示较差或者选择的约束较少，这会早于言语输出词汇层面产生影响，因为它会影响指向反应。这种损伤影响了语义系统的表征或通过快速粗略的访问方式激活这些表征。这一解释也与对威廉姆斯综合症（WS）儿童在屈折形态学研究结果的解释相吻合。如果要访问不规则过去时形式，需要一个阻止操作以抑制规则生成的形式（Pinker, 1999），那么WS患儿可能有一个太快而缺乏充分响应编辑的词库系统。因此，规则过去时形式可能会被有效处理，但在更适合不规则过去时形式的情境下也可能被引发。类似机制可能也适用于上文提到的比较级数据。一些关于词汇技能的研究结果并不排除这样的连接主义网络：其中语义表征的权重低于正常水平。这种解释可以说明命名困难，甚至可能还能解释口语流利度中的非典型错误和选择。增加语音表征的权重甚至可能解释在口语流利度中初始字母表现的提升。然而，尚不清楚为什么语义表征的权重降低也会导致语义流畅性表现提升，以及为什么语言概念（如相似性）的表现如此之好，或者为什么准确命名会比正常情况更快。模块化理论在解释这种广泛效果方面具有更大的灵活性。

5 WS中的阅读
如果词库检索是以快速粗略的选择为特征，并且语义规范可能贫乏或异常，我们预测这种情况下会在阅读发展中出现高比例的读音错误。群体研究表明，在儿童和成人中，WS的阅读发展滞后于其实际年龄（Howlin等人，Davies & Udwin 1998, Udwin, Yule & Martin 1987）。目前还没有详细的阅读心理语言学分析，也没有早期阅读发展的群体研究。Temple (2001) 提供了一个上述病例之一的WS患儿早期阅读发展的个案描述，其中包括对读音错误的分析。

在一个标准测试Schonell中，Emily的阅读年龄为5岁1个月。总共呈现了361个单词供其朗读，其中有25个正确读出，320个引发了读音错误。正确朗读的单词频率较高，正确读出的名词和形容词具有较高的形象性。在明显的读音错误中，有51个（16%）是语义读音错误（例如：queen -> “people”，blue -> “red”，chimney -> “house”，five -> “seven”，garden -> “beach”）；19个（6%）是视觉-语义读音错误（例如：ball -> “lead”，stupid -> “silly”，bird -> “bee”，mother -> “mum”，sock -> “mask”）；17个（5%）是视觉+语义读音错误（例如: shampoo -> “light” [通过lamp]，floor -> “stupid” [通过fool]，glass -> “everyone” [通过class]，shampoo -> “light” [通过lamp]，cloud -> “naughty” [通过loud]）。

原文[11/18]：

Thus in total 27% of errors had a semantic component. Both the error rates for semantic paralexias and for paralexias with a semantic component were significantly higher than the equivalent rates generated by random pairings of stimuli and responses, where only 5% of errors were semantic paralexias and 7.5% in total had a semantic component. They were also significantly higher than the rates reported by Seymour and Elder (1986) for normal beginning readers learning in a scheme emphasising whole words, where ‘phonics’ were not explicitly taught. Even the Seymour and Elder children (1986) have a rate of semantic paralexias of only 2% vs. Emily’s rate of 16%. The reading disorder for which semantic errors are the key characteristic is deep dyslexia (Marshall &Newcombe 1966). There have been few case descriptions of this disorder in children (Johnston 1983, Siegel 1985, Temple 1988, Stuart and Howard 1995). The number of distinct semantic errors (n=50) made by Emily is the highest reported in any of these cases of developmental deep dyslexia. Emily also displays the other characteristics of deep dyslexia. No nonwords can be read aloud correctly and the majority of errors in attempting to read nonwords are lexicalisations. Spelling is also impaired. This pattern of reading development would normally be interpreted as reflecting failure to develop a sublexical phonological reading route or a direct route from print-to-sound with dependence upon a partially established lexico-semantic route, within which a word’s pronunciation is activated only after its meaning is first derived (Coltheart et al. 1980) and this explanation would also apply to Emily Emily was able to name correctly and recognise the spoken names for the majority of items which

21

she read incorrectly. For a subset of items (n=33) data was available from reading, naming, and pointing to a picture from a spoken name, enabling cross-task comparison for the same items. Each of the 33 items generated errors in reading, of which 13 items generated errors with a semantic component. For 28 of the 33 items Emily was able to name the item correctly and for 26 of them she could recognise the spoken name by selecting the matching picture from 23 semantically related distracters. Of the 13 items which generated errors with a semantic component in reading, 10 were named correctly from pictures. The semantic errors cannot therefore be attributed to absence of semantic specification for the item nor to any generalised difficulty with lexical production of the item name. Activation of only partial semantic features may have occurred so that incorrect lexical entries were activated, an interpretation consistent with fast sloppy access in reading as well as in naming. However, despite the anomia discussed above, sloppy access to lexical entries appears to arise in reading to an even greater degree than in naming, since semantic paralexias are generated even to those items which can be read or understood correctly. The pattern of lexical access appears to differ in degree dependent upon the modality of input (written words vs. pictures). However the qualitative pattern of the impairment is very similar. It is of interest in relation to the issues discussed above, that Emily is able to do successfully a number of both implicit and explicit phonological processing tasks and there is no evidence of impairment here in relation to mental age. Emily can also sound 16/26 letters of the alphabet. Yet she seems unable to use this skill and her other explicit phonological skills to stop the production of semantic errors. Thus, for example, Emily can sound out all the component letters of the word friend, except for the letter e. Yet, when asked to read the word friend aloud, she says “boy”. This pattern of performance strengthens the argument for modular impairments and the independence during development of the lexico-semantic reading route and the phonological reading route, within which the grapheme-phoneme skills, reflected by the ability to sound out letters, are processed. Basic initial phonological skills have been mastered but they cannot be used in the lexico-semantic domain. There is certainly no evidence that they impinge upon or constrain thelexico-semantic skills in any way.

The form of some semantic errors, for example, a tendency to say “people” for living things,

22

whether animals or actual people, supports the view that there may be difficulty in activating lower nodes in a hierarchical structure. In similar fashion, problems with irregularly inflected word forms may reflect restricted activation or representation of lower nodes within morphological structures. 6. Discussion In this section, we will summarise the main findings and discuss them with respect to the current general controversy between modular and non-modular accounts of WS. We will also briefly mention results on face recognition in children with WS to show that the selective impairments wefound in their language extend beyond the linguistic domain.

当然，以下是该段落的中文翻译：

因此，总计有27%的错误包含语义成分。无论是语义性错词还是包含语义成分的错词的错误率都显著高于随机配对刺激和反应所产生的错误率，在随机配对中只有5%的错误是语义性错词，总共有7.5%的错误包含语义成分。这些错误率也显著高于Seymour和Elder（1986）报告的在强调整个单词的教学方案中学习的正常初学者的错误率，该方案中未明确教授“语音”。即使在Seymour和Elder（1986）的研究中，儿童的语义性错词发生率也只有2%，而Emily的发生率为16%。以语义错误为主要特征的阅读障碍是深层失读症（Marshall & Newcombe 1966）。关于儿童中这种障碍的病例描述很少（Johnston 1983, Siegel 1985, Temple 1988, Stuart and Howard 1995）。Emily所犯的独特语义错误（n=50）是迄今为止在所有发展性深层失读症病例中最高的。Emily还表现出深层失读症的其他特征。她无法正确地大声朗读任何伪词，并且在尝试朗读伪词时产生的错误主要是词汇化错误。拼写能力也受损。通常，这种阅读发展模式被解释为未能发展出亚词汇层面的语音阅读路径或直接从印刷文字到声音的路径，而是依赖于部分建立的词汇-语义路径，在这条路径中，一个词的发音只有在其意义首先被激活后才能被激活（Coltheart et al. 1980），这种解释也适用于Emily。Emily能够正确命名并识别大部分她读错的项目的口语名称。

对于一组项目（n=33），从阅读、命名和根据听到的名称指出图片等方面可以获得数据，从而可以对相同项目进行跨任务比较。在这33个项目中，每个项目都在阅读过程中产生了错误，其中有13个项目生成了包含语义成分的错误。在这33个项目中，Emily能够正确命名28个物品，并且能够通过从23个语义相关干扰项中选择匹配的图片来识别26个物品的口语名称。在产生包含语义成分错误的13个项目中，有10个项目能够从图片中正确命名。因此，这些语义错误不能归因于缺乏语义表征或一般的词汇产生困难。可能只激活了部分语义特征，从而导致了不正确的词汇条目的激活，这种解释与阅读和命名中的快速粗糙访问一致。然而，尽管上面讨论过的失名现象，但在阅读中，词汇条目的粗糙访问似乎比命名更加严重，因为即使是那些能够正确阅读或理解的项目也会产生语义性错词。词汇访问模式似乎取决于输入模态的不同（书面单词与图片），但损伤的质性模式非常相似。有趣的是，就上述问题而言，Emily能够在一些隐性和显性的语音处理任务中取得成功，并且在这方面没有相对于心智年龄的受损迹象。Emily还能拼读字母表中的16/26个字母。然而，她似乎无法利用这项技能及其他显性的语音技能来阻止语义错误的产生。例如，Emily能够拼读单词friend的所有组成字母，除了字母e。然而，当被要求朗读单词friend时，她说出了“男孩”。这种行为模式加强了模块化损伤以及词汇-语义阅读路径和发展中的语音阅读路径独立性的论点，其中图-音技能反映了拼读字母的能力。基本的初始语音技能已经被掌握，但是它们无法在词汇-语义领域中使用。没有任何证据表明它们对词汇-语义技能有任何影响或约束。

某些语义错误的形式，例如倾向于将活物称为“人”，无论它们是动物还是实际上的人，支持了可能存在激活层次结构中较低节点的困难这一观点。类似地，形态结构中不规则屈折形式的问题可能反映了较低节点的激活或表征受限。

讨论
在本节中，我们将总结主要发现，并就目前关于威廉姆斯综合症（Williams Syndrome, WS）模块化与非模块化解释之间的争议进行讨论。我们还将简要提及WS儿童面部识别的结果，以说明我们在他们的语言方面发现的选择性损伤超出了语言领域。

原文[12/18]：

Summarising the results on morphological skills, it was found that children with WS excessively overapply –ed past tense, -s plural and –er comparative formation and that they perform worse than controls on lexically constrained inflection, such as irregular past tense and plural forms and on exceptions to –er comparative formation. This was interpreted as a selective lexical deficit in which children with WS have difficulty retrieving or accessing inflected word forms which are stored in memory (as subnodes of complex lexical entries). Combinatorial operations, on the other hand, are unaffected enabling high scores for accuracy on regular inflection and frequent use ofovergeneralizations.

In processing base lexical items, comprehension of spoken words involving the activation of semantic representations is effective where general information is required and there are few similar competing responses in forced choice arrays. However when fine grain semantic knowledge is required to distinguish the item for multiple others from the same semantic class, performance is significantly poorer than controls. Thus error rates in naming are high and errors have fewer semantic features in common with targets than normal. Performance is significantly enhanced on oral fluency where access to the general semantic field of the entry is all that is required. Access in naming highly familiar items is also faster than normal. The results were interpreted as indicating fast sloppy access with enhanced skills where only partial activation of semantic specification is required but impaired skill where a more detailed representation musthave been established and must be available.

23

The pattern of early reading development in one case of WS was that of deep dyslexia. The form of some semantic errors, for example, a tendency to say “people” for living things, whether animals or actual people (e.g. fish ! “people”, dog ! “people”, queen ! “people”, daddy ! “people”), supports the view that there may be difficulty in activating lower nodes in a hierarchical structure. Non-words could not be read, though some letters could be sounded. The impairment was interpreted as reflecting absence of a direct reading route, and dependency upon an impoverished lexico-semantic route which appears disconnected from information about letter-sounds within the phonological reading route.

Modular vs. non-modular accounts A connectionist account of WS has been proposed by Thomas and Karmiloff-Smith (1999). However, it has been demonstrated above that this explanation is inadequate in accounting for the morphological results on past tense formation, compounding and comparatives. It also appears unable to account for either the distinction in lexico-semantic skill dependent on the task demands outlined above or the disconnection of phonological information from lexico-semantic selection inreading.

In contrast a modular account of these results with WS argues for difficulty in storing or activating subnodes and subentries of lexical representations for inflected word forms, and difficulty in activating or storing distant subnodes specifying fine-grain semantic information within lexico semantic entries, with intact combinatorial and rule-governed skills in forming morphologically complex words and enhanced speed and effectiveness of lexical access when only general semantic specification is required. In early reading development the impaired lexico-semantic access, which triggers semantic paralexias, is combined only with letter sound knowledge in thephonological domain.

翻译[12/18]：

形态技能结果总结

在形态技能的结果总结中，发现威廉姆斯综合症（WS）的儿童过度使用了-ed 过去时、-s 复数和-er 比较级的形成，并且他们在词汇受限的词形变化（如不规则过去时和复数形式）以及-er 比较级形成中的例外情况上表现比对照组差。这被解释为一种选择性词汇缺陷，其中具有 WS 的儿童难以检索或访问存储在记忆中的屈折词形（作为复杂词汇条目的子节点）。另一方面，组合操作未受影响，使得他们在规则词形变化上得分较高，并频繁使用过度泛化。

基础词汇项处理

在处理基础词汇项时，涉及语义表征激活的口语词理解在需要一般信息且强制选择阵列中相似竞争反应较少时是有效的。然而，当需要精细的语义知识来区分同一语义类别中的多个其他项目时，表现显著劣于对照组。因此，命名的错误率很高，且错误与目标的共有语义特征比正常情况下少。在只需访问词条的一般语义领域即可提升口语流畅性的任务中，表现显著增强。对高度熟悉的项目的命名访问也比正常情况下更快。研究结果被解释为快速但粗略的访问，在只需部分激活语义规范的任务中表现出色，但在需要更详细表征的任务中表现受损。

早期阅读发展模式

在一例 WS 中，早期阅读发展的模式呈现出深度阅读障碍。某些语义错误的形式，例如倾向于将生物（无论是动物还是实际的人）说成“人”（例如 fish → “people”，dog → “people”，queen → “people”，daddy → “people”），支持了可能存在激活层级结构中较低节点困难的观点。非词不能被阅读，虽然一些字母可以发音。这种损害被解释为直接阅读路径缺失的表现，并依赖于一条贫乏的词汇-语义路径，该路径似乎与语音阅读路径中的字母-声音信息断开。

模块化与非模块化解释

Thomas 和 Karmiloff-Smith（1999）提出了关于 WS 的联结主义解释。然而，上述内容已经表明，该解释不足以解释过去时形成、复合词和比较级的形态学结果。它也无法解释根据上述任务需求的词汇-语义技能差异，或者在阅读中的语音信息与词汇-语义选择之间的断开。

相比之下，关于这些结果的模块化解释认为 WS 患者在存储或激活屈折词形的词典表示的子节点和子条目方面存在困难，而在激活或存储词汇-语义条目中指定精细语义信息的远处子节点方面也存在困难，而组合能力和规则驱动的形成复杂词形的技能完好无损。在只需要一般语义规范的情况下，词汇访问的速度和效率得到了提高。在早期阅读发展中，受损的词汇-语义访问引发了语义错读，仅与语音领域的字母-声音知识结合。

非语言领域的模块化损伤

认为 WS 的表现模式不需要联结主义解释的论点也扩展到了非语言领域。最近有关面部识别的讨论表明…

原文[13/18]：

processing in WS, where it has also been argued that the pattern of development is completely different from normal, resulting from different underlying processes, which cannot be explained in terms of a normal brain with “parts intact and parts impaired” (Karmiloff-Smith 1997). In some of the earlier studies of WS, face processing was a skill argued to have developed well in WS. The evidence for this was based upon their performance on Benton’s Facial Recognition Task (BFRT), where accuracy was at normal levels (Bellugi et al. 1994). This task requires the matching of black and white, partially shadowed, photographs of faces. In the earlier part of the test the photographs to be matched are identical and in the latter part the target photograph has to be matched to three others of the same person, taken from a different angle. However, despite the name of the task, the face itself does not have to be recognised in terms of identified as a specific individual. A detailed feature based analysis, for example, where particular characteristics of a nose or eyes were matched, could be enough to perform well with these items. More detailed investigation of face processing in WS (Karmiloff Smith 1997, Deruelle et al. 1999) reveals that a feature based or componential analysis, dependent on the use of local cues in faces, such as the shape of individual elements within the face, is the mode which can be employed successfully by subjects with WS. This strategy is effective on some tasks but not in others. In contrast, more holistic configural processing of faces appears to be impaired in WS (Deruelle et al. 1999, Karmiloff-Smith 1997). It is notable in the description of both Deruelle et al. (1999) and Karmiloff-Smith (1997) that in the processing of faces with local cues, performance of children with WS is comparable to mental age. Thus Deruelle et al. (1999) indicate “they did not differ from normal in the number of local errors they made”; in Karmiloff-Smith’s (1977) figure 2, 90 95% of componential processing of faces is correct for both children with WS and controls. Scores “were high on those items allowing componential processing”. It is only in the configural processing that performance is abnormal, indeed at a chance level on the Karmiloff-Smith (1977) analysis. Thus, what we see in WS is normal ability on face processing tasks for which local componential cues are effective and impaired ability on tasks requiring configural skill. Normal children and adults can perform both local and configural analyses of faces successfully. Children with WS are accurate only the former. In terms of the normal brain, componential processing is

25

intact and configural processing is impaired, a potentially straightforward modular dissociation within face processing systems. There has been a long established recognition of these two contributory processes to face recognition, with the configural processing of the interrelationship of features, often considered to have a right hemisphere substrate in humans, whilst the feature based componential analysis is largely the province of the left hemisphere (e.g. Bradshaw & Mattingley 1995). A different mix of these processes may be necessary for normal recognition of familiar faces in comparison to matching or discriminating unfamiliar faces (Bradshaw & Mattingley 1995). For those normal skills dependent upon the configural processes, the subjectswith WS will be impaired.

7 Conclusion A recurrent theme in discussions of developmental abnormality is whether the pattern of performance reflects delay or deviance. Where delayed the pattern is that of the normal child at a different developmental stage. Where deviant the pattern differs from normal developmental stages. If deviant, there is then a further recurrent theme of debate about whether the deviance reflects a distinct system to normal. This could for example be a completely altered system, with generalised differences from normal, as in Thomas and Karmiloff-Smith’s account of WS. In this case, the information that can be learnt about normal function from the study of the deviance is restricted, as the deviant system does not reflect the normal system. In cognitive neuropsychological terms the assumption of transparency is violated (Ellis & Young 1988, Temple 1997a, b). However, within modular theories, the deviance may reflect the architecture of the normal system but with selective components of this system under or over-developed or operating atypically. It is the later interpretation that we find most parsimonious in accounting for the data inWS.

The argument for a pattern of deviance rather than delay is made on the basis that the children with WS display patterns of performance which normal children do not display at any age. For example, as discussed above, in WS regular plurals can freely occur in compounds, whereas normal children produce irregular plurals in compounds but avoid regular ones. This avoidance is

翻译[13/18]：

在威廉斯综合症（WS）的处理中，有观点认为其发展模式与正常情况完全不同，这种差异源于不同的潜在过程，而这不能用“部分完好、部分受损”的正常大脑来解释（Karmiloff-Smith, 1997）。在一些早期研究中，面部处理技能被认为在WS患者中发展得较好。这一观点的依据是他们在Benton面部识别任务（BFRT）中的表现，其准确率达到了正常水平（Bellugi et al., 1994）。该任务要求将黑白且部分阴影的照片进行匹配。测试的前半部分，需要匹配的照片是完全相同的，而在后半部分，目标照片则需要与三张同一人但拍摄角度不同的其他照片进行匹配。然而，尽管这项任务名为面部识别，但实际上并不需要识别具体的个体。一种基于详细特征的分析方法，例如，匹配鼻子或眼睛的具体特征，就足够完成这些项目。对WS中面部处理的更详细研究表明，基于特征或成分的分析方法——依赖于脸部局部线索（如脸内部件的形状）——是可以被WS患者成功使用的模式（Karmiloff-Smith, 1997；Deruelle et al., 1999）。这种策略在某些任务上有效，但在其他任务上则不然。相反，更整体配置性的面部处理方式在WS中似乎受到了损害（Deruelle et al., 1999；Karmiloff-Smith, 1997）。

值得注意的是，在Deruelle等人（1999）和Karmiloff-Smith（1997）的描述中，依靠局部线索进行面部处理时，WS儿童的表现与他们的智龄相匹配。因此，Deruelle等人（1999）指出，“他们在局部错误的数量上与正常儿童没有区别”；而在Karmiloff-Smith（1977）的图2中，对于WS儿童和对照组，90-95%的基于成分的面部处理是正确的。“在允许基于成分处理的项目上分数很高。” 只有在构形处理任务上的表现才异常，事实上，在Karmiloff-Smith（1977）的分析中，表现处于随机水平。因此，我们在WS中看到的是，当局部成分线索有效时，面孔处理任务的能力是正常的，而在需要配置性技能的任务上则是受损的。正常儿童和成人都可以成功进行局部和配置性分析，而WS儿童只在前者上准确无误。在正常大脑中，基于成分的处理是完好的，而基于配置的处理是受损的，这可能是一种面部处理系统内的直接模块化分离。人们很早就认识到，这两种过程对面部识别都有贡献，其中，特征之间关系的配置性处理通常被认为是在人类右半脑完成的，而基于特征的成分分析则主要在左半脑（例如，Bradshaw & Mattingley, 1995）。正常情况下，识别熟悉的面孔与匹配或区分不熟悉的面孔所需的过程组合可能会有所不同（Bradshaw & Mattingley, 1995）。对于那些依赖于配置性过程的正常技能，WS患者将会受到损害。

结论

在讨论发育异常时，一个反复出现的主题是，性能模式反映的是迟缓还是偏离。如果是迟缓，则模式对应于不同发育阶段的正常儿童。如果是偏离，则该模式与正常发育阶段不同。如果是偏离，那么进一步讨论的主题通常是偏离是否反映了与正常系统不同的独特系统。例如，可以是一个完全改变的系统，与正常情况有很大的整体差异，如Thomas和Karmiloff-Smith对WS的描述。在这种情况下，从偏离的研究中获得关于正常功能的信息受到限制，因为偏离系统并不反映正常系统。从认知神经心理学的角度来看，透明性假设被违反了（Ellis & Young, 1988；Temple, 1997a, b）。然而，在模块理论中，偏离可能反映了正常系统的结构，但其某些组成部分可能会发生选择性地欠发达或过度发达，或者以非常规的方式运作。我们认为，解释WS数据的最简洁解释是后者。

主张偏离而非迟缓的观点基于这样一个事实：WS儿童表现出的一些行为模式在任何年龄段的正常儿童中都不存在。例如，正如上面所讨论的，WS儿童可以在复合词中自由使用规则复数形式，而正常儿童则会在复合词中使用不规则复数形式，却避免使用规则复数形式。这种避讳是：

26

原文[14/18]：

a characteristic of all ages and the production and response to regular plurals in WS is not a feature of any normal developmental stage. Similarly, the children with WS relied almost exclusively on – er comparative formation and heavily overapplied –er without any obvious restriction, a pattern of performance that differs from that of unimpaired children in any of the age groups tested. The production of atypical responses in naming and oral fluency is also not a feature of any normal developmental stage. Indeed, although as children get older their knowledge of such low frequency words increases the proportion of these produced in fluency tasks actually reduces rather than increasing (Temple et al. 2001) so that the elevated proportions of these responses in WS is alsoatypical in comparisons to older children.

On the other hand, there is no data which suggest that the structure of the underlying architecture is different from normal or that there are any new modular components which are not seen in normal children or evidence of distinct patterns of interconnections between modules, which differ from normal. Instead, the deviant behavioural patterns can be explained in terms of selective deficits of an otherwise normal modular system. Thus in the construction of morphological forms the children with WS are able to form -ed past tense forms, –s plurals –er comparative adjectives, but they have difficulty with the lexical exceptions. In literacy, letters could be sounded but this phonological ability did not contribute to the recognition of words. Words were read via a lexico semantic reading system within which, a phonological output representation could only be triggered subsequent to the activation of meaning. Even in the non-linguistic domain of face recognition, the impairment in WS is modular. They can do well when componential processing of faces is required, whereas configural processing of faces is problematic.

翻译[14/18]：

以下是对您提供内容的中文翻译：

所有年龄段的一个特征是，在威廉斯综合症（WS）中产生和回应规则复数形式并不是任何正常发展阶段的特征。同样，患有WS的儿童在形成比较级时几乎完全依赖于-er后缀，并且在没有任何明显限制的情况下大量使用-er，这种表现模式与任何年龄组未受损儿童的表现模式不同。在命名和口语流利性任务中产生非典型反应也不是任何正常发育阶段的特征。实际上，尽管随着孩子年龄的增长，他们对低频词汇的知识逐渐增加，但在流利性任务中产生的这些词汇的比例实际上是减少而不是增加（Temple等人，2001），因此在WS中较高比例的这种反应与较大年龄的孩子相比也是非典型的。

另一方面，没有数据表明潜在架构的结构与正常情况有所不同，也没有发现任何新的模块化组件，这些组件在正常儿童中未见或与其他模块之间的连接模式有别于正常情况。相反，偏离的行为模式可以用一个原本正常的模块化系统的特定缺陷来解释。因此，在构造形态形式时，患有WS的儿童能够形成-ed过去时形式、-s复数形式和-er形容词比较级，但他们难以处理词汇例外情况。在识字能力方面，字母可以被读出音，但这种语音能力并未贡献到单词识别。单词通过词汇语义阅读系统被识别，在其中，语音输出表征只能在意义激活之后才能触发。即使是非语言领域如面部识别，在WS中的障碍也是模块化的。当需要成分加工面孔时，他们可以做得很好，而对面孔的配置加工则存在问题。

唐氏综合征

GPT-Academic Report

# Title:

The understanding of complex syntax in children with Down syndrome [version 2; referees: 3 approved]

# Abstract:

Down syndrome (DS) is associated with poor language skills that Background: seem disproportionate to general nonverbal ability, but the nature and causes of this deficit are unclear. We assessed how individuals with DS understand complex linguistic constructions, and considered how cognitive ability and memory and impact the ability of those with DS to process these sentence types. There were three groups participating in the study: children with DS Methods: (n = 33) and two control groups composed of children with cognitive impairment of unknown aetiology (CI) (n = 32) and children with typical development (n = 33). The three groups did not differ on raw scores on a test of non-verbal cognitive ability. Using a newly devised animation task, we examined how well individuals with DS (n = 33) could understand relative clauses, complement clauses and adverbial clauses compared to children with CI and typically developing controls. Participants also completed the Test for the Reception of Grammar-2, three measures of memory (forward and backward digit recall, visuo-spatial memory) and a hearing screen. Results indicated that (1) with the exception of intransitive subject Results: relative clauses, children with DS performed at floor on all other complex sentences, (2) they performed at a significantly lower level than both control groups, and (3) DS status accounted for a significant proportion of the variance over and above memory skills. Our findings suggest that children with DS have a Conclusions: disproportionate difficulty understanding complex sentences compared to two control groups matched on mental age. Furthermore, their understanding of syntax is not completely explained by poor cognitive or memory skills, rather it appears to be a specific deficit that may distinguish children with DS from other neurodevelopmental disorders.

# Meta Translation

当然，以下是题目和摘要的中文翻译：

题目：唐氏综合症儿童对复杂句法的理解 [版本2；审稿人：3位批准]

作者：Pauline Frizelle; Paul A Thompson; Mihaela Duta; Dorothy V M Bishop; Christopher Jarrold; L Abbeduto

摘要：
唐氏综合症（DS）常伴随语言技能较差的问题，这种问题似乎与一般的非言语能力不成比例，但其性质和原因尚不清楚。本研究评估了患有DS的人如何理解复杂的语言结构，并探讨了认知能力和记忆如何影响他们处理这类句子的能力。研究中有三组参与者：患有DS的儿童（n = 33）以及两组对照组，一组是由原因不明的认知障碍（CI）儿童组成（n = 32），另一组则是典型的发育儿童（n = 33）。这三组在非言语认知能力测试的原始分数上没有差异。利用新设计的动画任务，我们考察了DS儿童（n = 33）理解和处理定语从句、补语从句和状语从句的情况，并与CI组和典型发展的对照组进行了比较。参与者还完成了《语法接受测试-2》、三个记忆测验（正向和反向数字回忆、视觉空间记忆）和听力筛查。结果显示：(1) 除了不及物主语定语从句外，DS儿童在所有其他复杂句子类型上表现达到了最低水平；(2) 他们的表现显著低于两个对照组；(3) DS状态解释了很大一部分变量，这超过了记忆技能的影响。我们的发现表明，与两个与其心智年龄匹配的对照组相比，DS儿童理解复杂句子时存在不成比例的困难。此外，他们对句法的理解并不能完全归因于较差的认知或记忆技能，而更可能是一种特定的缺陷，这可以将DS儿童与其他神经发育障碍区分开来。

# Introduction

Down syndrome (DS) is the most common genetic cause of intellectual disability. A diagnosis of DS is given when an error in cell development results in an extra copy of chromosome 21, so there are 47 chromosomes rather than the usual 46. DS can also be the result of mosaicism, when only some cells include an extra copy of this chromosome, or translocation, when part of chromosome 21 attaches to another chromosome.
The majority of individuals with DS have a moderate intellectual disability (Chapman & Hesketh, 2001); however, IQ scores can span from the severe to the average range (Roizen, 2007). Language difficulties in children with DS are well documented, particularly those affecting vocabulary, phonology, morphology, and simple sentence structures (Dodd & Thomspson, 2001;Eadie et al., 2002;Laws & Bishop, 2003;Price et al., 2007). However, information regarding these children’s understanding of complex syntax is very limited. In addition, although children with DS have increased risk of a number of difficulties likely to influence their language development (involving limited cognitive ability, hearing level and memory skills) the relationship between these factors and language competence is not straightforward and has never been investigated in relation to the complex syntactic abilities of this population. We aim to address this gap in the literature.
Our previous research has shown that children’s performance on language comprehension tests can be heavily influenced by task demands (Frizelle et al., 2017). Previous studies have tended to use multiple-choice tasks that have a heavy cognitive load and make demands beyond the linguistic. Given that people with DS have a cognitive impairment, we anticipated that these tasks may underestimate their comprehension abilities. For the current study, we used a novel method of assessment, designed to minimize non-linguistic demands. We hypothesised that this may reveal a greater level of syntactic understanding than when using a traditional multiple-choice format.

唐氏综合症（DS）是智力障碍最常见的遗传原因。当细胞发育过程中出现错误，导致第21号染色体多出一个拷贝，从而使染色体总数从通常的46条增加到47条时，就会被诊断为DS。DS也可能是由于镶嵌现象引起的，即只有部分细胞包含额外的21号染色体拷贝，或者由于易位，即21号染色体的一部分附着在另一条染色体上。

大多数DS患者存在中度智力障碍（Chapman & Hesketh, 2001）；然而，智商分数可以从重度障碍到平均范围不等（Roizen, 2007）。DS儿童的语言困难有充分的文献记载，尤其是那些影响词汇、音韵、形态和简单句子结构的问题（Dodd & Thompson, 2001; Eadie et al., 2002; Laws & Bishop, 2003; Price et al., 2007）。然而，关于这些儿童对复杂句法理解的信息却非常有限。此外，尽管DS儿童在认知能力、听力水平和记忆力方面存在一定缺陷，这些因素可能会影响他们的语言发展，但这些因素与语言能力之间的关系并不简单，并且从未在涉及这一人群的复杂句法能力方面进行过研究。我们旨在填补这一文献空白。

我们之前的研究表明，儿童在语言理解测试中的表现可以受到任务需求的严重影响（Frizelle et al., 2017）。以前的研究倾向于使用多重选择题任务，这些任务需要较高的认知负担，并且超越了纯粹的语言要求。鉴于DS患者存在认知障碍，我们预计这些任务可能会低估他们的理解能力。在本研究中，我们使用了一种新颖的评估方法，旨在最小化非语言性需求。我们假设这种方法可能会比传统的多重选择题形式揭示更高的句法理解水平。

# Complex syntax

The term ‘complex sentence’ is used to refer to constructions that have more than one clause, linked in specific ways. This can be done through co-ordination (using connectors such as and or but) or subordination, where there is a main clause in which an element is embedded or expanded into a subordinate clause. Subordination is of particular interest as it allows for the expression of thoughts that involve hierarchical relationships between ideas, rather than just chaining them together. There are three distinct types of subordinate clause; complement clauses, adverbial clauses and relative clauses, and all three are the focus of the current paper. Examples of each clause type are given in Table 3. Complement clauses are the earliest developing form of complex sentence (Diessel, 2004) and are often used with mental state verbs such as know and think. In a complement clause, the embedded sentence serves as one of the arguments of the verb in the matrix clause (Quirk et al., 1985). The complement clause can therefore be the subject, object or indirect object of the main verb. In this paper we are concerned with complements that serve as the object of the main clause. In adverbial constructions the two clauses are linked semantically, most commonly using temporal (e.g. when) or causal (e.g. because) connectives. Finally, a relative clause serves to post-modify the noun in the main clause. They are usually defined according to (a) the sentential position of the modified noun phrase and (b) the role of the relativized noun phrase in the embedded clause. In this study, in keeping with children’s early production of relative clauses (see Diessel, 2004), we focused on relatives that modify the main clause object. In addition, we included relative clauses, where the relativized noun phrase realizes a range of syntactic roles, such as subject, object, oblique and indirect object.

复杂句法

术语“复杂句子”用来指那些包含多个由特定方式连接的从句的结构。这可以通过并列（使用诸如“和”或“但”之类的连接词）或从属来实现，在从属中，有一个主句，其中的一个元素被嵌入或扩展为一个从属从句。从属结构特别有趣，因为它允许表达涉及思想之间层次关系的想法，而不仅仅是将它们简单地依次排列。有三种不同类型的从属从句：补语从句、状语从句和关系从句，本文将重点讨论这三种类型。每种从句类型的示例见表3。

补语从句是最早发展的复杂句子形式（Diessel, 2004），常与心理状态动词（如“知道”和“认为”）一起使用。在补语从句中，嵌入从句作为主句动词的一个论元（Quirk et al., 1985）。因此，补语从句可以成为主句的主要动词的主语、宾语或间接宾语。在本文中，我们关注的是作为主句宾语的补语从句。

在状语从句结构中，两个从句通过语义上的联系最为常见，最常用的时间（例如“当”）或因果（例如“因为”）连接词来连接。最后，关系从句用于对主句中的名词进行后修饰。它们通常根据（a）被修饰名词短语在句中的位置和（b）被关系化的名词短语在嵌入从句中的角色来定义。在本研究中，与儿童早期产生关系从句的情况一致（参见Diessel, 2004），我们重点关注修饰主句宾语的关系从句。此外，我们还包括了各种句法角色的关系从句，例如主语、宾语、斜格和间接宾语。

# Language characteristics of children with DS

The characteristic profile of language abilities in those with DS suggests that receptive language is typically better than expressive language (Chapman et al., 2002;Laws & Bishop, 2003) and that vocabulary is stronger than syntax. The latter is evident in both receptive and expressive modalities (Abbeduto et al., 2003;Berglund et al., 2001;Chapman et al., 1991).
Much of the work in relation to syntax has focussed on expressive language and primarily on spontaneous language production. Given the marked differences between children with DS and their age-matched peer group, it is customary to compare their language profiles with that of younger, typically developing (TD) children. This makes it possible to see whether language development is merely following a typical, but markedly delayed, course, or whether there is a distinctive profile with strengths and weaknesses in specific aspects of language. Individuals with DS have been reported to produce fewer complex noun phrases, verb phrases, sentence structures, questions and negations than TD individuals of a similar non-verbal age (Price et al., 2008). A limited production of passives has also been reported

唐氏综合症儿童的语言特征

具有唐氏综合症（DS）的个体的语言能力特征表明，他们的接受性语言通常优于表达性语言（Chapman et al., 2002; Laws & Bishop, 2003），并且词汇能力比句法更强。后者在接收性和表达性两种模式中都表现明显（Abbeduto et al., 2003; Berglund et al., 2001; Chapman et al., 1991）。

关于句法的大部分研究集中在表达性语言上，特别是自发语言的产生。鉴于唐氏综合症儿童与同龄普通儿童之间存在显著差异，通常会将他们的语言特征与年龄较小的正常发育（TD）儿童进行比较。这使得我们能够判断语言发展是否仅仅是沿着典型的但明显延迟的路径进行，或者是否存在某种特定的轮廓，其中包含某些语言方面的强项和弱项。据报道，与相同非语言年龄的正常个体相比，患有DS的个体较少产生复杂的名词短语、动词短语、句子结构、疑问句和否定句（Price et al., 2008）。被动句的生成也较有限。

# Amendments from Version 1 Part-1

The main differences between this version and our original submission are as follows:
• A Table labelling error with respect to examples of sentences used in TECS-E
• An expansion of the literature review to include work by Christodoulou & Grohmann (2018) • More discussion of the ‘yes’ bias in children’s responses
• Clarification regarding when we refer to mental age we are referring to a non-verbal measure
• Clarification regarding: 1) the use of visuo-spatial STM in the method as a positive control; 2) the complexities involved in working memory; and 3) how we have used the backward digit span task
• References to our previous work explaining why we consider TECS-E to be a less demanding cognitive task.
• The addition of: 1) full statistical details for regressions 1 and 2 including the constant value; and 2) Cronbachs alpha as a measure of internal consistency See referee reports (Bridges & Smith, 1984;Fowler, 1990;Ring & Clahsen, 2005). In relation to complex syntax specifically, Thordardottir et al. (2002) analysed 12-minute narrative samples from 24 adolescents with DS (mean age 16.5 years) and a control group of younger TD children matched on mean length of utterance (MLU). Co-ordinated sentences, clausal complements and relative clauses were all noted in the narrative samples, with no significant differences between the groups in either the proportion or the diversity of complex sentences used. However, Thordartottir and colleagues did highlight the degree of variability in the group with DS.
More recently, Christodoulou & Grohmann (2018) reported on the comprehension of syntactically complex subjunctives (e.g. The cat wants to dance) in 30 Greek Cypriot bilectal adolescents with DS. Using an act out priming task followed by a picture selection task they found a high rate of comprehension accuracy in their DS participants and posit that their results contradict previous suggestions of an overall syntactic impairment in people with DS. However, a close look at the distractor items suggests that the participants could respond correctly by understanding key words in the sentence and did not need to understand the complex syntax i.e. for the sentence above, from an array of 4 pictures there was only one image depicting a cat dancing, therefore if the participant understands the words ‘cat’ and ‘dance’ they are likely to choose the correct picture.
Other studies have reported deficits in syntactic comprehension in individuals with DS, (see Fortunato-Tavares et al., 2015;Michael et al., 2012;Perovic, 2006;Ring & Clahsen, 2005) however, the range of structures investigated is narrow and complex syntax has been given little or no attention. When complex syntax is involved, it has been in the context of standardized measures, in which different syntactic structures (both simple and complex) are grouped together and a composite score is reported (for example using The Test for Auditory Comprehension of Language-Revised (TACL-R) (Carrow-Woolfolk, 1985) or the Test for the Reception of Grammar (TROG-2) (Bishop, 2003). It is, accordingly, not possible to tease out the potential contribution of the complex constructions included in these tests to the scores achieved。

修正版本1的部分-1

此版本与我们最初的提交相比，主要差异如下：

  • 修改了TECS-E中例句的表格标记错误。
  • 扩展了文献综述，包括Christodoulou和Grohmann（2018）的研究。
  • 对儿童回答中的“是”偏误进行了更多讨论。
  • 明确指出当我们提到心理年龄时，指的是非言语测验的结果。
  • 对方法部分进行了澄清：1）使用视觉空间短期记忆作为阳性对照；2）工作记忆的复杂性；以及3）如何使用逆向数字广度任务。
  • 引用了我们的前期研究，解释为什么我们认为TECS-E是一项认知要求较低的任务。
  • 添加了以下内容：1）回归分析1和2的完整统计细节，包括常数项；2）用Cronbach’s alpha作为内部一致性度量。

详见审稿报告（Bridges & Smith, 1984; Fowler, 1990; Ring & Clahsen, 2005）。具体到复杂的句法结构，Thordardottir等人（2002）分析了来自24名DS青少年（平均年龄16.5岁）和匹配MLU（平均语段长度）的年轻TD儿童对照组的12分钟叙事样本。在这些叙事样本中，出现了协调句、子句补语和关系从句，两组之间在使用这些复杂句子的比例和多样性方面没有显著差异。然而，Thordartottir及其同事确实强调了DS组内存在较大的变异性。

最近，Christodoulou和Grohmann（2018）报道了30名讲希腊语和塞浦路斯双语的DS青少年对语法复杂条件从句（例如“The cat wants to dance”）的理解情况。通过使用动作表演启动任务和图片选择任务，他们发现DS参与者有很高的理解准确率，并认为他们的结果反驳了先前关于DS患者普遍存在句法障碍的观点。然而，仔细观察干扰项表明，参与者只需理解句子中的关键词就能正确回答，而不一定要理解复杂句法。例如，在上述句子中，从四张图片中选择只有一张猫跳舞的图片，所以只要参与者理解“cat”和“dance”，就很可能会选择正确的图片。

其他一些研究报道了DS个体在句法理解方面的缺陷（参见Fortunato-Tavares等人，2015；Michael等人，2012；Perovic，2006；Ring & Clahsen，2005），但所研究的结构范围较窄，且很少或不关注复杂句法。当涉及复杂句法时，通常是标准化测试的一部分，在这些测试中，不同句法结构（简单和复杂）被组合在一起并报告综合得分（例如使用“语言听觉理解能力修订版测试”(TACL-R) (Carrow-Woolfolk, 1985) 或“语法接受测验”(TROG-2) (Bishop, 2003)）。因此，无法明确区分这些测试中包含的复杂结构对获得分数的潜在贡献。

# Amendments from Version 1 Part-2

In addition, we have found that children’s performance on language comprehension tests can be heavily influenced by the specific demands of the assessment method employed (Frizelle et al., 2017). The format used in the TACL-R and TROG-2 is the traditional multiple-choice sentence picture-matching presentation, where the goal is to select from an array the picture that matches a spoken sentence. The other images are distractors that represent alternative interpretations of the sentence and the child is required to rule them out in order to respond correctly. These competing interpretations are presented so that only children with a deep understanding of the construction will chose the correct item. However, this format is likely to lead to children failing for reasons other than a lack of linguistic knowledge. In particular, it can disadvantage children (such as those with DS) who are inattentive and impulsive, and those who do not appreciate the need to scan the array carefully to choose between similar-looking items. We developed a new test (TECS-E: Test of Complex Syntax-Electronic) that was designed to minimise such demands by using a format where the child sees a specific animation and has to judge whether it matches a spoken sentence. Because this is in effect a two-choice test, it is necessary to give at least eight items per structure to distinguish chance performance from understanding. Using this approach we found that TD children as young as 3;06 years showed understanding of some complex constructions that they had found difficult when tested using the more traditional multiple choice picture-pointing approach (see Frizelle et al., 2018a). Of course, no method is completely free of task demands or item-specific influences on performance, but our experience of the TECS-E with young children raised the possibility that traditional approaches to assessing comprehension may underestimate understanding in children with DS.
Receptive language and cognition in DS Although it is tempting to consider cognitive ability as a core factor in explaining receptive language differences between those with DS and other groups, the literature is not consistent in this regard, particularly in relation to vocabulary. Several studies suggest that the receptive vocabulary of those with DS is in keeping with that of cognitively matched children with typical development, (Chapman et al., 1991;Laws & Bishop, 2003;Miller, 1995) while other studies suggest a lower performance from those with DS (Caselli et al., 2008;Hick et al., 2005;Price et al., 2007). The literature regarding syntactic comprehension appears to be more homogenous with the majority of studies showing that those with DS have a lower than expected understanding of syntax relative to their non-verbal cognitive skills (Abbeduto et al., 2003;Chapman et al., 1991;Joffe & Varlokosta, 2009;Laws & Bishop, 2003;Price et al., 2007;Rosin et al., 1988). However, it is important to note that most of these studies have used the same assessment measures, with a significant focus on morphology and simple syntax and few embedded sentences. Some studies have compared those with DS to mentalage-matched TD controls, while others have matched cognitive ability with other cognitively impaired groups such as those with Williams syndrome, Fragile X syndrome and those with specific language impairment. The aim of these comparisons is to see whether there is a distinctive profile specific to those with DS relative to other groups who have a language and or cognitive impairment。

此外，我们发现儿童在语言理解测试中的表现会受到所采用的评估方法的具体要求的严重影响（Frizelle et al., 2017）。TACL-R 和 TROG-2 采用的是传统的多选句子图画匹配格式，目标是从一组图画中选择与听到的句子相匹配的图画。其他图画是干扰项，代表句子的替代解释，儿童需要排除这些干扰项才能正确回答。这些竞争性解释的呈现方式使得只有那些对句法结构有深刻理解的儿童才能选择正确的项目。然而，这种格式很可能会导致儿童因其他原因而失败，而不仅仅是缺乏语言知识。特别是，这种格式可能使注意力不集中和冲动的儿童（如 DS 儿童）处于不利地位，以及那些不理解需要仔细查看选项以区分相似项目的儿童。我们开发了一种新测试（TECS-E：复杂句法电子测试），旨在通过使用一种格式来最小化这类要求，该格式中儿童看到特定的动画并判断其是否与听到的句子相匹配。由于这实际上是一个二选一的测试，因此每个结构至少需要八个项目才能将随机表现与理解区分开来。使用这种方法，我们发现即使是 3;06 岁的典型发展（TD）儿童也能够理解他们在更传统的多选图画指认测试中难以理解的一些复杂结构（见 Frizelle et al., 2018a）。当然，没有任何方法完全不受任务要求或具体项目对表现的影响，但我们在年幼儿童中使用 TECS-E 的经验表明，传统的方法可能低估了 DS 儿童的理解能力。

DS 中的接受性语言和认知

尽管很容易将认知能力视为解释 DS 患者与其他群体在接受性语言差异方面的核心因素，但文献在这方面并不一致，特别是在词汇方面。一些研究表明，DS 患者的接受性词汇与认知配对的正常发展儿童相当（Chapman et al., 1991; Laws & Bishop, 2003; Miller, 1995），而其他研究则表明 DS 组的表现较低（Caselli et al., 2008; Hick et al., 2005; Price et al., 2007）。关于句法理解的文献似乎更为一致，大多数研究表明，DS 患者的句法理解能力低于其非言语认知技能的预期水平（Abbeduto et al., 2003; Chapman et al., 1991; Joffe & Varlokosta, 2009; Laws & Bishop, 2003; Price et al., 2007; Rosin et al., 1988）。然而，需要注意的是，大多数这些研究使用了相同的评估方法，主要关注形态学和简单句法，很少涉及嵌入句子。一些研究将 DS 组与心理年龄匹配的典型发展对照组进行了比较，而另一些研究则将其认知能力与其他认知障碍群体（如威廉姆斯综合征、脆性 X 综合征和特定语言障碍）进行了匹配。这些比较的目的是看看 DS 组相对于其他具有语言或认知障碍的群体是否有独特的特点。

# Amendments from Version 1 Part-3

While previous reports appear mixed and are somewhat dependant on the comparison group under scrutiny, existing literature suggests that children with DS perform at a similar level to those with Williams syndrome and specific language impairment. A summary of the findings comparing those with DS with other groups, on their understanding of syntax is shown in Table 1.

尽管先前的报告结果似乎不一，并且在一定程度上依赖于所研究的对照组，但现有的文献表明，患有唐氏综合征（DS）的儿童在语言理解方面的表现与威廉姆斯综合征和特定语言障碍的儿童相似。表1总结了比较DS患者与其他群体在句法理解方面的发现。

# Memory characteristics of children with DS

Individuals with DS show particular difficulties with verbal shortterm or working memory tasks (Jarrold & Baddeley, 2010;Jarrold et al., 2002;Laws, 2002) even when compared to other groups with cognitive delay, who do not have DS (Bower & Hayes, 1994;Chapman, 2006;Laws, 2004). In contrast, their visual memory skills are often superior to, or at least in keeping with these groups, (Bower & Hayes, 1994;Chapman, 2006;Rowe et al., 2006) suggesting that their memory deficits are specific to language. 1996).
Laws (1998); Laws (2004) reported a strong correlation between verbal short-term memory and a reduced mean length of utterance, as well as language comprehension difficulties. A strong relationship between memory and syntax has also emerged. Chapman et al. (2002) took a number of measures, at four time intervals over a 6-year period, from 31 individuals with DS between the ages of 5 and 20 years. They reported that along with chronological age, both verbal and visual working memory, were significant predictors of syntactic comprehension ability. In addition, Chapman & Hesketh (2001) reported these factors to be key predictors of expressive syntax at the onset of their study. The connection between memory ability and syntactic difficulties in those with DS is also evident in work by Michael et al. (2012). Michael and colleagues took a number of memory measures from individuals with DS, and a TD group matched on vocabulary, including digit span, word span, a spatial memory task and a sentence repetition task. Both groups performed similarly on all measures, with the exception of the sentence repetition task. They suggested that when compared to digit and word span, the syntactic processing load of a sentence was particularly difficult for the individuals with DS to parse and recall.
Because the current study focuses particularly on complex sentences, and these constructions require the parsing of different clauses over a more lengthy time span (Martin & McElree, 2009;Marton et al., 2006), we might predict that short term and working memory would be particularly relevant to the ability of someone with DS to understand them. However, to our knowledge, this has never been investigated in relation to this population.

唐氏综合症儿童的记忆特征

唐氏综合症（DS）患者在言语短期记忆或工作记忆任务中表现出特定的困难（Jarrold & Baddeley, 2010; Jarrold et al., 2002; Laws, 2002），即使与其他认知发育迟缓但不具有DS的群体相比也是如此（Bower & Hayes, 1994; Chapman, 2006; Laws, 2004）。相比之下，他们的视觉记忆能力往往优于或至少与这些群体相当（Bower & Hayes, 1994; Chapman, 2006; Rowe et al., 2006），这表明他们的记忆缺陷是特定于语言的。

Laws（1998, 2004）报告了言语短期记忆与较低的话语平均长度以及语言理解困难之间的强烈相关性。记忆与句法之间也显示出强烈的关联。Chapman等人（2002）对31名5至20岁的DS个体进行了为期6年的四次测量，发现除了年龄之外，言语和视觉工作记忆也是句法理解能力的重要预测因素。此外，Chapman和Hesketh（2001）在其研究开始时也报告了这些因素是表达句法的关键预测因子。Michael等人（2012）的研究也显示了DS患者的记忆能力和句法困难之间的联系。Michael及其同事对DS个体以及词汇量匹配的典型发育群体进行了多项记忆测量，包括数字广度、词汇广度、空间记忆任务和句子重复任务。两组在所有任务上的表现相似，除了句子重复任务。他们认为，与数字和词汇广度相比，句子的句法处理负荷对于DS个体来说特别难以解析和回忆。

由于本研究特别关注复杂句子的理解，而这些结构需要在更长的时间跨度内解析不同的从句（Martin & McElree, 2009; Marton et al., 2006），我们可以预期短期记忆和工作记忆对于DS个体理解这些句子尤为重要。然而，据我们所知，这一点从未在该人群中进行过研究。

# Current study

In sum, given the limited scope of previous research on comprehension, in terms of both methods and linguistic structures, we are uninformed about how individuals with DS process and understand specific complex structures as well as how cognitive ability, memory and hearing level impact the ability of those with DS to deal with these sentence types.
Our first aim was to investigate how well individuals with DS can understand complex structures such as relative clauses, complement clauses and adverbial clauses. Based on findings that individuals with DS produced relative and complement clauses in their narrative samples (Thordardottir et al., 2002), we hypothesised that many of those with DS would be able to understand these constructions, although, on the basis of prior literature, we anticipated considerable performance variation. We compared strengths or weaknesses seen in those with DS to two other groups: (a) those with intellectual disability but of unknown aetiology (matched to those with DS on non-verbal mental age), and (b) a group of TD younger children at the same non-verbal mental age. This allowed us to identify whether those with DS have a characteristic syntactic profile relative to the other two groups. Based on previous findings (such as those reported by Abbeduto et al., 2003;Chapman, 2006;Laws & Bishop, 2004) we hypothesised that those with DS would perform similarly to those with an intellectual disability of unknown origin but more poorly than the TD group matched on nonverbal ability. Based on data from TECS-E with TD children aged from 3;06 to 5 years (see Frizelle et al., 2018a) we anticipated an order of difficulty within each family of constructions (relative, complement and adverbial). Within the five types of relative clause we expected children to have the least difficulty with intransitive subject relatives, with other relative clause types being of a similar level of difficulty. Within adverbial clauses we expected causal adverbials to be the least demanding, followed by those that are temporal, with conditional adverbials causing the greatest difficulty. Finally, we anticipated that sentences using the verb pretend would be the least difficult complement clause items and that those using the cognitive state verb think would be the most difficult to understand. We based this expectation on previous (unpublished) data collected from young typically children between 3;06 and 4;11 years.
We also examined how children performed on TECS-E relative to a standardized test of grammar using the multiple-choice format. In the standardized measure (TROG-2; Bishop, 2003) children must show an understanding of the syntactically simple constructions before they progress on to those that are more complex. Therefore, by applying the discontinue rule, if a given number of items are failed, children will not be tested on complex sentences. Here, in order to compare test administrations between TECS-E and TROG-2, we always administered block S (relative clauses) from TROG-2 at the end of the test, even if the stopping criterion was reached. This block of four items uses relative clauses attached to a main clause object, two of which are similar in construction to those used in the TECS-E (albeit with some lexical differences-a noun rather that a pronoun in the head noun position: The girl chases the dog that is jumping) and two of which incorporate prepositional phrases (The cup that is on the box is red).
Finally we considered how far comprehension difficulties in those with DS were associated with cognitive ability, verbal short-term or working memory abilities and hearing thresholds, and whether these associations differed according to the assessment format used. We predicted correlations of comprehension scores with all three variables, though performance on particular clause types would differ, as discussed above. Given the additional cognitive load involved in a multiple-choice format, we hypothesised that children’s performance on this task would correlate more highly than TECS-E with overall cognitive and memory abilities.
Our pre-registered hypotheses https://osf.io/5ntvc/ were as follows:

  1. Individuals with DS will be able to understand a range of the complex sentences tested, although we expect considerable individual variation.
  2. Those with DS will perform more poorly overall than TD controls but at a similar level to those with cognitive impairment of unknown origin.
  3. Children will have greater difficulty understanding comparable constructions on the multiple-choice test than on the animation task.
  4. Cognitive ability, verbal memory, working memory and hearing level will predict performance in the DS group.
  5. Cognitive, verbal and working memory abilities will account for more variance on the multiple-choice than on the animation task.

综上所述，鉴于以往关于理解能力的研究在方法和语言结构方面的局限性，我们对唐氏综合症（DS）患者如何处理和理解特定复杂结构以及认知能力、记忆和听觉水平如何影响他们处理这些句子类型的能力知之甚少。我们的第一个目标是研究DS患者理解复杂的句子结构（如关系从句、补语从句和副词从句）的能力如何。基于Thordardottir等人（2002）的发现，即DS患者在其叙述样本中能够产生关系从句和补语从句，我们假设许多DS患者将能够理解这些结构，尽管根据前期文献，我们预计其表现会有相当大的差异。我们将DS患者的优劣势与另外两组进行了比较：(a) 有智力障碍但病因不明的个体（与DS患者在非语言心智年龄上匹配），(b) 一组非言语心智年龄相同的典型发育儿童。这使我们能够识别DS患者相对于其他两组是否具有特征性的句法概况。基于先前的研究结果（如Abbeduto等人，2003；Chapman, 2006；Laws & Bishop, 2004），我们假设DS患者在与未查明原因的智障群体的表现相似，但比非言语能力匹配的典型发育群体表现更差。基于TECS-E对3岁6个月到5岁之间的典型发育儿童的数据（参见Frizelle等人，2018a），我们预期每种构建类型的难度顺序（关系从句、补语从句和副词从句）。在五种类型的关系从句中，我们期望儿童对不及物主语关系从句的掌握最为容易，而其他类型关系从句的难度相似。在副词从句里，我们期待因果副词从句最容易理解，其次是时间副词从句，条件副词从句最难理解。最后，我们预期使用动词“假装”的句子是补语从句中难度最低的项，而使用认知状态动词“认为”的句子是最难理解的。这一预期基于先前从3岁6个月到4岁11个月之间的典型发育儿童收集的（未发表）数据。
我们还考察了儿童在TECS-E上的表现与采用多选题格式的标准语法测试的比较。在标准测量中（TROG-2；Bishop, 2003），儿童必须先展示对语法简单结构的理解才能进展到更复杂的句子。因此，依据停考规则，如果失败了一定数量的题目，孩子们就不会被测试复杂数目的句子了。为了比较TECS-E和TROG-2的测试管理，即使达到了停止标准，我们始终在考试结束时进行TROG-2中的S块（关系从句）。这四个项目中使用的是一种带有主句宾语的关系从句，其中两个构造与TECS-E中使用的相似（尽管有一些词汇上的不同——头名词位置是一个名词而不是代词：“女孩追逐着跳跃的狗”），另外两个包含介词短语（“杯子在盒子上是红色的”）。
最后，我们探讨了DS患者在理解困难方面与认知能力、言语短期记忆或工作记忆能力和听力阈值之间的关联程度，以及根据所使用的评估格式这些关联是否存在差异。我们预测理解分数与这三个变量之间存在相关性，但如前所述，对于特定类型的从句，表现会有所不同。考虑到多选题形式需要额外的认知负荷，我们假设孩子们在这种任务上的表现将与总体认知和记忆能力有更高的相关性。
我们在OSF.io (https://osf.io/5ntvc/) 上预先注册的假设如下：

  1. DS患者将能够理解一系列被测试的复杂句子，但我们预计会有很大的个体差异。
  2. DS患者整体表现会比典型发育对照组差，但与原因不明的认知障碍组的表现相同。
  3. 儿童在多选题测试中理解同类结构的难度将大于动画任务。
  4. 认知能力、言语记忆、工作记忆和听力水平将预测DS组的表现。
  5. 在多选题任务中，认知能力、言语记忆和工作记忆能力对评分变异的解释将比在动画任务中更大。

# Power analysis

For our main hypothesis, the best estimate of effect size came from prior studies that compared those with Down syndrome to TD controls on composite measures of syntactic comprehension. We calculated the average effect size for the difference between those with Down syndrome and TD controls matched on nonverbal mental age. We made the assumption that the effect size for the difference between those with cognitive impairment of unknown origin and those with typical development is similar in magnitude to the previous average effect. Cohen’s d values were calculated for each piece of metadata and then converted to f 2 for use in the sample size calculation. The conversion was done for two groups using the formula f 2 = d 2 /2k, where k is the number of groups and d is Cohen’s d. We use used f 2 as our measure of effect size as this corresponded to our method of analysis, linear multiple regression.
The median effect size from prior literature was 0.19. This was entered into G*power software (F test, linear multiple regression: Fixed model, R 2 increase (a priori; see Faul et al., 2007).
The sample size required with two tested predictors (intellectual level and Down syndrome status) at 90% power and alpha = 0.05 was 70, giving an estimate of 23 participants per group.
We had anticipated that our subsequent analyses would incorporate the additional predictors of memory and hearing level, giving a total of five predictors. With five predictors we estimated a total sample of 93 (at 90% power and alpha = 0.05). However, we also expected to be able to drop one predictor, depending on the results of our first analysis. If there was no group effect, the group term could be dropped, and if the Down syndrome group differed from the other two groups, then the group comparison could be coded in one variable. The effect number of predictors would therefore be four, with a required total sample size of 86. Accordingly we aimed for a sample of 30 participants per group.

功效分析

对于我们的主要假设，效应量的最佳估计来自先前的研究，这些研究比较了唐氏综合症患者与典型发育对照组在句法理解综合测量上的差异。我们计算了匹配非言语心理年龄的唐氏综合症患者与典型发育对照组之间差异的平均效应量。我们假设，未知原因认知障碍组与典型发育组之间差异的效应量与之前的平均效应量在数量级上是相似的。对于每一份元数据，我们计算了Cohen’s d值，然后将其转换为f²用于样本量计算。使用公式f² = d² / 2k（其中k是组数，d是Cohen’s d）将Cohen’s d值转换为f²。我们使用f²作为效应量的度量，因为这与我们的分析方法（线性多重回归）相对应。

先前文献中的中位效应量为0.19。我们将此值输入G*Power软件进行F检验（线性多重回归：固定模型，R²增量（先验；参见Faul等, 2007))。

在两个测试变量（智力水平和唐氏综合症状态）的情况下，达到90%的功效和α = 0.05所需的样本量为70，相当于每组约23名参与者。

我们预期后续分析会加入记忆和听力水平这两个额外预测变量，总共五个预测变量。在五个预测变量的情况下，我们估计总样本量为93（在90%功效和α = 0.05时）。然而，我们也预计根据第一次分析的结果可以删除一个预测变量。如果组效应不显著，可以删除组别这一变量；如果唐氏综合症组与其他两组不同，则可以在一个变量中编码组别对比。因此，实际的预测变量数目可能会减少到四个，所需总样本量为86。因此，我们旨在每组招募30名参与者。

# Participants

A total of 47 participants with DS were recruited to the study.
The study was conducted between November 2017 and May 2018, in the Republic of Ireland, where the prevalence of DS is one in every 546 live births (Johnson et al., 1996) et al., 2013) were included and children were required to be capable of producing 3-word utterances at a minimum. The sample size was calculated using a power analysis from a hierarchical linear regression analysis, with an expected effect size of 0.19 (see below for justification).
For the comparison groups, 32 children with cognitive impairment of unknown aetiology (CI) and 33 TD children were also recruited into the study. Those with typical development were recruited from mainstream schools and preschools, and those with CI were recruited from both special and mainstream schools. Both groups were matched on cognitive ability to those with DS, using the Leiter-3 (Roid et al., 2013) (F (2, 95) = 2.077, p < 0.131). TD children were included on the basis that they had never been referred for speech and language therapy, had typical language abilities (based on teacher and parental reports), and had no known neurological or hearing difficulties. All groups spoke English as their first language and the language of the home, and both control groups underwent hearingscreening tests across the same frequency range as those with DS. The descriptives for each group are given in Table 2.

参与者

本研究共招募了47名唐氏综合症 (DS) 患者。研究于2017年11月至2018年5月在爱尔兰共和国进行，该国唐氏综合症的发病率是每546个活产婴儿中有1例（Johnson et al., 1996）。纳入研究的儿童需要至少能够说出三词短语。样本量是通过层次线性回归分析的效能分析计算得出的，预期效应量为0.19（见下文的合理性）。

对于对照组，研究还招募了32名具有未知病因的认知障碍（CI）的儿童和33名典型发育（TD）儿童。典型发育的儿童从普通学校和幼儿园中招募，而认知障碍的儿童则从特殊学校和普通学校中招募。两组对照组在认知能力上与DS组进行了匹配，使用了Leiter-3（Roid et al., 2013），并通过方差分析表明两组在认知能力上的差异不显著（F (2, 95) = 2.077, p < 0.131）。典型发育的儿童被纳入的标准是：他们从未被转介接受言语和语言治疗，具有典型的语言能力（基于教师和家长报告），且没有已知的神经或听力问题。所有组别都将英语作为第一语言和家庭语言，并且两个对照组都接受了与DS组相同的频率范围内的听力筛查测试。各组的描述性统计见表2。

# Ethics

The Cork Teaching Hospitals Ethics Committee granted ethical approval for the study (ECM 4-07/10/14). Informed written consent was obtained from the parents/guardians of all participants. Each participant also completed an assent form.

伦理委员会批准了本研究（ECM 4-07/10/14）。所有参与者的父母或监护人均已签署书面知情同意书。每位参与者还填写了一份同意表。

# Procedure

Assessments were administered in a quiet room at the preschool, school or special school that each participant attended. The assessments were completed in three sessions and included the following:
Leiter-3. This is a non-verbal test of cognitive ability involving four core subtests: figure ground, form completion, classification and sequential order. Figure ground is a visual interference task, which involves the identification of images embedded within a

评估在每个参与者所就读的幼儿园、学校或特殊学校的安静房间内进行。评估分为三个会话完成，内容包括以下几项：

Leiter-3。这是一个非语言认知能力测试，包含四个核心子测试：图形背景、形状补全、分类和序列顺序。图形背景是一项视觉干扰任务，涉及从复杂的背景中识别嵌入的图像。

# Subject intransitive

He found the girl that was hiding.

他发现了那个正在躲藏的女孩。

# Subject transitive

He pushed the girl that scored the goal.

他推了那个进球的女孩。

# Object

The boy picked up the cup that she broke.

男孩捡起了她打破的杯子。

# Oblique

The man opened the gate she jumped over.
Indirect object She kissed the boy she poured the juice for.

斜格（Oblique）

那个人打开了她跳过去的门。
间接宾语：她吻了她为他倒果汁的那个男孩。

# Complement clause

补语从句章节内容如下：

她认为男孩的头发是干的
他知道女孩打破了椅子

这名男子希望他在公交车上。

在看电视之前，男孩踢了足球。
